Chapter 3101: Chapter 3099: The Tools Man Who Came to the Gate
 

Gem Domain.

Once, this era was the most flourishing of all the realms in the myriad practitioners in the universe. The Gem Domain was abundant in spirit stones, energy gemstones, rune stones, and other natural treasures... On every planet within the Gem Domain, as long as people were willing to work hard at excavation, the rewards were bound to not disappoint.

And the spirit stones and gemstones in the Gem Domain seemed inexhaustible and never-ending. No matter how they were mined, it was impossible to deplete them, and their quality was extremely high.

In those years, every planet in the Gem Domain seemed to twinkle with the light of gemstones, which is why it was called the ‘Gem Domain’.

But in the middle period of the ancient era, the spiritual qi in the Gem Domain suddenly ran out, without any warning — some suspected that the Gem Domain had been tampered with by some big shot.

After the depletion of spiritual qi, the spirit stones, gemstones, and precious jades that were originally everywhere were quickly mined out... the entire Gem Domain lost its past luster and turned into wasteland.

The twinkling planets, drained and hollowed out, lost their shine.

Now, it has become one of the most desolate worlds in the myriad realms.

But now, due to the emergence of the ‘Heavenly Dao Immortal Tomb’, the desolate Gem Domain has once again become bustling.

In these three days, Immortals and Top Tribulation Immortals from the myriad realms have crossed space and planes to descend upon the Gem Domain, searching here for information on the Immortal Tombs of the Second and Third Heavenly Dao.

Besides Immortals and Top Tribulation Immortals, many cultivators have also come after hearing the news, thinking whether they could gain some opportunity during this grand event.

While the big shots are feasting on meat, with a bit of luck, they might leave some soup, which they don’t care for, but for the majority of cultivators, that soup might be a chance to go against the heaven.

The entire Gem Domain seems to have regained its past glory.

The trajectories of cultivators flying can be seen from time to time on each planet...

There are also immense Immortal Ships and space battleships shuttling through the space of the Gem Domain...

Some cultivators are calling friends and forming teams to act...

There are also sect big shots, who simply bring their disciples over to broaden their horizons...

“Master, where shall we go next?” In the vacuum, a Fairy Soft Feather wrapped in a sheet softly asked.

“I will set up a stall over at that so-called ‘Second Heavenly Dao Immortal Tomb’, and you start work at the location of the ‘Third Heavenly Dao grand tomb’... Such a big festival is a good opportunity for us to make a fortune,” the man also wrapped in a sheet opposite Fairy Soft Feather said in a deep voice.

It was the Almighty Merchant and his disciple Almighty Seller.

“This time, our main products are ‘Immortal Aura Exploration Pointer’, ‘Mask to Shield Immortal Poison Barrier’, and also the ‘small-black-room-breaking disposable flying sword’ that we got from Fellow Daoist White,” the Almighty Merchant and his disciple introduced.

The master and disciple pair is very clear that this ‘Tomb of the Second and Third Heavenly Dao’ is just a ruse.

After all, their heritage is related to the Sixth Heavenly Dao Virtuous Daoist, and they are very aware of the true structure of the ‘Immortal Tomb’.

However, this does not hinder the master and disciple from doing business.

“Prosperous business, Master,” the Almighty Seller nodded.

“Prosperous business... Also, watch out for Tyrannical Song, if you see Tyrannical Song coming, just hide far away,” the Almighty Merchant reminded.

His intuition told him that this ‘event’ might have something to do with Tyrannical Song. In time, Tyrannical Song might become a source of trouble; it’s certainly best to stay far away.

“Master, you are biased against Tyrannical Song,” the Almighty Seller waved her hand and said, “On the contrary, I feel that Mister Tyrannical Song is a very nice VIP quality customer.”

“Bullshit, that guy has no money,” the Almighty Merchant retorted.

“But Mr. White has money,” the Almighty Seller giggled, crossing through space and heading towards the location of the Third Heavenly Dao Immortal Tomb.

...

...

On the other side.

The Immortals from the myriad practitioners in the universe each used their Magical Techniques, exploring separately in the two Immortal Tombs.

To attract these Immortals, Daozi, Father Goudan, and Senior Three-Eyes really invested a lot while creating the ‘Immortal Tombs’.

In the two Immortal Tombs, there is Immortal Spirit Qi everywhere.

In every layer, there are flowing springs and mysterious lights flickering, exuding a faint aura of immortality.

To allow Immortals to stay in the grand tomb for as long as possible, Daozi worked overtime to create a batch of magical treasures related to ‘Heaven’s Will,’ which he placed in every corner of the tomb.

He aimed to ensure that these Immortals would gain something and not leave empty-handed.

The three-eyed young senior contributed several ‘Strong Corpse Bones,’ placing them in the tomb, some to create ‘Fake Tombs,’ others arranged as if they were ‘casualties.’

Father Goudan set up many Killing Formations within the tomb... Exploring the Tomb of Immortality is not a leisurely affair; one must risk their life upon entering.

To do it, do it best, make it most realistic.

Thus, the two grand tombs were filled with traps and Killing Formations that could trap Immortals, or even heavily injure or suppress them.

In the Third Heavenly Dao Tomb.

“Pfft...” An Immortal spat out a mouthful of blood, fleeing from a spirit qi-entwined immortal gate; his blood spilled as he escaped.

A single drop of his blood, potent enough to obliterate cities, was absorbed directly by the tomb when it fell, turning into a power that fueled the operation of the tomb.

Beside him, a wooden sword burned and turned into ashes.

“This is not the gateway to the main tomb; it’s likely left by a powerful tomb explorer who came before us. The destination of this immortal gate is a Chaotic Dead Land, filled with endless and ever-shifting Killing Formations. Had I not just obtained a ‘Return City Flying Sword,’ I might have been trapped to death within the immortal gate,” the Immortal whispered softly.

Similar scenes occurred frequently in various places within the two Heavenly Dao Tombs.

And while this wounded Immortal silently took his elixirs and tended to his injuries, within the shadows, a pair of eyes quietly locked onto him.

An illusory sun, utilizing special means, was hidden within the shadows.

Recently, the ‘Void Sun Guardians’ and ‘Stellar Doomsday Demon Skulls,’ brought along by the ‘Cultivator Chat System New Year Event,’ quietly arrived upon learning of the ‘Second and Third Heavenly Dao Tombs.’

Their targets were not only the Immortal Tombs but also these tomb explorers, Immortals, and top Tribulation Immortals.

Those who were seriously injured during their exploration of the Immortal Tomb were their prey.

——They planned to secretly slay a few top-notch Tribulation Immortals and Immortals to propagate their species.

The traps and Killing Formations of the Immortal Tomb had created excellent opportunities for them.

...

...

The Stellar Doomsday Demon Skulls and Void Sun Guardians covertly observed the wounded Immortals and Tribulation Immortals.

Behind them, Daozi Big Shot held Scholarly Scripture with a smile on his face, watching these Void Suns that snuck in from the shadows.

“Should we deal with them?” Father Goudan asked lazily.

These annoying rats, how dare they actually come knocking of their own accord?

“No rush,” Daozi Big Shot said with a slight smile. “I was previously worried about how to make a shocking entrance for Tyrannical Song. These little rats are perfect props. I will make good use of them.”

Today was the day he would step down from his position in the Heavenly Dao.

Before stepping down, he would add to Tyrannical Song’s prestige one last time.

This was his final moment on the position of Heavenly Dao, cheering for Tyrannical Song.

“Do we need to coordinate any guidance?” the three-eyed young senior asked, playing with a pair of eyeballs.

“Hmm... It would be best to find a way to gather these injured Immortals together. This way, the Void Sun Guardians and Stellar Doomsday Demon Skulls, which are targeting them from the shadows, will also converge. Best to activate some Killing Formations that suppress the power of the Immortals, so these wounded ones can’t exert their full strength. Otherwise, if they go berserk, it won’t be good if they steal Song Shuhang’s thunder,” Daozi Big Shot contemplated.

“Leave it to me,” Father Goudan jumped up and called out, “Dada Egg, come with me. I need the cooperation of your Time powers.”

Heavenly Emperor’s child: “...”

“Senior, thank you for your hard work. Also, please pay attention to the power of the Killing Formation. Don’t let the Immortals and Top-Tier Tribulation Immortals actually get wiped out by the Void Sun Guardians, needlessly increasing the strength of the Void Sun,” Daozi reminded.

“Leave that to me. I’ll secretly protect these injured Tribulation Immortals and Immortals,” said the projection of Senior White Two as it crossed through space, returning to its origin.

Song Shuhang and Senior White were already on their way to the ‘Gem Domain,’ and after Senior White Two took a look around, he returned to work behind the scenes.

“Thank you, Lord White,” Daozi said with a nod.

The final script unfolds.

...

...

More than ten minutes later.

Inside the space of the Third Heavenly Dao’s Tomb.

Those severely injured Immortals and Top-Tier Tribulation Immortals, having slightly recovered after taking elixirs, got up and continued delving deeper into the tomb’s space.

In the grand tomb, every nook and cranny could hide a deadly trap, but there might also be treasures greatly beneficial to Immortals.

For instance, fragments of magical treasures personally refined by the Heavenly Dao, stained with ‘Weak Immortal Information’ that Immortals could access, giving them a tiny glimpse into the realm of immortality.

Some even found refining waste materials maintained by the power of the Heavenly Dao—foundations for primordial treasures. If one could incorporate them into their life-bound magical treasure, the benefits would be boundless.

Moreover, the formations and Killing Formations spread throughout the tomb, once deciphered, could bring immense benefits.

Therefore, as long as it didn’t affect their core essence, even if they were injured, the crowd wouldn’t waste time. They would get up and explore the tomb as much as they could within the limited time.

Unknowingly...

These wounded Immortals and Tribulation Immortals were led into a ‘Paradise.’

A Paradise World within the Heavenly Dao Tomb.

Here, birds sang and flowers fragranced, with the gentle strains of a zither echoing in the void.

In the air, there were chains of order and principles from the Great Way of immortality.

The Immortals only felt their inner strength being repressed, unable to wield their powers freely, their bodies becoming heavy, and the healing of their wounds slowed down.

“Is this... the core of the Heavenly Dao Tomb?” The Immortals thought to themselves.

But before they could react, several figures slowly became visible around them.

They were ten Void Sun Guardians plus the Stellar Doomsday Demon Skulls.

The new arrivals bore ill intent.

“It’s just about time,” murmured Senior White Two softly.

With a light tap of his finger, he activated a function.

The entire Paradise World soared.

An invisible sound wave spread throughout the entire Third Heavenly Dao Tomb.

All the Immortals in the tomb sensed something—there was a connection to this ‘Paradise World.’

[Is that the core of the Heavenly Dao Tomb? Did someone enter the core and trigger the alarm?]

Without any hesitation, everyone abandoned their current explorations and headed towards the ‘Paradise’ area.

Even those Immortals deep in the ‘Second Heavenly Dao Tomb’ projected their consciousness upon receiving messages from their comrades. They connected to the large tomb opposite to them and tried to connect to Paradise, keen to witness the developments.

...

...

In the Third Heavenly Dao Tomb, the Immortals and Top-Tier Tribulation Immortals desperately rushed towards the ‘Paradise World.’

But the various Killing Formations, protective barriers, and formations along the way hampered their speed.

They had to race against time while keeping in constant communication with the Paradise World, observing its developments.

In their conscious focus, the image of what was happening in the Paradise Space was reflected.

“Eh? Void Sun Guardians?”

“And Stellar Doomsday beings.”

“We’ve struck gold!”

The Immortal big shots were stirred—knowing that ‘Mister Tyrannical Song’s’ joint New Year’s event with the Heavenly Dao showed no signs of ending and seemed to persist indefinitely.

If they could capture a few Void Sun Guardians and Stellar Doomsday Demon Skulls, they could exchange them through Song Shuhang’s ‘Cultivator Chat System’ for grand rewards. These gifts, purified and decoded by the Heavenly Dao for Immortals’ absorption, included ‘Weak Immortality Information, Law Comprehension,’ and more.

“There are others! There are some fellow friends within the Paradise Space.”

“Lucky fellows, not only did they stumble into Paradise Space, but they’ve also encountered ready-made Void Suns and Doomsday entities.”

“Wait... the condition of these fellow friends seems off.”

“They are wounded?”

“And it seems they’re repressed by the rules of Paradise Space. Might they be the first group that barged in and suffered restrictions from the Killing Formation as punishment?”

“Things look unfavorable for them... Moreover, the number of Constant Star Guardians and Void Sun Guardians, there are ten in total.”

Furthermore, one of the Void Sun Guardians was bigger than all the other Void Suns combined.

This Void Sun Guardian exerted an oppressive heaviness.

“This oppressiveness has a faint whiff of a Confucian Sage, likely an existence just below that of a Confucian Sage,” they surmised.

“In that case, it is at least on par with our demonic sect’s Demon Emperor Hezhi?”

An existence just below that of a Sage would be one who could handle ten others at their level.

...

...

Inside Paradise World.

Immortal Yue Ruhuo sighed and fixed his gaze on the largest Void Sun.

This Void Sun put pressure on him that was nearly comparable to Tyrannical Song’s steel manifestation from before...

Yue Ruhuo was one of the injured Immortals this time.

Once the Void Sun Guardians and the Stellar Doomsday Skulls appeared, they attacked without any useless chatter.

They too had discerned the existence of their ‘Paradise World’ being sensed by all the Immortals.

Time was of the essence for them.

They needed to take down these several severely wounded Immortals and Tribulation Immortals before others arrived.

Afterward, they intended to unveil the secrets within this ‘Paradise Space’ and then swiftly withdraw.

So, the moment they made their move, it was with fatally tempting killer moves.

From the massive Void Sun, surging killing intent spilled forth like an endless sea, pressing against Yue Ruhuo and the other Immortals.

The rest of the Void Suns swelled, transformed into actual colossal suns, and bore down to suppress them directly.

Chapter 3102: Chapter 3100: Pretending to be Tyrannical Song until He Has No Room Left to Pretend
 

“Burning Star!”

“Star Burst Hell!”

“Residual Fire Apocalypse!”

At this moment, these were all techniques belonging to the ‘Stellar Doomsday Demon Skull,’ each of which possessed a combat power close to or equivalent to that of an Immortal. Their attacks were all inclined towards methods of destroying stars.

Coupled with a small amount of ‘Stellar Destruction Virus,’ once these moves were fully unleashed, they could obliterate medium-sized stars.

The attack methods of the ‘Void Sun Guardians,’ on the other hand, were much simpler, shedding countless cutting light rays from their bodies... These rays carried the power of principles and were unstoppable by anything.

Especially the largest ‘Void Sun Guardian,’ which exploded with thick pillars of light... Simultaneously, a substance similar to the ‘Stellar Destruction Virus’ was released from its body, enhancing the attack power of both the Stellar Doomsday Demon Skull and the Void Sun Guardians.

If not for the suppression of the Paradise Space’s laws of the Heavenly Dao, ten Suns acting together could directly obliterate the planets in the Gem Domain!

Including Scholar Yue Ruhuo, the six injured Immortals all had unsightly expressions—faced with attacks of this caliber, they thought they might need to use their ultimate, life-saving techniques to block them.

And the life-saving techniques of Immortals... were very expensive!

Replenishing them would require a huge consumption of resources or immense efforts to fill the gap.

...

...

Outside the Third Heavenly Dao’s Tomb.

When ten ‘Void Sun Guardians’ and ‘Stellar Doomsday Demon Skulls’ exerted their power at the same time, the night sky above the planet in the Gem Domain projected the image of ten scorching suns.

A single sun projection could certainly not compare with an actual star, but ten suns in the sky brought terrifying heat, forcibly driving away the night of the Gem Domain Planet and turning night into day.

The heat of ten suns in a short period of time began to wring out the moisture of the planet.

Within a few moments, the planet’s surface started making a disturbing ‘sizzle~’ sound... That was the sound of the surface water being rapidly evaporated, the ground beginning to crack and split.

The ice layers of the planet, which originally had a lower temperature, started to melt at high speed.

The ‘Almighty Merchant,’ who was quietly trading at the entrance to the ‘Third Heavenly Dao’s grand tomb,’ silently raised her head, looking at the ten suns’ phenomena in the sky.

She smelled a major business opportunity.

The more chaotic it was, the better it suited her business.

“Moreover, even such Heaven and Earth Phenomena have appeared... This is sparing no effort. Those six injured Immortals, the top Tribulation Immortals, probably can’t handle it,” the Almighty Merchant said as she began to search through her inventory for special elixirs tailored for ‘sunlight-type injuries.’

Perhaps they might come in handy later.

...

...

Within the Paradise Space.

Terrifying energy was surging, with the power of Sunrise Flames everywhere.

Even the Paradise grassland protected by a special Killing Formation turned to ashes under the attack of ten suns.

In the center of the ten suns’ assault.

The six injured Immortals had already gathered together, cooperating with one another.

They immediately used their ultimate techniques.

Scholar Yue Ruhuo summoned a sword formation capable of both offense and defense. At the same time, he began to play his zither, enhancing the condition of the other bamboo-like Immortals and suppressing their injuries.

To his left, a garment as thin as a cicada’s wings was offered up... This was a personal belonging of an immortal fairy, yet it could transform into a miniature fairyland for a short time, defending against the outside world.

To his right, a tall and mighty Immortal revealed his true form, that of a giant bear endowed with the power of the stars. His path to immortality seemed to be related to ‘star power’.

This giant bear Immortal clasped his bear paws together, and behind him emerged a projection of a sky full of stars, with the power of the stars accumulating around him to form three hundred armed star giant bears.

These giant bears carried illusory shields, each one appearing to be a star domain, blocking and isolating external attacks.

Another Immortal was purely offensive. He swung two divine weapons at the forefront, spewing blood while displaying exquisite swordsmanship, meeting attack with attack.

Another Immortal threw a vast amount of seeds, using them to start constructing the prototype of a secret realm on the spot, from which pure power continuously surged out, reinforcing the condition of his own side’s Immortals.

Out of the six severely injured Immortals, five had already employed magical techniques.

The last Immortal seemed to be too heavily injured; his face was devoid of color, and his ‘vitality’ had faded to an almost imperceptible level. He simply threw out two puppets, symbolically placing them at the forefront.

Across from them, when the first wave of attacks from the ten suns ended... the Immortal who was swinging his sword while vomiting blood had to retreat. The divine weapons in his hands were severely damaged by the ‘Cutting Light’ of the virtual sun.

The puppets were the first to be sliced into fragments and destroyed...

Scholar Yue Ruhuo’s sword formation was broken, and even the swords that formed the array could not be retrieved...

The fairyland of the immortal fairy was blown open by the Stellar Doomsday Demon’s explosion, forcibly...

In terms of frontal defense, only the three hundred star giant bears transformed by the giant bear Immortal were still desperately holding on. But the number of the star giant bears was sharply declining...

And the ten suns across from them did not give them a chance to reinforce their defenses.

Their attacks did not pause. Before the first wave had even ended, the second wave of bombardment was already upon them.

“Hold on for one more wave... I have friends already on their way,” Scholar Yue Ruhuo said calmly, analyzing the situation.

The advantage of the Cultivator Chat System was revealed at this moment.

At the first sign of the attack, Scholar Yue Ruhuo had already sent out rescue signals to all the friends he knew. His friends were already crossing space at the fastest speed to rush towards the Pure Land Space.

Among them, even the steel clone of Big Shot Tyrannical Song gave him a definite reply, stating that both it and the main body were on their way!

In fact, not just Scholar Yue Ruhuo, but the other Immortals were also calling their friends.

“Tyrannical Song is also arriving soon, hold on,” Scholar Yue Ruhuo said, painfully taking out a turtle shell – a treasure he had once acquired from the Almighty Merchant.

But due to severe damage and being irrepairable, every use meant one less opportunity.

“Tyrannical Song?” At this moment, the pale-faced Immortal behind him suddenly spoke up, his voice sounding like cold machinery.

A moment later, this Immortal shook his body.

“Since Tyrannical Song is going to appear, it can’t continue like this. Originally, what is here is just a puppet clone of mine; if broken, then so be it...” Saying this, the pale-faced Immortal reached into his chest and directly pulled out a core.

Then, he inserted his hand into the vacuum and opened a special space similar to Song Shuhang’s ‘main world,’ from which he took out an even bigger core and installed it into his body.

“Fellow daoists, have a rest for a while. From now on, leave it to me,” said the puppet Immortal, his voice transitioning from a mechanical tone to that of a charming man.

The other injured Immortals nearby looked at this puppet man in confusion.

“Are you... from the Mo family?” At this moment, Scholar Yue Ruhuo recognized him.

This man was a Mo family genius who had stepped onto the immortal path through ‘Puppet Dao.’

He was not the founder of the puppet technique, but he had surpassed the Mo family’s founder, stepping onto the path to immortality through Puppet Dao.

This Mo family genius had attained immortality during the late era of the Confucian Saints, before the Heavenly Emperor’s proving his Dao, between two invincible Immortals.

“`

There was an invincible Confucian Sage in times past, and then came the Heavenly Emperor, who reigned supreme for a myriad of generations, making this Mo family genius appear very low-key.

After the age of the Heavenly City ended, he rarely showed his face.

However, in the myriad practitioners in the universe, his footsteps are everywhere, with evidence of his research into ‘puppets’. Many cultivators have found remains of the puppets he battled within the depths of secret realms, reaping great benefits from them.

No wonder I felt that his face was bloodless before, and that his resistance wasn’t all that determined... The one here is just a puppet that can be replaced at any time.

“Fellow friend of the Mo family, do you also know Tyrannical Song?” Scholar Yue Ruhuo asked aloud.

“We have crossed paths indirectly once,” said the Mo family’s Immortal, undergoing a transformation after a new nucleus was installed.

A faint radiance enveloped the puppet body, and the original puppet actually began developing flesh and blood, evolving a special Puppet Dao. In a short time, it transformed into a genuine fleshly body.

After the transformation completed, the Mo family Immortal took a step forward, moving past the defensive line formed by the Star Giant Bears, and faced the destruction assault of the ten suns directly.

An apocalyptic flame, rays imbued with the principles of cutting, and a pillar of light from the virtual giant sun that pierced through everything, all focused fire on him.

“Before challenging Tyrannical Song... it’s not your turn,” the Mo family Immortal said with a slight smile... Beneath that smile hid his pride.

In his youth, he witnessed the might of the Confucian Sage without challenging him, only watching from a distance the battles between the Confucian Sage and various Immortals, gaining a deep understanding of the Confucian Sage’s strength at the time.

Later, when the ancient Heavenly City was established, he met the Heavenly Emperor once but did not challenge him, only engaging in a dialogue on the Dao.

After the discussion, he left a ‘puppetized manifestation’ in the ancient Heavenly City for the Heavenly Emperor to command.

Having witnessed the prowess of the Sage and personally engaged in discourse with the Heavenly Emperor, he knew very well the preeminent realm they occupied, one which was already half a step beyond ‘the limits of the Immortals’.

And now...

“I have finally reached the end,” he said.

The realm he was in now had already surpassed ‘the limits of the Immortals’.

For instance, the joint attack of the ten suns, though terrifying, seemed to him... nothing more than that.

The Mo family Immortal raised his hand, and a plain white cloak ‘grew’ out of his back.

With a gesture, he lifted the cloak, sweeping toward those apocalyptic flames, rays, and pillars of light.

The next moment, all attacks from the ten suns were swept away by him!

It was like brushing away a feeble breeze; he casually swept away all the attacks that could heavily injure a regular Immortal with ease.

Behind him, Scholar Yue Ruhuo and the other five Immortals’ pupils slightly contracted.

With just one strike, they could feel the gap between themselves and the Mo family genius.

The Star Giant Bear Immortal was particularly silent for a long time.

After a while, it said, “I feel as though I’m facing the Confucian Sage once more.”

This was another figure who had been hammered by the Confucian Sage in the past—because the hammering by the Confucian Sage was so traumatic, resulting in psychological shadows, it developed a complete three hundred Star Giant Bear Invincible Defense Formations.

The spectacle had stunned the ten suns on the opposite side, causing their continuous bombardment to pause for a split second.

For the Mo family genius, that split second was enough to do a lot.

The plain white cloak shifted its shape, turning into a giant bow in the hands of the Mo family Immortal—his cloak seemed to share a marvelous contrast with Song Shuhang’s ‘fat ball’.

Drawing the bow, fitting an arrow to it, he shot lightly.

There were no special effects added, just a very pure arrow.

Once the arrow was released, it locked onto causality, striking a ‘Stellar Doomsday Demon Skull’ that was the weakest of all, with only the strength of a ‘weak Immortal’.

After being hit, the enemy didn’t even have a chance to scream.

Even a stone hit by a single Pregnant Gaze would be forced to experience ‘the greatness of motherhood.’

The Confucian Sages of old would not start by educating others on the greatness of motherhood!

Occasionally, Immortals who had experienced the Sage’s ‘Expert’s Appraisal’ had brought it upon themselves by displeasing the Sage.

After being hit, Mo family’s Tian Zhi only felt a faint reaction in his abdomen... thankfully, this reaction was fleeting.

First, his body was that of a puppet.

“Being immune to the Expert’s Appraisal indicates that you have truly touched that realm,” Tyrannical Song slowly said from the other side.

Without having reached this realm, one would tremble under the Sage Level ‘Expert’s Appraisal.’

In the meantime, a spatial gate appeared next to Mo family’s Tian Zhi.

It was opened by Tyrannical Song.

Even in this ‘Immortal Information Blockade’ plus ‘a powerful Killing Formation suppressing’ Paradise Space, Tyrannical Song could still open spatial passages at will!

The spatial gate moved like a shadow, closely following Mo family’s Tian Zhi.

On the other side of the spatial gate, Tyrannical Song swung his fists, frantically punching into the gate, unleashing a barrage of punches.

Boom boom boom boom boom~

From the other side of the spatial gate, Tyrannical Song’s iron fists smashed towards Mo family’s Tian Zhi.

[This move truly has the flavor of a Sage!] Most of the Immortals present had been hammered by this move before, so upon seeing this scene, the flavor of a Sage emerged in their minds, and they simultaneously felt a phantom pain in their bodies.

Whoosh~ Fellow Daoist Mo Family Tian Zhi was not panicked; his windbreaker unfolded, enveloping him.

Although he had never directly challenged a Scholarly Sage, he had watched from afar the battles between a Sage and other Immortals on multiple occasions.

Boom boom boom boom~

Tyrannical Song’s iron fists continuously bombarded the windbreaker, and each first punch left a fist imprint on it, with the force even penetrating the windbreaker and directly hitting Mo family’s Tian Zhi.

Song Shuhang, although he was trying his best to suppress himself and simulate the fist strength of the Scholarly Sage from his memories—his body had already achieved a Sub-immortal status.

His fists, even when deliberately suppressed, were still a ‘Sub-immortal Level’ deadly weapon.

With each punch that landed, it carried an inherent bonus of additional damage.

Moans continued to emanate from inside the windbreaker of Fellow Daoist Mo Family Tian Zhi; even in his puppetized state, he couldn’t avoid the pain inflicted by Tyrannical Song’s punches.

This pain affected directly the soul, causing a feeling of powerlessness.

After a furious volley of punches, the barrage ended, and Tyrannical Song closed the spatial gate.

In the Void.

Mo Family Tian Zhi’s windbreaker dispersed, revealing a body covered with wounds.

Although these wounds started to heal quickly.

But injured meant injured!

“Even at this level, the gap between me and a Sage still exists,” stated Fellow Daoist Mo Family Tian Zhi softly.

The hallmark of a Sage, ‘Knowledge’s Iron Fist,’ when fully deployed, brought him substantial injury.

He looked thoughtfully at Tyrannical Song across from him.

A moment later.

“Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, how big is the gap between you and me?” Mo Family Tian Zhi grasped his spear: “I wish to test it.”

He began to gather all his power.

Behind him, phantoms of the myriad realms emerged.

In each plane of the myriad worlds, a ‘puppet’ was receiving power and transferring it to Tian Zhi at this moment.

“Gathering all my power in one strike, please instruct me, Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song,” Mo Family Tian Zhi raised his spear.

But this time, he wasn’t using it in a spear-thrusting stance.

Instead, he raised it high like a javelin.

The attack, gathering the power of countless puppets in the myriad worlds, had the other Immortals shuddering just by sensing the strike.

Most Immortals envisioned themselves in Tyrannical Song’s place.

If they were to face this strike... they might die!

How will Tyrannical Song confront this strike?

Everyone’s eyes turned back to Tyrannical Song.

[No movement?]

Facing this strike that concentrated the power of myriad worlds, capable of destroying any Immortal, Tyrannical Song showed no response.

He did not put up a defense, use any magical treasures, nor did he activate the ‘windbreaker’ on his body!

Mo Family Tian Zhi’s eyes also narrowed.

But the arrow had to be shot once the bow was drawn.

Boom~

The spear was thrown, shooting towards Tyrannical Song.

Chapter 3107: Chapter 3105: I, Tyrannical Song, Seek Eternity. Who Dares Not Accept?
 

This strike gathered the power of all the puppets set up within the “myriad practitioners in the universe” by Mister Tian Zhi of the Mo family; it was his truly full-powered strike!

The bright armor and cape on his body had already merged into the spearhead, pushing his life-bound magical treasure in its “Gun Form” to the ultimate limit.

The speed of this throw was so fast that even when the Immortals concentrated all their efforts, they could only barely see an afterimage.

Midway, the spear already turned scarlet from the powerful energy infused into it.

[?]

[Why isn’t he defending? Does Tyrannical Song intend to take this spear with his face?]

Directly onto the eyeball!

During this, Tyrannical Song did not even twitch an eyelid!

A true man faces imminent danger without even fluttering his eyelids—it’s a loss if he does!

[!]

This part of the damage would take a long time to slowly mend.

Spectating cultivators like Scholar Yue Ruhuo didn’t even dare to move.

Truly evolving into ‘Ultimate Tyrannical Song.’

Awkward.

Senior Song, you are going to offend Heavenly Emperor’s sister this way, meaning that she also cannot penetrate your eyelids!

Chapter 3108: Chapter 3106: The current Will of the Heavens turns out to be Tyrannical Song perfecting the setup of the ‘immortal path’!

Chapter 3109: Chapter 3107: Tyrannical Song Insists on Saying NO to the Strongest Rule
 

Fellow Daoist Tian Zhi of the Mo family had the strongest strength and the highest vision and persevered for the longest.

Moreover, his immortal path was that of puppets, and he was naturally very adept at “calculation.”

When his calculation power was fully unleashed, he could control billions of puppets simultaneously, displaying entirely different behaviors and even continuously simulating different lives.

Speaking of “calculation ability,” Tian Zhi of the Mo family ranked among the top Immortals throughout the ages.

Therefore, upon seeing the “cheat” transmitted to Tyrannical Song by the pillar of light, he was the first to discern the truth!

Of course... the reason he could perceive it so quickly and was somewhat “immune” to the shock of the immortal information was that he had secretive help.

Behind the scenes, a group of people wanted to use the mouthpiece of this most prominent ‘Mo family genius Immortal’ to release some shocking news that was not a secret, to confirm everyone’s suspicion that ‘Heavenly Dao is Tyrannical Song’s tool.’

It’s not horrifying to brag about oneself, but what’s truly terrifying is when the bragging is technically skilled and even stronger in power.

“Heavenly Dao Level Computational Ability?” Fellow Daoists like Scholar Yue Ruhuo at the scene felt their jaws numb with shock.

The current Tyrannical Song, is he already the Heavenly Dao?” said the constantly bleeding dual-blade swordsman, wiping the blood from the corner of his mouth.

Now, with a mortal body, he aims to conquer the Heavenly Dao. Without proving by the ‘Dao,’ he possesses all eternal attributes of the ‘Heavenly Dao,'” Scholar Yue Ruhuo slowly said.

This man is too terrifying.

Throughout history, no one has managed to achieve what this man has to this extent. Even the successive Heavenly Daos have never been like Tyrannical Song.

The cheat was activated!

But this was just the beginning of the cheat’s activation!

The cheat not only upgraded his software but also improved his hardware capabilities, enhancing both simultaneously.

Song Shuhang could feel his primordial soul, stored in fragmented parts in the ‘Tribulation Transcender Void Node,’ also beginning to be reinforced.

Senior White’s primordial soul was also being reinforced, alongside him.

Fleshly body, power, primordial soul, all sub-immortalized, along with the ‘undying fat whale golden core’ secured at the core, the current Song Shuhang could be said to have become a perfect organism.

Apart from not having ‘Heavenly Dao Authority,’ he was almost indistinguishable from the Heavenly Dao.

In this state, even if the myriad realms were obliterated, he could survive tenaciously, struggling into the start of a new era just like the Black Dragon World.

Moreover, with the main world bound to him, he could also enclose people he cared about plus the majority of Earth’s population into it, preserving them sealed away.

“Much better than I had imagined... at least, I have a way out,” Song Shuhang thought to himself.

Of course, this way out is only for desperate situations.

Song Shuhang was not willing to put himself in such dire circumstances.

What he sought was to prove his Dao with Senior White and then transcend, thereafter resolving the regrets of the past and the calamities of the future in one breath!

“This miracle, piled up by everyone from the past, present, and future, will be continued by Senior White and me,” Song Shuhang clenched his fists.

He was well aware that he and Senior White were currently at the turning point of this ‘miracle’.

What he had to do was to not let this hard-won ‘miracle’ break apart but to make it continue onwards and become an undying legend!

Only this way, he wouldn’t let down the past and the future.

Song Shuhang slowly opened his eyes.

In his eyes, there was no hint of confusion, for he was clear about what he had to do next, what his goal was.

As Song Shuhang opened his eyes, in the vacuum of myriad practitioners in the universe, the illusory symphony of the Heavenly Dao’s complete retirement resounded—it was the bugle announcing the abdication.

At the same time, it also signaled the start of the ‘new Heavenly Dao contention’. Amidst this illusory symphony, immortals from myriad worlds could battle to seize the next tenure of Heavenly Dao, the victor glimpsing the secrets of the Great Way’s eternity.

In the past, all immortals would be moved at such a time.

Even those with no intention of competing for the Heavenly Dao would not miss such a grand event.

But this time, the hearts of immortals from myriad worlds were serene, undisturbed.

All eyes were on Tyrannical Song, silently waiting for Tyrannical Song to speak.

Tyrannical Song was now a ‘Heavenly Dao walking among mortals’. It was uncertain whether he still had any desire for the ‘Heavenly Dao seat’.

If Tyrannical Song had no intention of competing for the Heavenly Dao, that would truly mark the beginning of the ‘Heavenly Dao contention’.

If Tyrannical Song desired this Heavenly Dao seat, then nobody from myriad worlds would object—Tian Zhi’s shot hadn’t even pierced the outer membrane of Tyrannical Song’s eyeball. Had it been another immortal, they probably couldn’t even slice off a single hair from Tyrannical Song!

In the vacuum, that ethereal symphony marking the Heavenly Dao’s resignation ended.

Tyrannical Song finally spoke.

“Senior White, come out~ It’s our time next!” Song Shuhang squatted on the ground and gently tapped the surface.

The next moment, a spatial passage opened on the ground.

The handsome White stepped out of the spatial gate, patting his spotless clothes, first carefully checking the foot he put forward.

After ensuring it was firmly placed, he stepped forward with his second foot.

“Proving the Dao now?” Senior White asked.

“That’s right, now,” Song Shuhang nodded, raising his right hand towards Senior White.

Senior White stretched out his hand and lightly high-fived Song Shuhang.

Mo family Tian Zhi: “!!!”

From the exchange between Tyrannical Song and Senior White, he heard a shocking piece of news.

“Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, you and Fellow Daoist White... are proving the Dao together?” Mo family Tian Zhi once again played the role of a ‘narrator’.

Such a thing was possible?

Initially, it seemed that Tyrannical Song intended to conquer the Heavenly Dao with a mortal body, but now it appears that Tyrannical Song is clearly planning to grind the dignity of the ‘Heavenly Dao seat’ into the ground.

According to the rules, there can be at most one person for each Heavenly Dao.

But Tyrannical Song insists on saying NO to this supreme rule.

Chapter 3110: Chapter 3108: A Domination Secret Method, a Gift for the Beloved Tyrannical Song Contestant!
 

This man was born to “break rules”.

His beginning mere actions included rubbing the rules of the Profound Sage Speech on the ground over and over again.

Afterward, he continuously broke the rules of the main world, the Netherworld Realm, and eternity.

Now, he would challenge the ultimate dignity of the realm of rules—the laws of the Heavenly Dao.

From today onwards, perhaps no rule in the myriad practitioners in the universe could bind this man—the only thing that could was himself.

The era that followed would be the era of Tyrannical Song.

A supreme immortal of the Mo family provided a non-diegetic commentary in his heart.

...

...

At the same time.

In an endless darkness.

A qualified figure pulling the strings, a Dark Giant suffering from all-nighters due to various reasons, was once again involuntarily awakened, and slowly three question marks emerged in his mind.

Sleep deprivation plus severe morning grumpiness made it irritable.

Buzz × 10!

What’s going on, why did I forcibly wake up again!

A moment later...

“The Will of the Heavens has abdicated?”

Another question mark rose in the mind of the figure pulling the strings.

What the hell?

According to the intelligence it had received... hadn’t the Will just assumed the position not long ago?

And yet, not long before, it had sensed the dominance of the current Wielder of the Will.

With the state of the current Wielder of the Will, it felt like there wouldn’t be any problems for billions of years.

Even, if nothing unexpected occurred, the current Wielder of the Will appeared to be the type to stay in the Heavenly Dao seat forever!

——This was the determination issued to the myriad practitioners in the universe by the implicit Will not so long ago.

Because of this, after rescuing the ‘Black Sun’, it assigned the task to the Immortal Daoist Body it “dominated” and then, as it couldn’t resist the urge to sleep, its background self gradually fell into deep slumber.

Its slumber state was a kind of “price”.

It was the heavy price paid for “freeing” itself from the Heavenly Dao seat back then.

Recharging for tens of millions of years, being active for a hundred years, and then, power-saving mode could sustain it a little longer against sleepiness.

This root problem was incurable and beyond healing.

Additionally, it’s worth mentioning that initially, its “awake time” could be longer, and the time it could be active after a full charge was more abundant than now. But later, because it angered a woman, under her various schemes, its active time after charging was at least halved.

Originally, it planned this time to have a good sleep to gather energy before coming out to make a big move, to push forward its grand plan.

But now... not even a month had passed, and the Heavenly Dao had abdicated?

Such an operation was crazy.

“What is going on with the thought processes of the recent Wielders of the Will?” It felt its state was awful.

Forced to wake up from an all-nighter, it had barely held up its exhaustion to complete the preparation work at hand, and it had barely returned to the cozy quilt ready to doze off for a while, but as soon as it fell asleep, it was forcibly awakened again.

This state was too miserable for words.

“Fortunately, I’ve finished storing energy for my ‘Domineering Secret Method’, and next, I can close my eyes and rest a bit longer... waiting for the upcoming ‘contestation for the Heavenly Dao’, hoping to fully rejuvenate before the next Wielder of the Will assumes a higher position.” The figure pulling the strings muttered to itself.

Its current state was very ominous.

It had to snatch every second to refresh itself before the contention for the Heavenly Dao concluded, to adjust its own condition.

Saying so, the Dark Giant once again closed its eyes, hastening to adjust its state.

But just as it had entered “adjustment mode,” something akin to an “alarm clock” function next to it emitted a jarring noise, jolting it from its “resting” state.

Dark Giant: “?”

At this moment, the weight of the question mark in its mind surpassed that of all previous question marks combined.

What happened again?

Wait a moment, let me wake up.

The first alarm clock’s sound marked the occasion of the “Heavenly Dao successor” being chosen.

The second, even more startling alarm clock, heralded that “someone was about to prove their Dao and achieve immortality,” a call for immediate action!

“Buzz what? Did my time just jump?” The Dark Giant’s emotions were in turmoil!

The mortal method of “let me sleep for five more minutes” actually worked on him as well?

Had the time passed by hundreds or even thousands of years while he just dozed off?

No... that’s not right.

There was no issue with the passage of time.

That means.

As soon as the “Heavenly Dao had stepped down,” someone immediately took over seamlessly and proved his immortality!

What’s going on here?

Where were all the immortals in the myriad practitioners in the universe?

Were they just for show?

No one stepped forward to prevent this newcomer from taking the Heavenly Dao seat?

They just watched as the target proved his Dao?

Is everyone’s desire for “eternity” really that low?

Even if it were Tyrannical Song trying to prove his Dao, immortals couldn’t possibly sit idly by, right?

I’m starting to understand this world less and less.

And what about... my Black Sun and Immortal Daoist manifestation? Why haven’t they reacted?

But no matter what, no matter how many doubts he had inside, he had to act.

Even if his own state was terrible, unendurable, with the other party about to start proving his Dao for immortality, if he didn’t act now, he would miss the chance.

So the Dark Giant struggled, using his will to resist the drowsiness surging up and with his tenacious will, he squeezed out of the endless dark, descending upon the main world.

He was the being who had failed time and time again, but was able to stand up over and over; a mere drowsiness, with will power, he could overcome!

After stealthily arriving, the Dark Giant faintly sensed the main world’s rejection of him.

“I don’t have much time, I must make it quick,” the Dark Giant thought to himself.

After infiltrating the main world, just like before, he utilized the Stealth Secret Method developed during his time as the Wielder of the Will, carefully concealing his figure, and then through spatial movement, he snuck into the location of the “new Heavenly Dao’s proof of Dao.”

When he quietly reached the destination, he noticed that the majority of immortals from the myriad practitioners in the universe had actually gathered in this tiny Gem Domain.

Next, he saw the candidate about to prove his Dao.

As expected, it was that “Tyrannical Song.”

But to his surprise... Tyrannical Song wasn’t alone in proving his Dao; by his side was another all too familiar scoundrel.

The beautiful White.

A big question mark emerged in the Dark Giant’s mind once again.

?

From the current scene, were these two about to prove their Dao together?

How could this be achieved?

More importantly...

If two were to prove their Dao together, whom should his “Domination Secret Method” be used on?

Should it be used on that scoundrel White? Or Tyrannical Song?

After hesitating for a moment, the Dark Giant quickly made a decision.

Is that even a question?

Of course, he’d choose Tyrannical Song!

Having been tricked by the handsome White so many times, he had no reason to chew on this tough bone.

So, without further thought—in fact, the situation didn’t allow for it.

He manipulated the secret techniques, sending a “Domination Secret Method” towards Tyrannical Song.

Chapter 3111: Chapter 3109: What to Do When There’s Never Enough Time at Critical Moments?

“What If”:

If the Dark Giant’s drowsiness wasn’t so profound, and his consciousness could be more alert to discover properly...

If the Dark Giant’s time wasn’t so urgent, giving him more time to ponder in detail...

Then, he would have noticed that there were quite a few issues with this instance of ‘Tyrannical Song + White proving their Dao’!

—Why, when the Heavenly Dao was about to step down, were all the immortals from the myriad practitioners in the universe gathered together?

—With so many immortals present, why did not a single one step forward to stop Tyrannical Song? No one could delay Tyrannical Song even for a moment. He was allowed to start proving his Dao the instant the Heavenly Dao abdicated?

—Moreover, having so many immortals converge in one place seemed like prep work for Tyrannical Song to ‘cut through the chaos with a swift stroke,’ stunning the audience in one breath, and rapidly proving his Dao!

Had he not been so drowsy, he would have noticed these issues at first glance!

Furthermore, if he had a little more time, he would have seen that at this moment, Tyrannical Song, from inside out, had transformed into a ‘Sub-immortal’ state, becoming a perfect being!

This condition was obviously very problematic!

Theoretically, even if the current Heavenly Dao helped Tyrannical Song with all its might, it would be impossible to enable him to achieve this ‘Full Body Semi-Immortal’ mode—this was, in fact, a minor restriction from the Heavenly Dao Authority.

Otherwise, each Heavenly Dao in office could create a ‘mini-immortal’ friend, and the world would have been in chaos long ago!

This state was not something that a single Heavenly Dao could achieve.

But Tyrannical Song had indeed gathered information from the second to eighth Heavenly Daos, as well as immortal information from an 8.5th Heavenly Dao!

This was simply an impossible miracle to accomplish!

Not every Heavenly Dao knew each other, and there were even feuds between some Heavenly Daos.

The idea of getting the Heavenly Daos of all eras to cooperate on creating such a ‘Sub-immortal being’ was utterly fanciful!

Yet Tyrannical Song had done just that!

Unfortunately...

Reality is harsh, it isn’t a composition, and there’s no “What If”.

Therefore, the Dark Giant, pushed to the limit by drowsiness and time, simply didn’t have the time to ponder more.

The little ‘thinking time’ he had was spent choosing between Tyrannical Song and the beautiful but tricky White.

An already prepared ‘Domination Secret Method’ fell silently upon Song Shuhang’s person.

It went smoothly.

The Dark Giant inwardly breathed a sigh of relief.

As with the states in which it had cast the ‘Domination Secret Method’ before, even an existence on the verge of proving his Dao couldn’t possibly notice its secret techniques.

After that, whether it would be both Tyrannical Song and the beautiful but tricky White proving their Dao together or just Tyrannical Song alone wouldn’t be a problem!

And even if Tyrannical Song were to fail at proving his Dao, and the beautiful but tricky White succeeded instead... its ‘Domination Secret Method,’ improved in the last Heavenly Dao era, could also transfer to the one proving his Dao, albeit with somewhat diminished effects.

[This time, there will no longer be any question...] As he thought this, waves of sleepiness bombarded the Dark Giant’s consciousness, and his mental processing began to slow.

[bly.] The Dark Giant muttered in his heart.

But just as this thought finally formed in his mind...an anomaly occurred on the opposite side!

Senior White and Song Shuhang, who were undergoing the ‘Dao-proving process,’ maintained their clapping posture.

Suddenly, Song Shuhang’s mouth curved up, revealing an evil smile.

For his honest, kindly good guy face to reveal such an evil smile was really not a small feat.

But he managed it!

With Song Shuhang’s smile, Senior White understood what was happening.

“Has the secret technique arrived?” Senior White asked.

“It has, I’ve waited quite a while for it,” Song Shuhang replied with a nod.

“Then I’ll help you form the handprints, inscribe the formations, and you’ll cooperate by casting,” Senior White extended his other hand, beginning to form the handprints for the ‘Reverse Dominating Secret Technique.’

—At this time, what Senior White held in one hand was Song Shuhang’s ‘primordial spirit projection,’ so as long as the two cooperated, Senior White could form the handprints on behalf of Song Shuhang.

Two beautiful runes condensed from the tips of White’s fingers, landing on Song Shuhang’s body.

Song Shuhang cooperated and began absorbing the ancient power of the Domination Secret Method from the Dark Giant, which had been refined and improved by the Seniors over tens of millions of years!

Although he couldn’t see where the Dark Giant was hiding, he was... thankful for the Domination Secret Method and the tens of millions of years of power that the Dark Giant had generously donated.

Once I and Senior White successfully complete ‘proving the Dao of two different individuals at the same time,’ you will have your share of the credit!

The Dark Giant hiding in the shadows was taken aback momentarily.

Its mind, which was running slowly due to intense drowsiness, was once again rudely awakened by the external stimulus—it was like a fatigued driver who had finally reached the destination after a long drive, only to let down his guard and crash the car into the wall of his own home, flipping over and waking up in an instant!

“My secret technique, is it being swallowed?”

“Wait... Tyrannical Song’s state?”

“No, I can’t let Tyrannical Song continue like this.”

The startled Dark Giant, although its thinking had become clearer, still didn’t have ‘time’ to ponder further.

Time is something that you never seem to value until it becomes crucial. And when that time comes, it becomes stingy, unwilling to give you even a moment more.

That’s the case with the Dark Giant, it’s short on time.

But now, its only choice is... to disrupt Tyrannical Song.

And the only way it can do that is with a single plan.

It must bring the Black Sun and the Immortal Daoist Body over and confront Tyrannical Song head-on.

Unless it wants to give up on Tyrannical Song’s era, it has no other choice.

This is a blatant plot.

And just in time, the Black Sun and the Immortal Daoist have also leaped across space!

The Black Sun is also in despair.

Ever since part of its ‘existence’ was swallowed by Tyrannical Song and White, its thinking has become clearer, its actions more cautious, and it prepares multiple contingency plans.

When it sensed that its sent ‘Void Sun Guardians, Stellar Doomsday Demon Skull’ died inside the Heavenly Dao Tomb, it knew something unexpected had happened there.

With caution, it prepared several plans to carefully probe the situation of the Gem Domain’s ‘Heavenly Dao Tomb.’

But while it was formulating its plans... it suddenly sensed that the Heavenly Dao had abdicated.

So, the cautious sun changed its policy and prepared new plans, facing the earth-shaking event of the ‘Heavenly Dao abdication,’ which shocked the myriad practitioners in the universe.

But while it was preparing new plans... it suddenly sensed someone was about to ‘prove immortality.’

Plans, it seems, can never keep up with changes.

Thus, the Black Sun reluctantly gathered a few magical treasures, armed itself with the ‘Stellar Destruction Virus,’ and together with the ‘Immortal Daoist’ body, rushed to the site of the Dao proving.

Upon arrival, it indeed saw Tyrannical Song and White.

Everything was as it had expected.

[Attack, attack Tyrannical Song with all your might, disrupt its casting] At that moment, a voice materialized in its mind.

It was the long-missed command from the ‘Heavenly Dao True Body.’

Moreover, this time it was a forced command.

It didn’t even give the sun time to think.

Its body moved, revealing its true form, and it spread out the ‘Immortal Sand,’ involuntarily blasting towards Tyrannical Song.

Following close behind, the Immortal Daoist is swinging that pot-sized fist, seemingly about to join it in confronting Tyrannical Song... but the position of the Daoist isn’t quite right.

The Daoist and it formed a straight line.

It’s like a line of spear-wielding soldiers, with Soldier A thrusting his spear towards the enemy.

Soldier B also thrust his spear.

But if not handled properly, Soldier B’s spear could very well mercilessly stab into Soldier A.

Chapter 3112: Chapter 3110: The Fist of the Enemy Makes Me Stronger—Cultivation Chat Immortal Path, Begin!
 

The attack from the Dark Sun arrived first at Song Shuhang and Senior White.

Immortal sand scattered and covered the sky, enveloping Song Shuhang’s figure.

Then, an endless barrage of sand, like raindrops, shot towards Song Shuhang and White’s location!

In this urgent moment, the Dark Sun didn’t even have time to unleash any large-scale skills or powerful lethal moves. Its task at this time was to interrupt Song Shuhang’s state.

Thus, it employed the most primitive yet most effective method of attack, calling forth all the immortal sand and launching an attack on Song Shuhang with the ‘immortal’ attribute.

Each grain of this immortal sand, a fragment of the Fourth Heavenly Dao, could easily destroy a solar system when bursting forth.

And at this moment, all the sand was focused fire on Tyrannical Song!

Even with Song Shuhang having condensed a ‘Sub-immortal Body’, facing such a bombardment, he would be in great pain!

Because the ‘immortality’ information grade of the other party was stronger than his, above him!

The powerful ‘immortal’ force would suppress the weaker ‘Sub-immortal’ state.

But...

The onslaught from the Dark Sun had only just begun when suddenly, a loud roar from the Immortal Daoist Body came from behind!

“Ah la ah la~ Ah la la la~” The Immortal Daoist Body roared and bellowed like a beast.

At the same time, his pair of iron fists pounded forward frantically!

He was indeed aiming his attacks at Tyrannical Song and White.

But the soldier A Dark Sun in front of him impeded his line of attack.

So the Dark Sun, with a confused look, was the first to suffer from this crazy barrage of punches!

The attack speed of the Immortal Daoist was several times faster than that of the Dark Sun... so his fists, though launched later, struck first. Before the Dark Sun’s assault reached Tyrannical Song and White, the fists of the Immortal Daoist had already slammed into the Dark Sun!

An unforgiving stabbing from an ally!

Boom boom boom~ Bang bang bang~

Violence! This sight was pure violence, fist to flesh, sending one’s blood racing with excitement!

In this moment, everyone could feel a momentum from the ‘Immortal Daoist’s’ fists—no one could stop him from striking Tyrannical Song!

Whoever stood before his fists would be smashed to pieces!

True grit, unyielding to the end!

Amidst the beastly roars of the Immortal Daoist, the sand particles transformed by the Dark Sun were punched tens of thousands of times and were forcibly exploded!

These tens of thousands of punches if converted into words, would be at least sixty pages worth!

After being pounded for a full sixty pages, the sand controlled by the Dark Sun was completely scattered, flung into every corner of ‘Paradise Space’!

The Dark Sun felt excruciating pain all over, with giant question marks popping up in its mind.

Was I hit?

Who hit me?

Why hit me?

All these changes happened in the blink of an eye.

Not only was the Dark Sun puzzled, but even Song Shuhang had a dumbfounded look on his face.

The Dark Giant of the Fourth Heavenly Dao hiding in the shadows closed his eyes in pain, his heart aching.

He had not anticipated that before the attack on Tyrannical Song, his own ‘Dark Sun Avatar’ and ‘Domination Immortal Daoist’ would end up fighting each other.

But fortunately... after the Immortal Daoist had exploded the ‘Dark Sun’, the attack did not stop.

“Ah la la la~” He continued to roar like a beast, his unmatched iron fists relentlessly smashing towards Tyrannical Song’s location.

Because of the speed of his fists, to the many Immortals watching, it was as if millions of punches were being thrown at Tyrannical Song in one breath!

Not even the Buddhist lost technique ‘Thousand-Handed Guanyin Fist’ could compare to one ten-thousandth of this!

Boom~~

The moment his fists made contact with Tyrannical Song, Tyrannical Song was blown apart!

The exploding Song Shuhang turned into a ball of fire that rose up into the air.

And within that burst of flames, one could faintly see the figure of a flaming adult Sixteen.

Mister Tyrannical Song’s death-evading secret technique — Flame Substitute Technique!

This time, the blasted flaming Sixteen shivered uncontrollably, not daring to utter another word.

She had never imagined that, after disappearing for two months, the ‘enemy’ Mister Tyrannical Song faced had suddenly reached the ‘Immortal Existence’ level — the pinnacle!

She was just a pathetic monster with the ability to ‘invade the body of a cultivator’, and from her birth to now, she had never seen such an enormous scene.

The moment the Immortal Fist burst upon her and blew her apart, she almost felt like she was truly about to experience a ‘cruel death’, with even her existence mark being erased by the power of eternity.

But luckily, her ‘Life Line’ now resided in Mister Tyrannical Song.

After being blown up, as long as Mister Tyrannical Song performed the ‘Flame Substitute Technique’ again, she could come out.

[But I don’t want to come out at all, I was wrong, isn’t that enough?] At this moment, the flaming adult Sixteen was truly frightened — Mister Tyrannical Song, when you confront ‘immortals’ and defy the ‘Heavenly Dao’ in these ‘Big Boss level events’, can you please not drag me, a minor monster, into it?

“Ah la la la~” After blowing up the Flame Substitute, the Immortal Daoist did not stop.

His eyes blood-red, he locked onto Mister Tyrannical Song’s position again and charged like a wild ox!

This time, Song Shuhang did not use the Flame Substituting Technique or similar means to evade.

“Come on! Hit me!” Song Shuhang activated his four great body refining techniques.

The ‘Holy Ape Dragon Power Technique’ that had been deduced to the ultimate.

The mutated and further mutated ‘Mutated Steel Hand Technique’.

The ‘Scholarly Indestructible Body of the Buddha’ strengthened by a Sage from Confucianism.

The ‘Liquid Golden Body’ with the added blessing of the fat ball.

This was the first time he had fully activated his defensive cultivation techniques since condensing the Sub-immortal State.

A rustling sound echoed.

The entire ‘Paradise Space’ above was instantly filled with innumerable monkeys.

A huge number that was impossible to count, even overlapping each other due to insufficient space in the ‘Paradise’, the army of Holy Apes manifested before everyone.

The Great Holy Ape, gifted by Senior White two, guarded the center.

The Holy Apes had bodies like the ‘fat ball’ with pitch-black liquid metal coating them, true dragons wrapped around their necks, and Confucian classics spread out in their hands.

“Hit me, come on and try to hit me!”

“If you don’t kill me, I’m going to kill you!”

“Today I have a wish, either I die by your hands, or I kill all of you!”

“English online translation: Hit_me!”

Thousands of Holy Apes spoke at the same time, taunting the Immortal Daoist.

And that wasn’t the end of it.

“Saber intent armor!”

“Big bone shards of Song Shuhang!”

“Empress made of light of virtue•Heavenly Court Projection Defense!”

Taking advantage of the brief ‘time’ gained by the ‘Flame Sixteen Replacement’, Song Shuhang set up layers upon layers of despair-inducing defense in one breath.

So many defenses, which all had the ‘Sub-immortal’ attribute boost.

If an Immortal Level existence tried to launch an attack, it might take years just to break through these defenses!

And it wasn’t until that moment.

Mr. Tian Zhi from the Mo family, Scholar Yue Ruhuo, Star Bear, and a few other Immortals finally reacted to the sudden events!

The changes that had just happened were too quick, so quick that even Immortals couldn’t keep up.

[Is this sand transformed from the Dark Sun, carrying the aura of eternity on it? Is it true immortality? Stronger than the eternity on Mister Tyrannical Song?]

[And who is this Immortal Daoist who keeps roaring like a beast?]

[Why are they attacking Mister Tyrannical Song?]

[Are they trying to interrupt Tyrannical Song’s process of ‘Proving pseudo-immortality’?]

[Could it be the shadowy figures behind the scenes manipulating ‘Heavenly Dao’, or even influencing ‘Heavenly Dao’?]

The waters of the myriad practitioners in the universe, how profound!

Those at the pinnacle of status among the Immortals seem to still have so much they do not understand!

“Those who can possess immortality, apart from Tyrannical Song’s kind of ‘pseudo-immortality’, are only the former Heavenly Dao.” Mister Tian Zhi from the Mo family began bleeding from his eyes from ‘directly gazing upon immortality’.

As expected, those ‘retired’ Heavenly Daos haven’t disappeared. Those Heavenly Dao still exist, hidden in the world in ways unknown to people.

And this time, Tyrannical Song’s ‘proving his Dao’ seems to have hurt the interests of a ‘past Heavenly Dao’, did the other party directly show their hand and take action against Tyrannical Song?

“The aura emanating from the Immortal Daoist and that of the fragments of the Dark Sun are different, are they two distinct ‘Heavenly Daos’?” Scholar Yue Ruhuo by now could no longer bear the strain, his body kneeling on the ground, his eyes seeming to split open.

Two Heavenly Daos, working together to deal with Tyrannical Song.

It was truly a dire situation within a dire situation.

Tyrannical Song, could he hold on?

This miraculous man, could he break out of this desperate situation?

“How laughable that I actually harbored the delusion of proving the Ninth Heavenly Dao.” Mister Tian Zhi from the Mo family covered his eyes in pain—if this time it wasn’t Tyrannical Song who was proving his Dao, but him instead... faced with a sudden attack from two ‘true immortals’, he probably would have been blasted to extinction on the spot.

Don’t lose, Tyrannical Song!

You are the man who defeated me, stand firm and upright against the attack, prove your immortality, and sweep all these guys into the trash heap of history!

Mister Tian Zhi’s consciousness began to blur, but he still struggled to maintain his intent—even if his eyeballs exploded, he wanted to see the end!

He wanted to witness Tyrannical Song prove his immortality with his own eyes!

Aside from Mister Tian Zhi of the Mo family, among the other Immortals, a large number have already fallen into a state of blurred consciousness, falling to the ground one by one.

The release of immortal information by two different immortals at the same time, the effect was way more than just double.

At the entrance of the Heavenly Dao Tomb.

The Almighty Merchant clutched the sheet tightly, his consciousness firmly locked on the ‘Immortal Daoist’.

“Hold on, Tyrannical Song,” he murmured softly.

In such a situation, he actually had to place his hopes on someone he had blacklisted, and the emotions in the Almighty Merchant’s heart were incredibly complicated.

But now, all he could hope for was that Tyrannical Song could hold on—the ‘Virtuous Seed’ he had given to Tyrannical Song would surely sprout one day!

...

...

“Ah-la-ah-la~ Ah-la-la~” The Immortal Daoist paused slightly, the next moment he swung his fist again, stirring the wind with his punches, and began to bombard the position where Song Shuhang was located like mad!

His punches covered a wide area.

The previously blown away Dark Sun tried to fly back but found no opportunity to get involved. The sand it controlled, if it got even a little closer, would be blown away by the ‘Ah-la-la’ fists of the Immortal Daoist!

If it weren’t for the fact that the Immortal Daoist’s punches were so solid, without any holding back, the Dark Sun would have suspected that this guy was an undercover, specifically targeting it.

Bang, bang, bang~

The ‘Heavenly Court Projection Defense’ held up by the virtuous lamia was shattered, and after shattering, all the light of virtue was added to Song Shuhang’s body, enhancing his state.

Immediately following, half of the body made of ‘Slow-Witted Song’s Big Bone Shards’ was also forcefully exploded—the entire process happened almost without any time difference.

As the Immortals watched intently, they saw the ‘projection of the Heavenly City’ and ‘Slow-Witted Song’s Big Bone Shards’ being wiped out almost simultaneously!

Too frightening, this is the fist of a true ‘Immortal’.

Without defense of the same level, there is simply no way to withstand a single blow!

Then, Song Shuhang’s ‘saber intent armor’ also couldn’t hold up.

After Song Shuhang’s ‘energy’ transformed into ‘Sub-immortal Power’, the saber intent armor also strengthened to the same level.

But it still couldn’t withstand a few punches and was blown to pieces.

The Immortals who still retained consciousness, upon seeing this scene, felt a chill in their hearts.

Even the terrifying Tyrannical Song, when facing true immortality, was retreating step by step, apparently without a chance of victory.

[Hurry up, hurry up and prove your immortality!] Mister Tian Zhi clenched his fists hard.

“Stop trying to ‘ascend together,’ even if it’s just one of us who needs to ascend to get through this wave!” someone among the Immortals thought anxiously.

Boom, boom, boom~

The Immortal Daoist’s fists crazily smashed down.

All of Song Shuhang’s other defenses were also shattered in one breath.

In the end, only his body tempering technique and a sub-immortal fleshly body remained.

“Senior White, take good care of yourself,” Song Shuhang said in a deep voice.

He transferred Sixteen, Pavilion Master Chu’s dumb hair, the white dragon sister’s scarf, Scarlet Heaven Sword, and Fellow Daoist Stone Tablet to Senior White first.

Even the fat ball cloak belonging to Song Shuhang was transferred.

At the same time, his body hugely expanded, becoming a small giant.

With the body tempering technique fully operational, his muscles bulged all over.

After turning into a small giant, Song Shuhang protected Senior White and all the seniors.

“You’re not going to dodge?” Pavilion Master Chu’s dumb hair asked with some concern.

“As long as the enemy’s fist can’t kill me in one hit, it will only make me stronger!” Song Shuhang revealed a reliably charming smile, “Trust me.”

His words were not only for Senior White and Pavilion Master Chu, but also for sending his conviction to the end of time.

Trust me, rely on me!

“Ah la, ah la, ah la~” The fists of the Immortal Daoist finally mercilessly struck Song Shuhang’s back.

A true clash between immortality and sub-immortality!

Boom~

The collision of fist and body rang out like a large bell.

This sound was like the sound of the Great Way—no, it was even higher level than that. This was the collision of Great Way against Great Way!

After officially contacting Song Shuhang, the Immortal Daoist’s fist quietly underwent some changes.

Rather than concentrating, the fist dispersed and hammered every corner of Song Shuhang’s body.

If one observed closely, they could see the Immortal Daoist’s fist landing on the ‘junctions’ of each of the ‘2-8.5’ Heavenly Dao immortal information within Song Shuhang’s body.

These places were the weak points in Song Shuhang’s ‘Sub-immortal Body’!

Even without consciousness, the Immortal Daoist’s body could still find the ‘weak points’ and execute a deathly hit within a short time.

The black sun who had been knocked away felt somewhat satisfied after seeing this scene.

One moment, two moments, three moments...

‘Sub-immortal’ blood was forced out from Song Shuhang’s body, and his sub-immortal body was marked with fist imprints.

“Is this an Immortal’s fist?” At this moment, Song Shuhang turned around.

It hurt so much!

If this continued, wouldn’t his body be pounded into a lump?

“It hurts, but it’s not that painful. It’s not enough, I have endured pain that is perhaps a hundred times worse than this.” After turning around, Song Shuhang started to counterattack!

❮Basic Buddhist Fist Technique❯—Meteor Punch!

Fist against fist, brutality against brutality, strength against strength!

Not only that.

“Self-corpse!” Song Shuhang mentally called out.

The silent projection of his self-corpse appeared behind him.

“Saint’s secret technique, the Immortal Path, transfer!” The Sage Eye Golden Core in his cheat lit up.

Parts of the ‘light of virtue and karmic ties’ from Song Shuhang’s Immortal Path were sacrificed and some fragments of the Immortal Path were transferred to his self-corpse.

Because the time was ripe.

Chapter 3113: Chapter 3111: The Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy’s VIP-Level Backup Plan
 

As Song Shuhang shouted, a tsunami-like sound emitted from the path to immortality that enveloped him.

The light of virtue and the rules of karmic immortality burned intensely...

The Sage’s “Confucian Classic” was summoned, appearing behind Song Shuhang.

Immediately afterward, the ‘Immortal’s Full Moon’ above Song Shuhang’s head began to dim.

Some of the immortals who were powerful enough to remain conscious, enduring the severe pain in their eyes as they continued to watch the battle, were puzzled by this scene.

But at this time, Song Shuhang hadn’t forgotten his ‘three corpses.’

After becoming ‘sub-immortal’ throughout his body, he developed a slight immunity to the effects of the Heavenly Dao’s small black room.

The ‘Cultivation Chat Immortal Path’ is not a solitary path to immortality.

The ‘Cultivation Chat Immortal Path’ loading progression 100%!

Loading complete!

This blade does not ferry across worlds; it simply opens a VIP passage within ‘reincarnation’ solely for the Fourth Heavenly Dao.

This immortal sand, grain by grain, was transported into the VIP passage opened by the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy, entering an infinite cycle of reincarnation.

If the immortal sand cannot be destroyed, then let it cycle through reincarnation endlessly.

As for when it might be released?

That would depend on the mood of the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy!

The ‘Fourth Heavenly Dao’ Dark Giant, hiding in the shadows and witnessing this scene, finally could not sit still anymore.

The process of ‘proving his Dao’ by the Heavenly Dao completed!
