Chapter 3114: Chapter 3112: Is This the Last Defiance of the Laws of the Heavenly Dao?
 

Yes, it was too fast!

Tyrannical Song and that handsome scoundrel should have jointly proven their Dao... Logically, proving the Dao should take even longer.

But it didn’t!

Even under normal circumstances when the Heavenly Dao begins to prove the Dao, and until the proving process completes, it requires a certain amount of time.

In the past, the Fourth Heavenly Dao ‘Dark Giant’ suffered in this respect—the handsome scoundrel, halfway through the lengthy ‘proving process,’ suddenly quit and then passed the ‘Heavenly Dao seat’ to Daoist Priest Virtue.

But now, Tyrannical Song and the handsome scoundrel, proving the Dao together, not only did not extend the time of the ‘proving process,’ but significantly shortened the proving time.

From start to finish, it took roughly only about one-third of the normal Heavenly Dao ‘proving process’ time!

At this moment, the Fourth Heavenly Dao ‘Dark Giant’ felt the world’s profound malice towards it.

Its gaze, unwillingly, fell upon Tyrannical Song and the handsome scoundrel, who had both ‘completed proving the Dao.’

...

At this time, Song Shuhang’s body detached from that ‘Reincarnation Seal’ state.

A portion of the ‘immortal sand’ was sent into the VIP reincarnation channel opened by the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy—unfortunately, because Song Shuhang’s proving process concluded early, the Reincarnation Seal’s ‘VIP cycle Soul Ferrying’ skill was interrupted, so the immortal sand of the Dark Sun, along with some remnants, still existed in the world.

After being pulled out of the Reincarnation Seal, Song Shuhang immediately transferred Sixteen to the main world to keep her away from any potential threats.

Along with the pendants on him and the pendants that had been transferred to Senior White and the others previously, all were moved to the main world.

—Now it was time to enter the ‘Heavenly Dao Rules Core’ process, and he could no longer carry the pendants on him.

Even his life-bound magical treasure could only remain in the dantian during this phase.

Senior White’s Meteor Sword was likewise retracted into the space of the dantian.

Next, Song Shuhang and Senior White began to ascend.

This scene was projected to myriad practitioners in the universe.

It let all cultivators in Myriad Realms + Netherworld Realm know that a new Heavenly Dao had been born!

...

The Fourth Heavenly Dao ‘Dark Giant’ felt unwillingness, but the other party had already completed the ‘proving process’ and was in a mode of ‘about to wield the Will,’ making them no longer susceptible to external interference.

It could only stare at Tyrannical Song, unable to intervene anymore.

After staring at Tyrannical Song for a while... its sleepy, tired brain suddenly had a flash of insight.

It guessed the main reason Tyrannical Song and the handsome scoundrel were so quick.

—It was due to the peculiar ‘Sub-immortal’ state on Tyrannical Song’s body, filled with ‘Heavenly Dao-level information.’

Because his body had already prematurely entered ‘sub-immortalization,’ that is, during the ‘Immortal’ segment, he had actually completed much of the time needed by the ‘proving process.’

That’s why his proving time was so short.

As for the handsome scoundrel next to him, there’s even less to discuss; that fellow is full of tricks.

According to the Fourth Heavenly Dao ‘Dark Giant’s’ memory, this was the third time the handsome scoundrel participated in the ‘proving’ segment.

The speed of proving from that guy, even if twice faster, wouldn’t surprise the Dark Giant at all.

[But luckily...]The only consolation for the Dark Giant was that Tyrannical Song had not completely deciphered his ‘Domination Secret Method.’ The effects of the Domination Secret Method were still settling inside him.

Although the results might be slightly poor, the secret method’s energy was still present.

As long as the secret method took effect, it could buy him time.

Just as it was thus pondering, it suddenly saw Tyrannical Song, ascending, starting a new maneuver—he began forming two formation runes.

Although they were just simple two runes, the spell that they composed was extremely familiar to the ‘Dark Giant.’

It was the Domination Secret Method!

In the ‘Dark Giant’s’ sleepiness-filled brain, a huge question mark popped up.

It wasn’t mistaken, nor hallucinating... it was its Domination Secret Method!

And it was a simplified and improved version!

Why did Tyrannical Song know its Domination Secret Method?

“My Domination Secret Method, when exactly was it leaked?”

On careful thought, from beginning to end, Tyrannical Song seemed to have been guarded against his ‘Domination Secret Method.’

Moreover, he could ‘reverse’ the effects of his Domination Secret Method.

Obviously from the beginning, he might have known of its existence and had been guarding against it.

“Every time I executed the ‘Domination Secret Method,’ I was never detected, and amongst all the predecessors of the Heavenly Dao, no one had ever discovered my Domination Secret Method.”

“I had never had any contact with Tyrannical Song before... wait, a reincarnation of the Confucian Sage?”

Could this guy really be the Confucian Saint?

The very culprit who, during the last battle of the Heavenly Dao, caused him countless sleepless millenniums, ultimately leading to severe sleep deprivation?

If that’s really the case, it might indeed make sense.

But now, what exactly was Tyrannical Song trying to do suddenly using ‘Domination Secret Method’?

Whom did he intend to use it on?

He wasn’t planning to use it on me, was he?

The Dark Giant of the Fourth Heavenly Dao felt a pang of anxiety.

At this moment, Tyrannical Song stretched out his hand and pointed... and the target of the casting was that beautiful good-for-nothing!

“???”

The somewhat befuddled brain of the Dark Giant couldn’t figure out this possibility no matter how hard he thought.

Tyrannical Song actually used the ‘Domination Secret Method,’ cultivated over millions of years, on the beautiful good-for-nothing who was proving his Dao together with him?

What kind of bewildering maneuver was this? It was enough to make one pull their hair out.

And, the beautiful good-for-nothing on the other side didn’t resist and accepted the effects of the ‘Domination Secret Method’ entirely.

But at the same time, he also began operating the ‘reverse Domination Secret Method’ within him.

A moment later.

The beautiful good-for-nothing turned around and reapplied the ‘Domination Secret Method’ on Tyrannical Song.

However, the ‘Domination Secret Method’ energy inside him only consumed half, and the other half remained with him.

As a result, with the ‘Domination Secret Method’ as a connection, the ‘link’ between Tyrannical Song and that beautiful good-for-nothing became even more robust, unbreakable.

Although the two individuals remained ‘distinct entities,’ through various methods they were bundled together, becoming a buy-one-get-one ‘same existence.’

“Buzz!” The Dark Giant finally understood.

Having understood, he felt like someone had stabbed him in the heart, the discomfort unbearable.

The energy of the ‘Domination Secret Method’ that he had painstakingly accumulated over millions of years was just used by these two individuals, making all his millennia of effort others’ wedding garments?

You perform face-to-face NTR on my ‘Domination Secret Method’s power, have you considered my feelings?

Am I just a tool?

“But, it’s not completely over yet!”

“You think you can prove your Dao, but there’s one last hurdle ahead.”

“You are two different entities trying to prove your Dao simultaneously, which is different from all past Heavenly Daos.”

“Even if the ‘proving Dao process’ is completed, but at the last step of accepting the ‘Heavenly Dao Authority’ and ‘Immortal Incarnation,’ if the laws of the Heavenly Dao sense that you are two distinct entities, a rejection is bound to occur.”

“Without passing the last test, you might not succeed!”

“Perhaps, both of you could meet a cruel death!”

The Dark Giant glared fiercely at Tyrannical Song and the beautiful good-for-nothing, who were in the midst of ascension.

In this brief period, he had no mood to cause more troubles.

Whether Tyrannical Song and the beautiful good-for-nothing could overcome the last hurdle was what he and all beings in the myriad realms needed to focus on.

Moreover, as a being who once was a ‘Heavenly Dao’ and had even attempted transcendence, he saw deeper into the act of ‘two individuals proving their Dao together’ carried out by Tyrannical Song and the beautiful good-for-nothing.

“Could they be aiming for transcendence?” Within the depths of the Dark Giant’s heart, such a thought surged.

The more it thought about it, the more it felt this was a possibility.

The authority of the Heavenly Dao was like a rope, firmly tying each generation of the Heavenly Dao, preventing it from transcending, trapping it within the “myriad practitioners in the universe,” unable to fully surpass time, unable to eliminate the obsession and karma of the past.

But what if there were two Heavenly Daos online at the same time?

Could it be that one of them could take over all the ropes, and then let the other Heavenly Dao become a free bird, breaking away from the ropes and the cage?

In the mind of the Dark Giant, two images mysteriously emerged.

One was Tyrannical Song with a smile, extending his right hand—on his right hand, there was a handsome troublemaker with wings on his back, like a bird yet like a butterfly, achieving true great freedom, soaring high.

The other was that handsome troublemaker, making a decision at the last moment. He slightly bent down, untied the rope tied to Tyrannical Song’s feet, tied the rope to himself, and then opened the cage, sending Tyrannical Song away.

[Could it be, I was wrong?]

[Could it be, this is the correct posture for transcendence?]

No, it’s still too early to say!

Whether Tyrannical Song and that handsome troublemaker could withstand the final test, no one could say for sure.

After a brief thought, the Dark Giant, bracing against his fatigue, stretched out his hand and summoned back the remaining “Immortal Sand”!

“The Domination Secret Method was used by the opposition, and moreover, they have become vigilant towards the Domination Secret Method. Although the ‘Domination Secret Method’ still has many loopholes that might be exploited by me... it’s not wise to place too much hope on this.”

“So, what I can do now is to make a final gambit.”

“If you are indeed aiming for ‘transcendence’, then let’s see who can transcend first.”

Whether you transcend before me, or I transcend before you.

Without dominating and remotely influencing the Heavenly Dao, forcefully initiating my transcendence plan is very risky.

But considering that the opposition might be aiming for ‘transcendence’, he couldn’t keep waiting.

What if the opposition transcends and enters a higher dimension, where time and space are no longer ‘restrictions’ for them, who knows what they could achieve?

That would be a level that no one had ever reached before, and even going back to the past and targeting the past him is not impossible.

Perhaps he has the ‘Immortal’ enhancement, and the opposition might not be able to do anything to him. But if the opposition ‘transcends’, that would mean that he, will have no more chances.

So, no matter how great the risks, there is no turning back.

This generation’s Tyrannical Song and handsome troublemaker, from beginning to end, did not give him a chance to choose.

Luckily... at least now, he has an ‘Immortal Daoist’ body in his hands, which can suppress some of the risks associated with the ‘Transcendence Plan’.

However, in using the ‘Immortal Daoist body,’ he still needed to be wary of its condition.

The Domination Secret Method had been cracked, so the state of the Immortal Daoist could not be fully trusted. When using it, he must be careful!

After making up his mind, the Dark Giant left behind a grain of ‘Immortal Sand’ to continue to witness the outcome of Tyrannical Song and the handsome troublemaker.

At the same time, he took the Immortal Daoist and directly vanished without a trace.

What followed was a race.

He, at all costs, was going to make this ‘myriad practitioners in the universe’ become the past—and it must be an irreversible past.

Not like before, when the Immortal Daoist slashed the karma and started the entirety of the myriad practitioners in the universe anew!

Better still, would be to complete all this before Tyrannical Song and the handsome troublemaker transcended.

And then see who transcends first.

...

...

At the end of their ascent.

Song Shuhang and Senior White stood side by side.

As the Dark Giant speculated, Song Shuhang and Senior White were facing their final test.

Normally, to prove immortality through the Heavenly Dao, after completing the ‘proving process,’ it’s supposed to be the stage where one enters the ‘Heavenly Dao Rules Core,’ receives the Heavenly Dao Authority, and forges an immortal body—a step that can be completed lying down.

But Song Shuhang and Senior White were different, they were two separate individuals, proving their Dao simultaneously.

Throughout the ages, this had never happened before!

The laws of the Heavenly Dao may cause repulsion between two entities.

“We have done all we could,” Senior White said, glancing at Song Shuhang.

The two had theoretically completed all the prerequisites for ‘two distinct individuals achieving Dao simultaneously’ through ‘Primordial Spirit Cutting’ + ‘Confucianism Saint’s Innate Secret Technique’ + ‘Domination Secret Method’.

What could be done had been pushed to the limit!

“Hmm,” Song Shuhang nodded.

The final step of whether he and Senior White could ‘transcend’ was approaching.

After striving for so long... this was the moment they had been waiting for.

If successful, the past and the future, whether it be grievances, resentments, or obsessive fixations, would be resolved through either him or Senior White.

If they failed... then at least one of them between him and Senior White must achieve an immortal proofing.

Then, they must suppress ‘Dark Sun’ and the hidden ‘Dark Giant’ of the Fourth Heavenly Dao tightly, preventing it from causing trouble during the Ninth Heavenly Dao reincarnation period!

But...

“We will not fail,” Song Shuhang declared confidently, and failure was not an option.

After succeeding, the next step would be transcendence!

“Time passes so quickly, yet it seems so slow,” Senior White said, no longer suppressing his menacing charm.

At this moment, he was completely relaxed.

The sensation of the world seeming to turn into black and white, with only Senior White in color, descended once again.

But this time... Song Shuhang did not turn into black and white.

Because by now, he had grown enough to stand shoulder to shoulder with Senior White.

“Are you ready?” Senior White asked.

“I have been ready,” Song Shuhang replied.

“Boom~~”

In the perception of Song Shuhang and Senior White, the world shook.

A dimension that only the ‘Heavenly Dao’ could step into opened its gates to them.

And deep within this Heavenly Principle Dimension, the core secret door of the ‘Heavenly Dao Rules’ was also slowly opening!

This phase was something Song Shuhang had once experienced through ‘Daoist Senior,’ although only as a dreamland skill, which felt like looking at flowers through fog, very vague.

This time, he and Senior White were personally experiencing this process!

Both of them took a step forward simultaneously—the distance of the step was exact, taken and landed at the same time.

It was as if they were one entity.

The next moment, Song Shuhang felt himself ‘crossing a dimension.’

This was the huge dimensional gap between the Heavenly Dao and the mundane world.

The Heavenly Dao and those below it were already on two different levels.

Song Shuhang and Senior White took their second step together, fully entering the ‘Heavenly Principle Dimension.’

Once both bodies had completely entered... the expected ‘repulsion’ indeed occurred.

In one Heavenly Dao, one immortal.

The simultaneous entry and Dao achievement of two entities were bound to bring about repulsion.

This repulsion was utterly distinct from what Song Shuhang had imagined.

Too weak, too helpless!

The force of that repulsion, acting on Song Shuhang’s ‘Sub-immortal Body,’ was like a child using the strength needed to nurse, trying to push away a robust adult man.

Is this the final stubbornness of the Heavenly Dao rules?

Chapter 3115: Chapter 3113: ‘My Roommate is the Will of the Heavens

This degree of repulsion couldn’t make Song Shuhang retreat even half a step.

It was too weak!

“It really is a bit... unexpected,” Song Shuhang gently brushed his clothing with his hand.

Throughout the process, not even his hairstyle had changed.

This slight repulsion felt like the laws of the Heavenly Dao lightly pounding on his chest with small fists.

Not only was it not uncomfortable, but it also felt somewhat pleasant?

If it was just this degree of repulsion, then the difficulty of him and Senior White attaining enlightenment as ‘two distinct entities at the same time’ seemed not so great?

It was about the same as the feeling during the 8.5 Ren Daozi’s enlightenment that he remembered.

“It’s because of my full body being semi-immortal,” Senior White, fully awakened, reminded him.

If what was here just now was the ‘Heavenly Dao’ proceeding in the normal course,

the moment they were repelled by this Heavenly Dao-level information, without officially coming into contact with the ‘Heavenly Dao Rules Core’ and condensing an immortal body, they would be directly forced out of the ‘Heavenly Dao Dimension.’

Even their cultivation foundation would be damaged, and their cultivation level directly demoted to that of a mortal!

The repelling power of Heavenly Dao-level rules was no joke; it was genuinely strong.

But, it had met Song Shuhang at this moment.

A full 360-degrees, from inside to outside, completely semi-immortal!

Moreover, the ‘Cultivation Chat Immortal Path’ that Shuhang had last set foot on had also already broken through the level of an Immortal!

An unprecedented body plus an unprecedentedly powerful path to immortality had created this ultimate Song Shuhang.

So ultimate that even the repulsion of the Heavenly Dao rules couldn’t move him.

This was the weight of a major player!

In the end, the Heavenly Dao rules could only turn stubbornness into grievance.

...

And Senior White himself had a similar situation.

Behind him, an ‘Immortal Galaxy’ flickered now and then, easily neutralizing the repulsion of the Heavenly Dao rules.

And after Senior White entered the ‘Heavenly Dao Dimension,’ this ‘Immortal Galaxy’ even plundered the power of the ‘Heavenly Dao Dimension,’ replenishing itself and growing stronger.

It was simply brutally humiliating the Heavenly Dao rules.

“Because of our special nature, we feel that the ‘Heavenly Dao repulsion’ is weak. But in reality, its repulsion is not weak,” Senior White spoke while casually dispelling the continuously incoming ‘Heavenly Dao rules repulsion’ with a gentle swipe.

Imitating Senior White, Song Shuhang dispersed the repulsion pushing against him with a palm strike and said, “So that’s how it is, it was because of us.”

You are strong, but we are stronger!

—If the Heavenly Dao rules had sentient consciousness, they would definitely have been crying bitterly by now!

These two guys were too oppressive.

Completely grinding the ‘Heavenly Dao rules’ into the ground.

...

“Let’s go, since we can handle the repulsion, let’s head directly to the ‘Heavenly Dao Rules’ core, to receive the Heavenly Dao information and authority... We need to hurry,” Senior White said, slightly quickening his pace.

Song Shuhang, intuitively synchronized with Senior White, maintained the same rhythm and pace as Senior White as they stepped forward together.

“Hurry for what, is something about to happen?” Song Shuhang asked.

“Just an intuition,” Senior White nodded: “I feel that during our process of proving our immortality, the Fourth Heavenly Dao lurking behind the scenes might make a move. If we delay... it might cause a bit of trouble.”

Although Senior White referred to it as ‘a bit of trouble,’ the trouble that the looming Dark Giant could trigger must be massive enough to instinctively make Senior White accelerate their pace.

Song Shuhang dared not take it lightly.

Regarding the Fourth Heavenly Dao, he always used the worst-case scenario for his calculations, fearing that he might underestimate the level of disaster of the opponent.

Anyway, regarding the Fourth Heavenly Dao, assume the worst when predicting its actions, and you cannot go wrong.

Senior White and Song Shuhang sped up in sync, rushing toward the channel leading to the core area.

In the meantime, Song Shuhang also tried to record all the action scenes of himself and Senior White after they “entered the Heavenly Dao Dimension.”

These scenes, which contained “Heavenly Dao information,” could not be directly shown to ordinary people.

But once he and Senior White proved their Dao and held authority over Heavenly Dao, they could pixelate or blur some areas of these scenes, downgrading them so that Immortals or Tribulation Transcenders could watch them.

By then, they could show them to the various senior pendants, allowing them to also experience the process of “proving the immortal Heavenly Dao” and learn something from it.

When one attains Dao, even chickens and dogs ascend to heaven—as long as the enlightened one is willing, those connected to him will definitely benefit.

After nearly half an hour...

Song Shuhang and Senior White finally arrived at the entrance to the channel leading to the “Heavenly Dao Rules Core Area.”

Mainly because in the “Heavenly Dao Dimension,” the current state of him and Senior White prevented them from using their spatial powers, forcing them to rely solely on their legs to move around.

Moreover, the journey from the ‘Heavenly Dao Dimension entrance’ to the ‘Heavenly Dao Rules Core Area’ is a process that all Heavenly Daos who proved their immortal status had to go through.

Its name is “Heavenly Dao Patrols All Worlds.”

During this process, Song Shuhang and Senior White experienced what it was like to “step into a different world with each step.”

With each step, they left footprints in one realm corresponding to the myriad practitioners in the universe, leaving behind their own “Heavenly Dao Marks”—including Song Shuhang’s “Overlord World” and the “Dream Realm” overseen by Senior White.

In the end, Song Shuhang and Senior White took a step in the Heavenly Dao Dimension with their fleshly bodies, and their consciousness passed through that “Throne World,” where they left their final footprints, ending the process.

The “Throne World” was precisely that special world into which Song Shuhang’s consciousness, bound to the “bone of eternity,” had been brought by the Sage’s urn.

There, in the Heavenly Dao, marks the last footprint before proving its Dao and ascending the throne.

It is the final stop in the Heavenly Dao’s journey of patrolling the myriad worlds.

After the last step was taken, even the practitioners and ordinary mortals or beings of the myriad worlds felt something instinctively.

Ordinary beings couldn’t help but look up at the sky.

Even those that had never cultivated felt an intuition—at that moment, it seemed that the previously masterless firmament had found its new ruler atop the vacant throne.

From today onwards, two supremely powerful and exalted beings reign from the celestial throne, becoming the sovereigns of the world!

Those ordinary beings who didn’t know Song Shuhang or Senior White didn’t react much; they just looked up at the sky when their instinct kicked in.

But as soon as the intuition ended, they quickly lowered their heads, everyone going about their own business.

However, ordinary people who knew Senior White and Song Shuhang were plunged into intense shock.

On Earth.

You thought my roommate had become the ruler of the universe? Nope, my roommate has become the ruler of over ten thousand universes!

The impact was too strong, causing Gao Moumou’s brain to almost crash.

One was primal chaos, which could evolve into any form of eternity.

Only the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy Seal, Dark Heavenly Dao Seal, and Fat Ball’s seal remained.

At this moment, Reincarnation Blade Fairy finally suggested, “Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, I just communicated with the Reincarnation Seal, and it suggests that your ‘clone’ is the key. Your clone had been nurtured within the ‘Reincarnation Seal’ before — release him, and he can pull our Heavenly Dao seals. If lucky, your clone might pull her as well, aiding you in capturing the Fourth Heavenly Dao Seal. Also, Sixteen’s scabbard might be useful, though we cannot guarantee the results.”

“My clone had once replaced Lady Onion and stayed a while in the Reincarnation Seal, which is really good news,” Song Shuhang felt heartened.

Thus, the only adversary he currently faced was the ‘Heavenly Dao fat ball’!

Meanwhile, information on the ‘Heavenly Dao fat ball’s weaknesses was being gathered by Dark Song and the Heavenly Emperor’s son.

After all, the Heavenly Dao fat ball was an old adversary.

Song Shuhang was familiar with its attack methods through the past experiences with Fat Ball.

This was considered the best kind of opponent.

Song Shuhang clenched his fists together.

Across from him, eight Heavenly Dao marks under the effect of the ‘Heavenly Dao rules’ completed their construction and opened their eyes simultaneously.

Suddenly, an immense pressure descended, pressing down on Song Shuhang and Senior White.

Senior White stepped back... and then, the Heavenly Dao White Seal and the Virtuous Daoist Seal, like being drawn by a magnet, voluntarily followed Senior White and left.

“Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber, come!”

“Song Two clone, appear!”

“Sage Eye Golden Core system, activate!”

Song Shuhang immediately sprang into action.

The Song Two clone was summoned — it had experienced nurturing in the ‘Reincarnation Seal,’ so it could exist within this ‘Heavenly Dao dimension.’

Upon appearing, it first confronted the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy Seal, and both sides produced a kind of resonance.

The Song Two clone was responsible for pulling the ‘Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy Seal,’ ideally to drag the Reincarnation Fairy Seal along and head towards the Fourth Heavenly Dao.

If that failed... Song Shuhang would have to face both Fat Ball and the Dark Giant simultaneously.

The Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber affectionately rubbed against Song Shuhang, charging toward Heavenly Dao Father Goudan.

“Expert’s Appraisal!” the Confucian Saint Eye Golden Core was activated, locking onto the Three-Eyed Heavenly Dao Seal and Daozi’s Seal.

Two Gaze of Maternal Love settled respectively on Daozi’s Seal and the Three-Eyed Seal, holding them in place.

Finally.

Only the Fat Ball Heavenly Dao and the temporarily unbound Dark Giant advanced toward Song Shuhang!

Boom~

The core area of the Heavenly Dao Rules transformed into a boundless starry sky, constructing a battlefield for the Heavenly Dao battle.

The Fat Ball Heavenly Dao Seal directly transformed into a battle fortress, colossal and overwhelming, the familiar cannon barrels locking onto Shuhang, numerous and large.

The Dark Giant Seal was even more exaggerated; its form dispersed, transforming into thousands of stars.

Each star emitted an ancient aura from the primordial times... Then, those thousands of stars transformed into meteors, trailing long tails of fire, smashing toward Song Shuhang with an apocalyptic force.

Although these stars were only the size of the moon, the light they emitted was more blinding than the sun.

But this was all just superficial... The most terrifying aspect was the eternal power contained within them.

For Song Shuhang, who was still at the Sub-immortal level, these star attacks were capable of causing harm.

Facing the simultaneously roaring and menacing Fat Ball and Dark Giant...

Song Shuhang did not panic.

Having experienced great trials and tribulations, he was not easily shaken anymore.

His eyes bore a calm that was terrifying.

Then, he reached out and grabbed a saber scabbard.

A thousand tiny hands formed from Sub-immortal level hair grasped the scabbard.

“Not long ago, I realized something... There is still love in this world,” Song Shuhang said, seemingly out of nowhere.

The next moment.

A vast amount of cheap love transformed into a light brighter than the ‘stars,’ and in an instant, a billion ‘Saber-Nurturing Techniques’ fell upon the scabbard.

The scabbard was almost stripped bare.

Across from him, the array of menacing stars surprisingly braked sharply, stiffening for a few breaths.

The Fat Ball Seal, originally synchronized in attack, arrived first instead.

Millions of barrages and beams of attack light roared towards Song Shuhang.

“Universe Hiding Sleeve!” Song Shuhang swung his arm.

His sleeve transformed into a giant robe, sweeping all of Fat Ball’s attacks inside in one breath.

Boom~

But as soon as they were collected, the Universe Hiding Sleeve exploded, turning Song Shuhang’s right arm into blackened char.

Pits were blasted into the Sub-immortal arm.

But soon, it regained its elasticity.

“The damage is about what I estimated; a Sub-immortal body can hold it,” Song Shuhang said softly.

As long as he could hold on, then next, he could demonstrate to the ‘Fat Ball Heavenly Dao Seal’ his strongest ability from the ‘Cultivation Chat Immortal Path’ — the Enhanced Version.

“Karma Blade•Cultivation Chat Enhanced Version,” Song Shuhang’s right hand mimed gripping, and a projection emerged from Sixteen’s scabbard.

It was the shadow of a saber.

Song Shuhang drew the saber.

The ‘Cultivation Chat Immortal Path’ operated at full power!

The karmic debts of myriad creatures across the universe began loading!

The virtuous lamia materialized, constructing defenses for Song Shuhang while enhancing the ‘Virtuous Network’ signal.

In the main world.

Song Shuhang’s Kindness Corpse, Evil Corpse, and Self-Corpse broke out of the ‘small black room’ and stepped into the main world.

In the Netherworld Realm, Dark Song opened her eyes, gathering the karmas of the Netherworld Realm.

Ultimate Tyrannical Song, at this moment, fully unleashed his power!

Cultivation Chat Immortal Path, 200% power!

A massive oppressive force exploded from Song Shuhang as he assumed the sword-drawing stance!

From the scabbard, the Illusion Blade began to unsheathe.

As this sword-drawing action took place, the starry sky beneath everyone’s feet, formed by the ‘laws of the Heavenly Dao,’ actually began to fade!

The picturesque starry sky washed away its colors, turning into a stark white, becoming a pure white space.

Even the marks of the Dark Giant, the fat ball of the Heavenly Dao, and the marks of the past Heavenly Dao were affected, their bodies beginning to turn white.

In this nearly pure white space, only Song Shuhang retained his original colors.

And the oppressive force emanating from him seemed to materialize, turning into a black aura that dominated the entire area!

From a starry sky fading to pure white, then from pure white dyed with Tyrannical Song’s black—through this process, the entire starry world was dominated by Tyrannical Song!

This is the power of the ‘Cultivation Chat Immortal Path,’ painstakingly condensed by Song Shuhang and the senior powerhouses supporting him.

An unprecedented path to immortality, power unprecedented!

The Illusion Blade in Tyrannical Song’s hands finally unsheathed—a moment that seemed like an instant but, under the effect of Song Shuhang’s materialized oppressive force, felt like a century!

The moment the blade was drawn, what was originally an illusionary blade edge condensed into reality, transforming into the ‘Dao Artifact•Reincarnation Blade’—this was the effect of the Karma Blade “Flower Rule.”

The Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy and the Reincarnation Blade Fairy were also among the ones from whom Song Shuhang drew karma.

Their power, through Sixteen’s saber scabbard, temporarily materialized this illusionary projection blade into a true Dao artifact blade.

Not just the Reincarnation Blade Fairy and the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy, but also Father Goudan, Senior Three-Eyed, Senior White two, the Immortal Daoist, and many other seniors, creatures of the main world, demons of the Netherworld Realm—all karmic links were gathered, transformed into this single strike in Tyrannical Song’s hand.

All the power plus Song Shuhang’s immortal power left a deep blue trail as the blade moved.

Slash!

The ‘Karma Blade•Cultivation Chat Immortal Version’ swept toward the mark of the Heavenly Dao fat ball.

Faced with this oppressive threat, the Heavenly Dao fat ball mark, in an instant, unleashed incalculable firepower.

The brilliant and dazzling firepower covered the skies, its special effect +100.

In comparison, Song Shuhang’s ‘Karma Blade’ seemed pitifully small.

Yet, this seemingly tiny blade light, when slashing through that endless firepower, cut through it as easily as if slicing through vegetables, effortlessly splitting all the firepower.

The blade light locked onto the Heavenly Dao fat ball mark.

Power of karma, power of virtue, power of reincarnation were all layered locking... making it impossible for the Heavenly Dao fat ball mark to evade.

No matter how it tried to dodge, no matter how it tried to defend, this strike, the moment it was made, had already determined the outcome.

It could only resist forcefully!

Shriek–

The nearly ten thousand layers of defenses on the Heavenly Dao fat ball were all split open by this strike!

Immediately afterward, its body, as vast as the stars, was mercilessly cut in two by the blade light.

And from this clean cut as the source, the massive body of the Heavenly Dao fat ball began to collapse.

Even its powerful ‘self-healing ability’ was suppressed.

The speed of self-healing couldn’t keep up with the rate of bodily collapse.

Moments later, the mark of the Heavenly Dao fat ball was destroyed into fragments.

Marks of the Heavenly Dao, possessing indestructible Dao traces and attack powers nearly of the Heavenly Dao itself... but they themselves are not indestructible and eternal.

After all, if the marks were indestructible, then Song Shuhang and Senior White wouldn’t need to challenge it; they could just surrender directly.

“Is it over?” asked the Reincarnation Blade Fairy, who, with the ‘power of karma’ condensed into a physical form, spoke out.

As the vessel for this strike, the Reincarnation Blade Fairy experienced the power of this strike from a ‘first-hand’ perspective.

But as soon as the Reincarnation Blade Fairy finished speaking,

across from her, the shattered fragments of the Heavenly Dao fat ball’s seal began to resurrect and condensed into a smaller version of the fat ball!

Aside from being somewhat smaller in size, the Heavenly Dao fat ball’s seal had once again regained its bouncing ability.

This formidable regenerative ability, clearly lacking an ‘Immortal Physique,’ yet nearly indestructible, was truly the nightmare of all cultivators!

“It still isn’t dead?” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy was a bit surprised. This Heavenly Dao fat ball had some tricks up its sleeve!

However, after collapsing once, the body of the Heavenly Dao fat ball had significantly reduced in size.

So, its ‘resurrection’ definitely had a limit.

“Then let’s strike it one more time!” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy prepared herself, attempting to once again wield the ‘Karma Blade’ with Song Shuhang.

But Song Shuhang, holding the saber hilt, slowly sheathed his saber.

“It’s already over,” Song Shuhang said softly, “It’s already dead.”

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy was puzzled: “???”

Whoosh—next to the Heavenly Dao fat ball, another ‘blade light’ suddenly appeared.

This blade light, as if transcending karma and space, slashed from the past to the future!

The blade fell.

The hardly resurrected ‘Heavenly Dao fat ball’s seal’ was once again cleaved in two and shattered at the cut inflicted by the blade.

“Is this... the strike you just delivered?” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy asked.

As she spoke, the mark of the Heavenly Dao fat ball revived once more, transforming into an even smaller Heavenly Dao fat ball’s seal.

But as soon as its form was restored, the ‘blade light’ appeared once again, slashing at it.

No matter how many times it recovered... the outcome was always the same!

After Song Shuhang executed that note of the ‘Karma Blade•Cultivation Chat Version’ and in the moment he struck, that strike had already completely annihilated the ‘Heavenly Dao fat ball’s seal’ before him.

From the time the blade was drawn to the future, the ‘Heavenly Dao fat ball’s seal’ had already perished under that single strike!

The moment Song Shuhang sheathed his saber, the Heavenly Dao fat ball’s seal was finished.

The scenes of the ‘Heavenly Dao fat ball’s seal’ continuously resurrecting and being slaughtered before their eyes... were, in fact, just ‘projections of events that had already transpired’.

The real ‘Heavenly Dao fat ball’s seal’ had already died in the ‘past’ a few moments ago.

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy quickly grasped the causality of the scene before her eyes and understood.

“Your path to immortality... is really terrifying. This enormous computing ability is not something a non-proven person can achieve. You are still a step away from proving your Dao,” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy said.

“I have a Heavenly Axiom-level calculation cheat,” Song Shuhang coolly replied.

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy: “!!!”

You cheater!

“Next, the Dark Heavenly Dao Seal,” Song Shuhang turned around and looked toward the Dark Heavenly Dao giant that had transformed into thousands of stars.

At the same time, he glanced at the Song Two he had dispatched to seduce the ‘Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy Mark.’

Song Two, successful halfway!

The Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy Mark wasn’t enticed to join his ranks.

But because of the resonance with Song Two, the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy Mark had become a bit more ‘flexible.’

This bit of flexibility was just enough for her to lock her ‘Hate Value’ onto the Fourth Heavenly Dao.

Her gaze fixed onto the Fourth Heavenly Dao Seal became sharp.

Not because he underestimated the attack power of the Dark Heavenly Dao.

And what's interesting is, the Fourth Heavenly Dao Seal under the effect of the 'laws of the Heavenly Dao' should be in an 'ally' state with the Reincarnation Heavenly Dao Fairy, and it wouldn't strike at an 'ally' nor would it guard against an 'ally's' attack.

You cannot attack me, yet I can mercilessly stab you in the back!

The Heavenly Dao Fairy leaped up directly, and her body transformed into a giant blade that could Create of Heaven and Earth—this was the true Star-cutting Saber, a full 12345 kilometers in length!

What are forty-meter great sabers or five-hundred-meter machetes in the face of the giant blade transformed by the Heavenly Dao Fairy? They're laughably weak!

When Song Shuhang witnessed this, his eyes lit up.

—Because, he could tell that the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy's strike wasn't any sort of 'innate ability,' but rather a saber technique!

Under the effect of Heavenly Dao Level Computational Ability + the resonating empowerment from Song Two and the Heavenly Dao Fairy, Song Shuhang began to attempt to analyze this saber technique.

Becoming the blade with one's body, transforming into the Star-cutting Saber!

Song Shuhang's innate skill for saber techniques was truly of a Super Rule Level, all thanks to the exchange for the innate inability to use sword techniques!

Under his analysis, he actually managed to obtain some understanding of the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy's technique.

Slash!

The 12345-kilometer-long Giant Blade transformed by the Fifth Heavenly Dao Reincarnation Fairy cut horizontally, slashed vertically, and performed Tornado Slashes!

A blade this size, larger than the diameter of Earth, its sweeping saber qi and intent were enough to slice a planet the size of Earth like a watermelon, smashing it to pieces.

And among the thousands of stars formed by the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao, the average size was only that of the moon.

Facing the terrifying slash from the giant blade, and especially in the 'ally unguarded' mode, they were sliced up like fruits in a game!

Out of the thousands of stars, only a few managed to break through the assault of the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy's 12345-kilometer blade and hurtle towards Song Shuhang.

Truly appealing.

Unless all the 'stars' were extinguished in one breath, it could keep producing more.

While she was speaking, from behind the stars formed by the Dark Heavenly Dao Seal, a huge fist erupted from a 'spatial gate,' wildly pounding the stars!

This classic method of attack was characteristic of the Confucian system.

Turning to look, Song Shuhang saw that the left eye socket of 'Heavenly Dao • Daozi Seal' had been scooped out... and replaced with a 'Sage Eye Golden Core.'

Thus, the Daozi's Mark, with its new eye, didn't hesitate to attack its own 'ally,' the Fourth Heavenly Dao Seal!

This was a betrayal between two allies!

Meanwhile, the Dark Heavenly Dao Seal, completely disregarding the betrayal of its ally, was solely focused on bombarding Tyrannical Song with incessant attacks!

Attacking my teammates, protecting my enemies.

Moreover, since ‘Heavenly Dao Mark’ is a materialized pure energy, Shuhang simply had no way to force the ‘Sage Eye Golden Core’ into it unless it wished so.

It sounds unbelievable, but in fact, it was Daozi’s Heavenly Dao Mark itself that installed the ‘Sage Eye Golden Core’ into its eye socket!

Daozi’s Mark might have sensed the aura of its teacher within the ‘Sage Eye Golden Core’ and then instinctively plucked out its own eyeball to fit in the ‘Sage Eye Golden Core’—all to protect its teacher’s possession.

Upon acquiring its teacher the Saint’s eyes, Daozi’s Mark was slightly ‘activated’ and immediately turned traitor!

To Daoist Senior, the teacher is more important than the Heavenly Dao.

The Fourth Heavenly Dao Seal became Daozi’s ‘First Hatred’ target, opening a spatial passage and bombarding it with a flurry of knowledge-charged punches!

In the vacuum, the stars manifested by the Fourth Heavenly Dao kept exploding and being severed.

This is too hard...

What should have been an 8 vs. 2 situation had turned into a one-on-three against the ‘Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao Mark’.

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy in Tyrannical Song’s hands let out a chicken-like joyous laugh.

With the addition of Daoist Senior’s ‘mark,’ the stars formed by the Fourth Heavenly Dao Seal were being destroyed at a much faster pace.

It was like a relentless ‘monster-spawner,’ frantically generating massive stars.

The body of the phoenix expanded boundlessly, eventually growing to match the size of starry forms.

It not only had to defend but also had to use all its energy to ‘increase the number of stars,’ turning into a monster-spawning machine without any feelings!

Apart from ruthlessly spawning monsters to maintain the continuously blasted stars, it couldn’t do anything else.

Even without consciousness, the three-eyed young man’s mark still treated the ‘Sage Eye Golden Core’ with caution, controlling the power of its techniques to not harm the Sage Eye Golden Core.”

But this is only because the ‘Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao Mark’ has become the ‘First Hatred’ target of the other Heavenly Dao Marks, temporarily surpassing Song Shuhang, the ‘Second Hatred’ target.

The relationship between Song Shuhang and the other Heavenly Dao Marks hasn’t shifted from ‘hostile’ to ‘allied’.

Even the Daozi’s Mark, which had integrated the ‘Sage Eye Golden Core,’ at best, has only become ‘neutral.’

Therefore... now is not the time to directly take out the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao Mark.

Once the Fourth Heavenly Dao Mark is destroyed, and we lose this ‘hatred target,’ the rest of the Heavenly Dao Marks will once again fix their ‘hatred target’ on Song Shuhang!

“That makes sense,” Senior White instantly understood Song Shuhang’s point.

“Although it feels a bit ruthless, it indeed is the most correct choice,” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy comprehended, “Since that’s the case, while the various ‘Heavenly Dao Marks’ are stabbing the Fourth Heavenly Dao Mark in the back, let’s backstab them first!”

A backstab of a backstab.

“So, which Heavenly Dao Mark shall we pick as our first target?” Song Shuhang asked.

Currently, the fat ball Heavenly Dao, Heavenly Dao White, and Daoist Priest Virtue’s Heavenly Dao Marks had been dealt with.

The ones left to backstab are the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy Mark, Heavenly Dao Goudan Father’s Mark, Daozi’s Mark, and the spectating Three-Eyed Youth’s Heavenly Dao Mark.

“How about we start with the weakest in attack power? Retain those Heavenly Dao Marks with strong attack power so that we can maximize their attack power to suppress the Fourth Heavenly Dao’s stars?” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy suggested.

“Then, let’s take out the three-eyed Heavenly Dao Mark first!” Song Shuhang’s eyes, filled with ill intent, looked toward the second Heavenly Dao Mark that was idly playing with the ‘Sage Eye Golden Core.’

The Second Heavenly Dao had not participated in the act of ‘suppressing the Dark Heavenly Dao Stars’ and, being unsociable, was isolated from the rest.

Since it could not contribute to the suppression of the Fourth Heavenly Dao Stars, it might as well be blasted away first!

“Agreed,” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy said—as long as her family’s Heavenly Dao Mark isn’t the first one to be blasted away, that’s fine.

Better yet, if her family’s Heavenly Dao Mark could remain after the ‘Dark Heavenly Dao Mark’ is taken out.

That way, she would feel a little better.

“I also think it’s feasible,” Senior White agreed, nodding his head.

Since Senior White has also chosen to agree, it means that this choice is more than 90% likely to be the ‘best option,’ with the remaining 10% being a ‘decent choice.’

“Goudan’s Father and Senior Three Eyes have no objections either. They agree that we should blast away the three-eyed youth’s mark first. After speculation, Daoist Senior also feels this plan is most appropriate,” Song Shuhang added.

In order to keep the ‘Field Support Team’ seniors informed and ready to offer advice, Song Shuhang had been using the ‘path to immortality’ to photograph the battle situation and post it to his circle of friends, limiting viewing permissions to the support team.

This way, though they were on the sidelines, each powerful expert could keep abreast of the situation at all times and promptly provide Song Shuhang with the most useful advice.

Tyrannical Song was never fighting alone!

“Well then, let’s discuss the plan to take out the three-eyed Heavenly Dao Mark. My Reinforced ‘Karmic Saber Technique’ should still be usable for about two more times... As for the three corpses in the main world, each one can currently take on a part of karma for me,” Song Shuhang spoke out. “If we don’t consider the ‘karma’s’ impact on the final stage of proving his pseudo-immortal body, then my main body can still strike one more time as the carrier.”

The method Senior White mentioned was the ‘Combined Magical Treasure’ left by the Wielder of the Will White, a successor of near-transcendence. It was the contingency plan of the Wielder of the Will White, who was one step away from transcendence.

Previously, it was with this set of ‘Combined Magical Treasures’ that Senior White, using the Heavenly Dao White Seal, blasted away the Daoist Priest Virtue’s Mark.

“I need your Sub-immortal State, and the 10000 kilometers Giant Blade form you’re currently using can also come in handy,” Senior White brought out the ‘Combined Magical Treasure.’

This magical treasure set, refined by the nearly transcendent Wielder of the Will White himself, could withstand the pressure from the Heavenly Principle Dimension.

Then, Senior White gently clapped his hands.

The Combined Magical Treasure started assembling and transforming.

The scene was cool.

Shortly, the Combined Magical Treasure transformed into a ‘cannon’ shape.

However, this cannon didn’t just have one barrel, but rather, like a Gatling Gun, it had many barrels grouped together in a terrifying stance.

When Song Shuhang saw this contraption, he subconsciously felt a chill in his heart.

—Even when facing the countless barrels of the battle fortress form of Fat Ball Heavenly Dao, Song Shuhang had never felt such a chill.

This chilling feeling stemmed from an ‘inhumane’ intuition.

His Heavenly Axiom-level intuition told him that the ‘Gatling Gun’ Senior White had invoked might be very ‘expensive’ in terms of ‘people’.

At this point in the battle, even without Song Shuhang, the other Heavenly Dao Marks could still firmly suppress the ‘Dark Heavenly Dao Stars,’ keeping them in a state of ‘exhausted defense’ without the strength to counterattack.

So Song Shuhang could completely step away for a moment.

Song Shuhang was, after all, a Full Body Semi-Immortal plus his path to immortality had been ‘strengthened in the sub-ascension-to-Heaven’s-Will phase.’

At the Sub-immortal Level, he was almost indestructible.

You could say that at this moment, Song Shuhang was indeed much more effective than a ‘Heavenly Dao Mark.’

Moreover, he was at a level where he could be recycled and reused.

Song Shuhang gritted his teeth, closed his eyes, and offered no resistance.

And Tyrannical Song, stuffed into a strange magical treasure.

Chapter 3121: Chapter 3119: As a Senior, I Can’t Let You Bear the Hardships Alone!
 

Song Shuhang’s method of calculation was actually quite modest.

A senior should act like one.

If possible, Senior White hoped he could shoulder more of the hardships.

Taking care of juniors was also a fine tradition among the fellow friends of the Nine Provinces Number One Group.

He barely passed the certification of the magical treasure.

The price was a slightly reduced conversion rate.

After being drained of energy in an instant... thanks to the power of the “undying fat whale golden core” and the sub-immortal physique, plus the constant replenishment from “Cultivation Chat Path,”

As soon as he was drained, Song Shuhang’s mental energy would quickly recover.

From the Gatling magical treasure’s barrels, the compassionate Tyrannical Song bullets were fired continuously.

Since all the Heavenly Dao Marks were clustered together anyway, wouldn’t it be perfect to wipe them all out in one fell swoop?

Chapter 3122: Chapter 3120: Zhu Sheng’s Peak

Chapter 3123: Chapter 3121: Some things still need to be shared with an intimate friend

The virtuous lamia transformed into the ‘Pillow of Leather’.

Followed by the Heavenly Emperor’s Child + Stellar Destruction Virus’s ‘Emperor Destroying Pillar’.

And then the ‘Stardragon Pillar’—empowered by Dao Artifact Long-Eyed Planet Power + Lady Long Luo Power—this pillar, if brought to the Black Dragon World, undoubtedly wouldn’t be weaker than a ‘Heavenly Dao Pillar’.

Using the Stardragon Pillar, Pillow of Leather, and Emperor Destroying Pillar as the main, and Kun King Pillar, Overlord God Pillar, and Virtual Sun Pillar as auxiliary, the combined effect should also match one and a half ‘Heavenly Dao Pillars’.

As each Heavenly Dao Pillar, Dao Artifact Pillar, and Pillar of Longevity were loaded into the Gatling Gun, Song Shuhang considered thoughtfully.

[Perhaps, this is the true way to unlock my ‘Overlord God Pillar’!]

My Overlord God Pillars, hammering people one by one, is too inefficient and frankly a waste.

Just like the ‘Combined Magical Treasure,’ I should also be able to assemble my Overlord God Pillars into Senior White’s ‘Gatling Gun’ mode.

Then, I’ll load in the Overlord God Pillars, firing Heavenly Dao Pillars, Pillars of Longevity, heavenly tribulation pillars... who could withstand that?

Even the active Dark Giant of the current main world’s Fourth Heavenly Dao would have to retreat in the face of such an attack!

“With so many pillars, even in their reduced form, they’re still massive... Along with you and Fellow Daoist White, can the magical treasure accommodate them?” asked the Reincarnation Blade Fairy at that moment.

She would be responsible for operating the magical treasure on behalf of Song Shuhang and Fellow Daoist White in a while.

“Don’t worry... the ‘ammo chamber’ of the magical treasure actually contains vastness within tininess, it may look small, but its internal space is huge!” Senior White patted the magical treasure.

Not to mention fitting him and Shuhang, even if they added ten more people, it wouldn’t feel cramped.

“Alright, then let’s blow up all the ‘Heavenly Dao Marks’ in one breath,” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy transformed into her human form.

Just the thought of personally blowing up the four Heavenly Dao Marks later made her a bit excited.

Although she was a Dao artifact, she had never done something so thrilling in her lifetime.

Especially since one of her own Heavenly Dao Marks would also be blown up by her.

Chapter 3124: Chapter 3122: The Time for Proving the Dao Has Arrived
 

Song Shuhang shrank the “Overlord God Pillars” one by one and handed them to Senior White.

Senior White, after taking the “Overlord God Pillars,” then loaded them into the ammunition space.

After all the “Overlord God Pillars” were loaded, Song Shuhang turned his head to look at the illusory Reincarnation Blade Fairy and said, “Fairy, can you hold on?”

“Of course I can, how could I possibly drop offline at such a thrilling moment?” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy replied confidently. “However, if you could speed things up a bit, it would be safer.”

She hoped to see the four Heavenly Dao Marks blasted apart before her mental energy was completely depleted, instead of just after firing, running out of energy.

“Roger that, the next part... is up to you, Fairy,” Song Shuhang said, then with a handsome diving pose, he leaped high into the air towards the ammunition space.

But just as his body reached its highest point, a pair of slender arms suddenly stretched out and gently held him.

Song Shuhang: “???”

It was the virtuous lamia...

The virtuous lamia suddenly appeared, grabbing Song Shuhang and then diving in a perfect scoring dive into the ammunition space.

With both Fairy Creation and black-skinned Soft Feather absent today, she had to take on the positive energy roles of three people.

When Shuhang began to show his handsome side, she had to triple her effort to make Shuhang even more handsome.

Whoosh~

As she fell into the ammunition space, the light of virtue from the virtuous lamia also depicted the imagery of ‘entering water’.

The light of virtue spread out, making a sound like splashing water.

Reincarnation Blade Fairy was stunned for a moment, but she quickly reacted. She stretched out her hand and pushed Song Shuhang, Senior White, the virtuous lamia + all the “Overlord God Pillars” into the Gatling Gun magical treasure.

Then, mimicking Senior White’s previous operation, she aimed the cannon at the faraway fiercely contested four Great Heavenly Dao Marks and locked onto them.

The confrontation between the four Great Heavenly Dao Marks had reached a white-hot stage.

The Heavenly Dao Marks fought from one end of the starry sky to the other, engraving the stars with Dao Traces, constantly blowing up stars, eroding laws, and almost bursting the starry sky.

The laws of the Heavenly Dao, when manifesting the eight Great Heavenly Dao Marks, definitely didn’t anticipate a moment when the Heavenly Dao Marks would turn on each other.

Its last bit of defiance shivered at the cunning ploys of Tyrannical Song and White.

“Good, locked on successfully, ammunition sufficient, next...four Heavenly Dao Marks in one breath!” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy felt a long-missing sense of ‘nervousness.’

Just as she locked onto all four Great Heavenly Dao Marks, suddenly, the battling Daozi’s Mark, the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy’s Mark, and Goudan’s Father’s Mark all turned their heads and looked in her direction.

The Heavenly Dao Marks, even if just acting on instinct, still had sharp senses toward danger—previously, when the Three-Eyed Heavenly Dao Seal was locked on by firepower, it also reacted immediately.

However, its reaction was to protect the ‘Sage Eye Golden Core’ with its body.

If not for protecting the ‘Sage Eye Golden Core’, the bombardment fired by Senior White using Song Shuhang as ammunition would not have succeeded in easily blowing up the Three-Eyed Heavenly Dao Seal.

Now, as the four Great Heavenly Dao Marks were locked on, they too sensed the crisis, and subconsciously looked towards the Reincarnation Blade Fairy.

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy only felt four heavy pressures bearing down on her.

Disaster!

If the four Great Heavenly Dao attacked her at the same time...

Just as this thought flashed through her mind, among the four Great Heavenly Dao Marks, Daozi’s Mark suddenly exploded, his spatial gate opening two more doors, encompassing both Goudan’s Father’s Mark and the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy’s Mark.

He was attempting to entangle the other two Great Heavenly Dao Marks to create an opportunity for the Reincarnation Blade Fairy.

Even as a Heavenly Dao Mark, Daoist Senior was still the strongest tool in the Heavenly Dao!

As Daozi Senior took action decisively, an anomaly almost simultaneously occurred on the side of Goudan’s Father’s Mark—it suddenly transformed into a real dragon, fully powering up to release the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber, letting it break away from the battle.

Following that, its dragon body moved, enveloping the other three major Heavenly Dao Marks.

The case with the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy was even more straightforward—since the Reincarnation Blade Fairy was her primordial treasure, originating from the same root as her. She also chose to shield the Reincarnation Blade Fairy.

“Turning the one qi into the three pure ones, one strike turning into three blades.” The Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy’s blades flickered, and with one split into three, she chopped towards the three major Heavenly Dao Marks.

Not to mention the Dark Heaven, which had always been the target of the three great Heavenly Dao Marks’ attacks, and was too tired to defend itself, passively enduring strikes without any chance to counterattack.

The four major Heavenly Dao Marks, attacking each other, entangling each other, dragging each other down, no one giving the others a chance to “escape.”

Seeing this, the Reincarnation Blade Fairy did not hesitate to trigger the attack of the ‘Combined Magical Treasure.’

Da da da—Boom boom boom—Dong dong dong—Awoo awoo awoo—

For a moment, various sounds erupted at the “mouth of the cannon”... the sounds emitted by different types of ammunition were also distinct.

The voices from the Heavenly Dao Pillar, Tyrannical Song, and Senior White, each had their unique traits.

The Gatling gun’s muzzle burst into a palpitating blue light.

An endless barrage of ammunition poured onto the four great Heavenly Dao Marks...

When there was originally only Tyrannical Song’s ‘magazine’, the number of rounds fired from the muzzle was about one in a thousand.

But with so many ammunition sources loaded, the quantity of ammunition poured out started at at least thirty thousand rounds a minute.

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy felt her adrenaline surge.

This sensation was addictive!

Holding this artifact, firing unrivaled firepower, tearing apart any target, such thrill accelerated the heartbeat of the Reincarnation Blade Fairy.

She felt herself getting hooked on this feeling.

Da da da da da—

After nearly two minutes of relentless bombing, the merciless Tyrannical Song bullet, White bullet, and Overlord God Pillar bullet, conducted a saturation coverage strike on the battle area of the four great Heavenly Dao Marks.

The magical cannon stopped rotating, the gunfire died down, and smoke rose from the muzzle.

“Is it over?” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy said, feeling somewhat reluctant.

If possible, she truly wished to experience this thrill a few more times!

Her form gradually started to fade.

As she was about to dissipate, her gaze turned towards the area of the four great Heavenly Dao Marks.

“All annihilated, it’s done,” declared the Reincarnation Blade Fairy, satisfied.

The four great Heavenly Dao Marks had all turned into fragments, and her corresponding Fifth Heavenly Dao Mark was no exception.

“Mission complete, Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, remember to call me next time there’s such an opportunity,” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy said with reluctance.

Her form dissipated.

The Combined Magical Treasure also reached its limit, automatically disassembled, and turned into thirty-three artifact spirit fairies, supporting Song Shuhang and Senior White.

Under the era-changing firepower, the last stubbornness of the Heavenly Dao was mercilessly shredded.

From this moment, in the Myriad Realms, no power or principle could prevent Song Shuhang and Senior White from proving their Dao together!

“Senior White, the time to prove the Dao has arrived,” Song Shuhang struggled to sit up, showing a brilliant smile.

Chapter 3125: Chapter 3123 Senior White: Don’t you have any guard against me at all?
 

Having been drained once before, Song Shuhang developed an immunity to “becoming a power source,” so his recovery was much faster than last time.

—This ability was probably an upgraded version of his “pain endurance.”

Senior White opened his eyes and smiled, “Ah, finally... we’ve reached this step. From now on, nothing can obstruct our path to enlightenment.”

He spoke a cool line, but Senior White was so weak that he couldn’t even move a finger and could only lie there, resting for a while.

Unlike Song Shuhang, he didn’t have the “undying fat whale golden core” or a body that was fully semi-immortal, nor did he possess the bug-level innate skill of “pain endurance.”

“Are you happy?” Song Shuhang asked.

He wasn’t asking if Senior White was “happy about proving his Dao,” but rather if he “enjoyed the process.”

“Mm, it was somewhat interesting. But I doubt I’ll experience it a second time,” Senior White replied, using the back of his hand to shield his eyes from the blinding light spreading from the immortal root source.

“Me neither,” Song Shuhang nodded in agreement.

The sensation of becoming a power source, with even the marrow feeling like it was being drained, was more troubling than the sprint to the college entrance exams back in the day.

With that, Song Shuhang’s gaze fell upon the fragments of the four great Heavenly Dao Seal lying not so far away.

The virtuous lamia received the signal, emerging behind Song Shuhang with a delighted expression.

Then, with graceful movements, she floated over, gathering the freshly shattered fragments of the four great Heavenly Dao Seal and the residual energy, for Song Shuhang to use shortly in condensing the “Heavenly Dao Pillar.”

Heavenly Dao Pillar•Black Pillar.

Heavenly Dao Pillar•Dragon Column.

Heavenly Dao Pillar•Dao Pillar.

And the pillar formed by the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy.

This was quite impolite.

Next time he went to the Su Clan’s Ancestor Star, he would ask the Reincarnation Fairy.

For now, for the sake of symmetry in naming... perhaps call it Heavenly Dao Pillar•Reincarnation Pillar?

After collecting all eight Heavenly Dao Pillars, Song Shuhang turned towards Senior White, “Are you rested? Senior White?”
