Song Shuhang stepped forward, reaching out to help Senior White up.

Not far away, the virtuous lamia, who was swimming joyously in the Heavenly Dao starry sky, saw this and leisurely flew back, perching behind Song Shuhang, on top of his head.

—Becoming Song Shuhang’s “Virtuous Manifestation” was also an accident.

The “karmic” connection between Fairy @#%× and Song Shuhang originated from Cheng Lin.

After becoming Song Shuhang’s “body of virtue,” she never imagined that in just a brief year, Song Shuhang would advance by leaps and bounds, proving his Dao to immortality.

She wouldn’t have even dared to entertain such a thought, and the previous her would not have even conceived such a notion.

Yet, incredibly, it had become a reality.

During the subsequent process of enlightenment, she might even benefit more than Song Shuhang’s “Three Corpses Avatar.”

Manifestations and clones, during the original body’s proof of the Dao, were only indirect beneficiaries.

Some manifestations and clones would even be reclaimed during the “Heavenly Dao enlightenment” phase, merging back with the original body and returning to wholeness.

But she was different, as a “body of virtue,” she was a part of the original body itself.

Similar to the magnificent manifestation of light of virtue of the undying Daoist Priest Virtue, Fairy @#%× would also be bathed in immortal light when the time came.

To tell the truth, even as Song Shuhang and Senior White formally stepped into the “Heavenly Dao Rules Core Area” to undertake the final step of proving their Dao, the virtuous lamia still felt as if she were dreaming.

As if all of this had an unrealistic, dreamlike quality.

...

...

Heavenly Dao Rules Core Area.

After the last defiance was shattered, the Heavenly Dao rules ceased to resist Song Shuhang and Senior White, opening up completely to the two of them.

Song Shuhang and Senior White, maintaining 100% synchronization, stepped into the core of the Heavenly Dao’s rules at the same moment.

The next moment, the authority of the Heavenly Dao, its rules, and immortal information enveloped Song Shuhang and Senior White.

For the first time, the right to inherit the Heavenly Dao’s authority was simultaneously assumed by two different entities.

“Is this the Heavenly Dao’s authority?” Song Shuhang reached out his palm, looking at his body that began to evolve from ‘sub-immortality’ to full ‘immortality’.

The information enveloping his body was the ’cause’ of all things in the world, the ‘source’ of all phenomena, and the ‘ultimate’ of all knowledge.

Authority and knowledge that were close to ‘omniscience and omnipotence’.

The reason it was said to be close to omniscience and omnipotence was only because it was lacking the knowledge and ability of ‘detachment’.

From the moment they inherited the authority of the Heavenly Dao, Song Shuhang and Senior White became the source of all and mastered the ultimate knowledge of the myriad practitioners in the universe.

“However, even at the final step, is the Heavenly Dao’s rules still expressing its dissatisfaction?” Song Shuhang suddenly laughed.

He and Senior White had begun to ‘immortalize’.

But the immortal information they received from the ‘Heavenly Dao Core’ and their ‘portion’ of the Heavenly Dao’s rules was only about 1.5 portions.

“It’s probably already at its limit,” Senior White said aloud.

His intuition told him that the material and information the Heavenly Dao could provide for someone to forge an ‘immortal’ state were limited. Moreover, Daozi had recently proved his Dao through Fat Ball’s backup plan to become the 8.5 Heavenly Dao and had obtained immortality once.

The 1.5 portions of immortality that the Heavenly Dao Core could provide now might just be its current limit... The remainder might require tens of thousands or even hundreds of millions of years to replenish.

If it had been any other two ‘different individuals’ proving their Dao, the lack of 0.5 portions of immortality probably would have prevented them from proving their Dao perfectly.

But neither Senior White nor Song Shuhang... needed a full two portions of immortality.

Song Shuhang originally had the ‘undying fat whale golden core’ + ‘sub-immortal’ state.

And Senior White also had a complete ‘immortal galaxy’.

So, even with just 1.5 portions of ‘immortality,’ it was more than enough to allow both to achieve immortality, even with plenty to spare!

Inheriting the ‘Heavenly Dao Authority’.

Receiving ‘ultimate knowledge’.

Condensing the ‘immortal body’.

The entire process was orderly and methodical.

The next step...

Was for the two of them to step out of the ‘Heavenly Dao Origin’ and declare to the myriad practitioners in the universe the incident of ‘two Heavenly Dao simultaneously proving their position,’ and to take over the ruling authority of the entire universe.

“By the way, Shuhang.” Before stepping out of the Heavenly Dao Origin world, Senior White spoke to Song Shuhang, “After proving the Dao, have you thought about the next step, ‘detachment’?”

“Mhm,” Song Shuhang nodded.

“Based on our current progress, after two different individuals have proven the Dao... one Heavenly Dao must stay behind to take over the complete Heavenly Dao authority, while the other completes detachment,” Senior White said seriously. “That means, among you and me, only one can achieve transcendence and eternity.”

Song Shuhang nodded again; he had deduced this as well.

“Then... have you ever considered that all my actions have been aimed at transcending immortality, to achieve detachment?” Senior White suddenly asked. “Haven’t you been the slightest bit cautious against me?”

“Senior White, stop joking around. You and I are attuned in heart and mind. You know my thoughts better than anyone,” Song Shuhang said. “For me, if Senior White can detach, it would also make up for the regret left behind by the master of the Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion, Pavilion Master Chu, and deal with the problems of the Future Subworld. The obsessions of the past, the karmic ties of the present, and the hopes for the future are all borne by us. Therefore, it makes no difference who detaches.”

The only regret might be that no matter who ‘detaches,’ it’s uncertain if they could continue to linger in this universe.

Whether there will be a time to meet again in the future.

This was the only concern in Song Shuhang’s heart regarding the ‘detachment’ plan.

“Although I am quite clear about it, I just wanted to ask,” Senior White stretched and revealed a satisfied smile.

Chapter 3126: Chapter 3124: You Might Not Believe It, But I Once Beat Up Tyrannical Song!
 

Song Shuhang himself didn’t have much longing for the seat of the Heavenly Dao.

If possible, maintaining the realm of an ‘Immortal’ was the most ideal state for him... and the ‘Sub-immortal State’ was even more perfect.

After all, once Sub-immortal... not even the descending Heavenly Dao coming to hammer him would be able to bring him down.

Song Shuhang’s character was not satisfied with the ordinary; compared to a mundane life, an exciting one attracted him more. Hence, when he first came into contact with the ‘Nine Provinces Number One Group’ and learned that its members were real cultivators who could turn rivers upside down and fly on swords, he instantly made up his mind to engage with the world of ‘cultivation.’

But on the other hand, he didn’t have any obsession with becoming truly ‘ultimate, detached.’

[To become one of the strongest beings, it would be best if no one could lay a finger on me.]

[I don’t easily provoke others, but I must have the power to deter anyone from offending me, ensuring that if someone tries to cross me, I can immediately retaliate and crush them on the spot.]

This was Song Shuhang’s mindset.

Now, the reason he desperately pursued immortality and strived for ‘transcendent’ eternity was not just for himself alone.

He bore the wills of the past, present, and future.

Therefore, between him and Senior White, there had to be one to transcend and resolve the obsessions of the past, present, and future.

But as to who specifically would transcend, it made no difference to Song Shuhang.

Since Senior White was obsessed with ‘transcendence,’ Song Shuhang was more than willing to become the hand that would unlock the ‘Heavenly Dao Prison’ imprisoning Senior White—releasing Senior White to gain true freedom, not bound by any worldly rules, and to dance freely beyond them.

And for himself, remaining an immortal forever also sounded quite delightful.

If he ever grew tired of that, he would discuss with the seniors to see if there was a way to free himself from the ‘Heavenly Dao seat,’ then return to the mundane world as a ‘Sub-immortal’ little Heavenly Dao whom even the Heavenly Dao itself couldn’t hammer—a truly beautiful scenario.

“Alright, let’s go... Leave the source of the Heavenly Dao, and then declare to the myriad practitioners in the universe that we have successfully proved our Dao, and synchronize with the ‘Netherworld World Origin’ to give birth to a ruler of the Netherworld,” Senior White waved to Song Shuhang, cheerfully said.

“By the way, can I give birth to another ruler of the Netherworld?” Song Shuhang followed Senior White and asked curiously.

After all, in the current Netherworld, there was already one Song Dark.

If another Song Dark two were to appear, how would the two Song Darks get along? Would it feel strange to coexist? After all, both were his rulers of the Netherworld, different from Fat Ball and Senior White two.

“Who knows? But it feels like it would be very interesting... Netherworld already has one White from the Netherworld and Netherworld Song; one more wouldn’t be a problem. In any case, everyone should be able to coexist peacefully, right?” Senior White was not troubled by this and instead found it rather interesting.

Once Song Shuhang joined him, the two once again adjusted their synchronization rate and stepped out of the ‘Heavenly Dao Origin,’ emerging from the Heavenly Principle Dimension into the main world.

At this moment, the myriad practitioners in the universe welcomed the era of two co-rulers for the first time!

This was a historic moment.

Unprecedented, and it’s likely very difficult for future generations to achieve!

The Myriad Realms once again trembled, paving the way for the arrival of the two sovereigns.

...

Among the myriad practitioners in the universe.

[Here it comes, finally! It’s been a long wait!] The Immortals who had been ready for a while had been waiting for this moment.

Since Tyrannical Song had withstood the might of the former Immortal Existence and forcefully entered the body proving process, the Immortals had been looking forward to this moment.

[You must succeed!] The last wisp of intent from Daoist Senior lingered nervously.

—Even though he had been watching the live broadcast of Tyrannical Song and Fellow Daoist White from the ‘Cultivator Chat System,’ he couldn’t rest easy until the very last moment.

[Will it be two people proving their Dao together, or just one?] The projected clone of Senior White two also watched the void.

[Don’t lose, Tyrannical Song. You must successfully prove your Dao and then relegate the former Immortal Existence to the dustbin of history!] The commentator from the Mo family clenched his fists and muttered internally—You’re the man who defeated me; if you fall at the last moment of proving the Dao, I’ll look down on you!

Inside the ‘Nine Provinces Number One Chat Group,’ the screen was flooded with countless messages.

—Everyone was anticipating the final outcome.

...

Some looked forward to it, while others despaired.

On a minor asteroid in the Cang Yan Realm of the myriad practitioners in the universe, Demon Emperor Hezhi rubbed his face, unable to speak.

He glanced at the ‘Heavenly Dao Pillar photo’ Tyrannical Song had sent him not long ago and then at the figure of the new Heavenly Dao slowly emerging in the vacuum. Despair filled his heart.

Just a few months ago, he was thinking of taking revenge on Tyrannical Song once his injuries healed.

Now, to take revenge with a hammer?

The other party had even taken a step further by proving his Dao and becoming the Heavenly Dao.

From hereon, there probably would be no place for him in the vast myriad realms. Before, he could still escape into the ‘Black Dragon World,’ a unique place that didn’t belong to the “myriad realms.”

But now, if he entered the Black Dragon World, he would die even faster.

As Demon Emperor Hezhi felt miserable, the ‘Cultivator Chat System’s system announcement function sent him a bright red notification: [Look, Tyrannical Song has proven his Dao.]

This was adding insult to injury.

Demon Emperor Hezhi reached out to dismiss the announcement: “...”

But a new system announcement popped up again: [Make sure to recover quickly, little brother Hezhi. Once your injuries are healed, I will suggest to Tyrannical Song to add a ‘Hezhi tribulation’ every thousand years, specifically for you—a VIP service.]

Demon Emperor Hezhi closed his eyes, ignoring the bright red announcement.

[Alternatively, you can come to the Black Dragon World and apologize to me. As long as your apology moves me, I can consider sparing you.] Lady Kunna almost snickered as she swiftly sent a ‘system announcement’ to Demon Emperor Hezhi.

The once powerful Hezhi, who had nearly driven her to collapse and snatched away her control of the ‘Dragon Network,’ had finally fallen to this day.

The resentment in Lady Kunna’s heart finally felt almost vented at this moment.

Then, she unfollowed Demon Emperor Hezhi.

Because Demon Emperor Hezhi could no longer bring her any more pleasure... Her true joy now came from the continuous upgrades of the ‘Cultivator Chat System.’

Each wave of upgrades, every new feature, and each user’s positive feedback made her overjoyed.

Next up, her goal was to integrate the ‘Black Dragon World’ into the ‘Cultivator Chat System.’

Before it was not possible, but now that Tyrannical Song had proven his Dao and the ‘Cultivator Chat System’ had the backing of the Heavenly Dao, the barriers between the Black Dragon World and the main world were no longer a problem.

“After the Black Dragon World successfully integrates into the ‘Cultivator Chat System,’ should I learn a small hair-growing technique? Or get a hair transplant?” Lady Kunna touched her forehead, feeling that her hairline seemed to have receded slightly.

...

Aside from cultivators who embraced this with anticipation and fear, a very small group of cultivators in the myriad realms had very complicated feelings.

These feelings were quite nostalgic.

For example, in the vicinity of the moon.

There was a red-haired Fifth Stage Golden Core expert looking up at the sky with his fellow friend.

“You might not believe it if I tell you... A few months ago, while I was chasing the ‘Soul Devouring Demonic Gourd’ in the starry skies near the moon, I encountered Tyrannical Song. At that time, I even chased and almost killed him all over the starry sky, nearly making him fall to the ground. Had it not been for summoning his senior, Venerable Seventh Cultivator of True Virtue, I might have actually taken him down. Now, Tyrannical Song has become the Heavenly Dao,” the red-haired Fifth Stage expert said with nostalgia.

His fellow friend looked at him as if he were insane, subconsciously distancing himself.

—Had his old friend lost his mind?

Actually fantasizing about attacking Tyrannical Song?

One should not boast like that!

Moreover, don’t you know that Mister Tyrannical Song has already proven his Dao and become an immortal?

Blowing your own trumpet at the time of his ascension, aren’t you afraid of attracting heavenly tribulation, to be struck to death by its might?

Even if the Heavenly Dao Tyrannical Song spares you, the laws of the Heavenly Dao might remember you... When you face your own tribulation, the might of their heavenly tribulation will surely rise by several levels!

Are you weary of living?

“Don’t say any more, if you keep this up, I’ll have no choice but to sever ties with you,” his fellow friend warned. He certainly didn’t want to inexplicably face a larger future heavenly tribulation simply because of his friend’s wild fantasies.

“I knew it, you definitely wouldn’t believe me,” the red-haired Spiritual Emperor lamented.

——Even I have trouble believing it myself!

If he hadn’t remembered that the Venerable Seventh Cultivator of True Virtue had taken his “Blade Dragging Technique” and “Flame Substituting Technique”, sparing his life as the price, he might have thought he was dreaming.

...

Like the red-haired Spiritual Emperor, Uncle Zheng De, the sect master of the Immortal Farming Sect, was similarly feeling nostalgic.

At that moment, Uncle Zheng De and several of his Immortal Farming Sect disciples were observing the scene of the “Will of the Heavens making an entrance.”

“You might not believe this, but I once firmly punched the face of the Heavenly Dao Tyrannical Song and knocked him out cold on the spot, unable to rise again... The incident even made the news in the Jiangnan District,” Uncle Zheng De said, stroking his chin with a wistful expression.

In other words, I was once someone who had triumphed over the Will of the Heavens face to face!

Damn, that’s enough to boast about for a lifetime.

Should I record this glorious event in the ‘Immortal Farming Sect’ archives?

And along with that, I should also collect that piece of news from the Jiangnan District from back then—the news about how he met Tyrannical Song and punched him unconscious.

In the future, when the disciples of the Immortal Farming Sect look at the records, they will surely be shocked by his feat!

After all, each Heavenly Dao in its youth fought above their level as easily as breathing, nearly always undefeated!

Beating a young Heavenly Dao at the age of eighteen is definitely something to boast about for a lifetime!

Some disciples of the Immortal Farming Sect looked at Uncle Zheng De with disbelief in their eyes.

But the several elder mentors of the Immortal Farming Sect standing by similarly looked wistful and nodded slightly, saying, “This is true. However, overall, our Immortal Farming Sect has a fairly good relationship with the Heavenly Dao Tyrannical Song. So, you don’t have to worry about punishment from him. On the contrary, we may even benefit from this.”

Cultivating a good relationship with Tyrannical Song is really the most correct and wisest choice for the Immortal Farming Sect.

...

In the world at the bottom of the sea.

The king of the sea urchin warriors, the Sea King, silently touched the Tribulation Immortal Armor on his body.

“I’m truly freaking clever,” the Sea King said with palpitations.

Luckily, I decisively chose to give up hatred and settled with Tyrannical Song through the channel of the ‘Almighty Merchant.’

Otherwise, facing Tyrannical Song who had proven his Dao and ascended to the Will of the Heavens, I and the sea urchin warriors would definitely face extinction!

But the price... was that it would lose a portion of its internal consciousness within its ‘Body of Eternity.’ That part of its immortal body would become a ‘Blank Nickname,’ losing all control.

Chapter 3127: Chapter 3125: Whether You Come or Not, the Nine Consecutive Championships are Always Here!

Chapter 3128: Chapter 3126: The Divine Said: Let There Be Light! (1st Update)

Chapter 3129: Chapter 3127: No Choice but to Work Harder (2nd Update)
 

What happened?

If Song Shuhang agrees, the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy might even offer him a tip to get the chance to confront the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao head-on!

The Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy has compassion for all living beings—except for the ‘Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao’.

As merciful as she is to all beings in the myriad realms, she is equally cold towards the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao.

Just now, the effect on the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao was one of the billions of techniques she developed, specifically aimed at the ‘Fourth Heavenly Dao’.

During the ancient era, when designing countermeasures for the ‘Fourth Heavenly Dao’, she simulated many possibilities.

—This included the possibility of the ‘Fourth Heavenly Dao temporarily restoring Heavenly Dao Authority’, which she also accounted for!

And for the hypothesis that ‘temporary recovery of Heavenly Dao Authority is likely to come with a cost’, she developed the “Let There Be Reincarnation” strategy.

While maintaining the “cost” to the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao, to cycle back and reverse what it was doing.

Allowing it to labor and pay costs, without gaining anything.

This Reincarnation effect carried a flavor of ‘time-reversal’, yet it wasn’t a brute reversal of all states of time.

It required greater difficulty, more refined calculations.

The Reincarnation principles, so terrifying!

“So, since this sentence is over now, it should be me saying this!”

“Darkness Big Shot, you have already failed!”

“And there’s only one reason for your failure, and that is encountering me, Tyrannical Song!”

Song Shuhang struggled to maintain an ‘expressionless’ face, so as not to give away his bluff to his opponent.

“Over?” asked the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao, extending its hand in the vacuum and grabbing the ‘Heavenly Dao Pillar’ as a flash of ‘Dao Traces’ appeared in its hand... shredding Song Shuhang’s Dao Traces and intent added to the ‘Heavenly Dao Pillar’.

These Dao Traces and intent were a setup!

They were the setup for releasing “Let There Be Reincarnation”.

The massive enclosed Reincarnation world, the sky-filled lightning of tribulation, the Overlord God Pillar leaving stealthy remaining Dao Traces beside the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao on impact, all were part of the setup.

All of this, combined with the power transferred from the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy + Tyrannical Song’s Heavenly Dao Authority, constituted the “Let There Be Reincarnation” contingency.

“You’re not the Fifth Heavenly Dao, and using her techniques requires a setup,” said the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao while continuing to maintain the operation of “suppressing Song Shuhang”, and it began to destroy Song Shuhang’s Dao Marks.

As long as Tyrannical Song is denied the opportunity to set up, the “Let There Be Reincarnation” technique can’t be reactivated.

The cost is that it must split its focus to stop the “Overlord God Pillars” Tyrannical Song keeps blasting over, unable to fully concentrate on suppressing Tyrannical Song’s “Heavenly Dao Authority” operation.

This invisibly extends the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao’s time of “Ultimate Sublimation, Manifesting as Temporary Heavenly Dao”, with each extra second causing irreparable damage and cost.

But if it doesn’t address the ‘Overlord God Pillars’ and Song Shuhang’s Dao Traces, Tyrannical Song can reactivate the Fifth Heavenly Dao’s techniques.

So, however unwillingly, the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao had no choice—facing Tyrannical Song and Bai Hou, its life gradually lost the right to choose.

“It’s a pity. Against such an experienced big shot, a skill used once cannot be used again,” Song Shuhang kept his face expressionless.

If he could keep repeating the process, without much effort, he could exhaust the ‘Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao’ into a pure Blank Nickname, an eternity body without a soul.

Now, it seemed more effort was required; new methods had to be utilized!

The Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy left him with the “A Billion Contingencies for Confronting the Fourth Heavenly Dao,” filled with countless plans and methods.

If one method fails, simply switch to another.

Song Shuhang’s goal wasn’t just to defeat Dark Heaven... he had an even more thrilling plan.

He wanted to grind Dark Heaven into white.

To grind it into a state of pure white without consciousness.

Chapter 3130: Chapter 3128: When Did You Start Having the Illusion That You Could Suppress Me? (3rd Update)
 

Song Shuhang was aware of the physical state of the “Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao” before him... he even knew the method by which the other could “re-prove its Dao” in a short time, as well as the price it had to continuously pay!

These pieces of information, the moment the “Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao” arrived in the “Heavenly Principle Dimension” and appeared before Song Shuhang, were all displayed in his eyes without omission!

This might be related to the “Heavenly Dao Authority” that can perceive the essence of all things—however, logically, this perceptive authority should have been neutralized by the Dark Heavenly Dao, which had equally evolved to become the “Flawless Heavenly Dao.”

Even to prevent his greatest secrets from being captured by Tyrannical Song and Senior White and targeted by Tyrannical Song, before stepping into the “Heavenly Principle Dimension,” the Dark Heavenly Dao should have shielded or even altered its own information.

Being in the role of the current “Heavenly Dao,” theoretically, its secrets should not be easily captured by Song Shuhang.

But theory, before being tested, is always subject to change—thus, as soon as the Dark Heavenly Dao stepped into the “Heavenly Principle Dimension,” its bodily state had already been represented as a digitalized panel before Song Shuhang.

This function seemed like an ultimate evolved version of Tyrannical Song’s demonic technique, the “secret appraisal technique,” as well as the “dreamland skill!”

The secret appraisal technique allowed Tyrannical Song to obtain practical information from others through direct contact, at a certain cost. The greater the cost, the more information obtained.

The dreamland skill was even more of a bug—merely by satisfying a certain “connection,” Tyrannical Song could unreasonably access the “past” of others and obtain a wealth of intelligence.

And there were not a few such “connections” between the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao and Song Shuhang.

For example, the constant emission of the “Heavenly Dao Pillar•Black Pillar.”

And then there was the “Domination Secret Method.”

Additionally, there was the “portion of existence” that Song Shuhang and Senior White had snatched from the Dark Sun using the “Confucian Saint Talent.”

There were even instances like the “Dark Heavenly Dao” using an alternate account to register in the “Cultivator Chat System,” which ended up locking the real ID due to the system’s automatic tracking.

Song Shuhang had both direct and indirect contacts with the Dark Heavenly Dao, which provided grounds for using the “dreamland technique.”

These numerous deep connections, once the conditions were satisfied, turned into channels through which Tyrannical Song could grasp the data information of the “Dark Heavenly Dao.”

Moreover...

In the process of contesting the “Heavenly Dao Management Authority” with the Dark Heavenly Dao, a distracted part of Song Shuhang had personally experienced the Dark Heavenly Dao sacrificing the “Dark Sun Avatar” to greatly elevate itself and re-enter the seat of Heavenly Dao, in the form of a “dreamland skill”.

Additionally, the “Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy” provided intelligence on the “millions of contingencies of the Dark Heavenly Dao,” including the predication results for various states of the Dark Heavenly Dao.

Therefore, at this point, there wasn’t a single spot, from outside to inside, that was unfamiliar to Song Shuhang in regard to the Dark Heavenly Dao!

It seemed utterly defenseless in Tyrannical Song’s eyes, without the slightest secret.

The confrontation between current Heavenly Dao wielders wasn’t just a comparison of crafty moves... Intelligence was also a crucial factor!

“Song Shuhang, has something unexpected happened in the Heavenly Principle Dimension?” At this time, Senior White’s voice rang out beside Song Shuhang’s ear.

“There’s a slight problem, but I can handle it. Of course, if you, Senior White, could finish up quickly and then quietly come over to block the exit to prevent the ‘Dark Heavenly Dao’ from escaping, that’d be even safer.” Song Shuhang specifically emphasized to come and block the gate “quietly” to avoid startling the Dark Heavenly Dao, giving it no choice but to escape in despair.

“Received, I will carefully make my way there.” Senior White replied.

“Hehehe.” Song Shuhang sent back a mischievous smile emoji.

Time ticked away by the second.

On the opposite side.

The Dark Heavenly Dao no longer urgently sought to hurry.

This time, it was distracted in coping with Song Shuhang’s various crafty tactics—the deflecting effect of the Heavenly Dao Pillars was immune to it, Dao Traces left by Tyrannical Song were broken by it. Even to prevent Tyrannical Song from playing more tricks, it was also covertly divining the heavenly mechanism.

In this ‘steady and solid’ pace, it took three times the usual duration... After sacrificing nine grains of “Immortal Sand” bodies to the sky, it suppressed Song Shuhang once again.

“It’s over.” The Dark Heavenly Dao voiced inwardly.

This time, it even refrained from showing any emotions, lest it be detected by Tyrannical Song.

It planned to seize the Heavenly Dao management authority by surprise and burst forth unexpectedly.

Bursting!

In an instant, the Dark Heavenly Dao drastically elevated its operation over the “Heavenly Dao Authority.”

Boom~

The related segment of “Heavenly Dao Authority” management was once again acquired by it.

The authority that Tyrannical Song had in this area was completely suppressed by it.

This time, Tyrannical Song could not use the method of “bringing about Reincarnation” to stop it.

“Spread.” The moment it obtained the authority, the Dark Heavenly Dao immediately employed its measures—countless “Stellar Destruction Virus•Ultimate Heavenly Dao Reinforced Edition” that had been prepared in advance were spread to all stars in the myriad worlds using the Heavenly Dao authority.

Almost in the instant when it completed its plan, the feedback from the “Domination Secret Method” used by the Immortal Daoist at that place came—it was contacting ‘White Heavenly Dao’ face to face.

Under the effect of the reinforced “Domination Secret Method,” the Immortal Daoist, exerting his full strength, began to drag out ‘White Heavenly Dao.’

“Very good, just like that...”

Use all your strength to pin down ‘White Heavenly Dao,’ buying me time.

“The world... shall end today.”

“On the path of transcendence, I will take a step ahead.”

The Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao stretched out its hand and snapped its fingers lightly.

In an instant, all the ‘stars’ across the myriad worlds were ignited.

The ultimate version of the Stellar Destruction Virus erupted.

Compared to that time during the Sixth Heavenly Dao Virtuous Daoist’s reign, this stellar destruction was even more exaggerated, more irreversible!

This time, even using the method of ‘cutting off karmic ties’ couldn’t restart this myriad realms.

Stellar destruction, galaxy obliteration, space obliteration, plane annihilation, the scene of the destruction of the myriad worlds unfolded once again before Song Shuhang’s eyes.

The Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao stretched out its arms.

It had made preparations to exit the ‘Flawless Heavenly Dao’ state and, if successful, step into the phase of ‘Final Transcendence’ right after exiting the Heavenly Dao state.

Before exiting the ‘Flawless Heavenly Dao’ mode, the Dark Heavenly Dao glanced at Tyrannical Song.

It wanted to see Tyrannical Song’s despair.

However, when it looked over, it discovered a vivid expression of ‘pleasure’ on Tyrannical Song’s face.

Tyrannical Song’s originally expressionless face suddenly transformed into talking captions.

After a brief interpretation of Tyrannical Song’s facial expression, the following message could be understood.

Fool, did you think you really won? Did you really think everything was over?

“Has it not ended yet?”

Did you think from start to finish, that you suppressed me?

“What does this mean?”

When did you start having the illusion that I was under your suppression?

“?”

Then, in the next moment... the figure of the White Heavenly Dao appeared behind Song Shuhang.

“Is it about time?” White Heavenly Dao said with a smile.

“Yep,” Song Shuhang nodded.

Chapter 3131: Chapter 3129: The Big Villain Who Got Whitewashed (4th Update)
 

Senior White’s appearance marked that everything had already entered the ultimate stage and could come to an end.

“Time for a redemption arc?” Senior White asked again.

Before he arrived, he had already learned the details of the situation through Song Shuhang.

“In some light-hearted movies, it’s normal for the main antagonist to be redeemed in the grand finale,” replied Song Shuhang.

The ‘Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao’ before him was about to be redeemed.

Both spiritually and physically—a double redemption.

Across from him,

The moment the white-robed figure appeared, the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao felt something was amiss.

From the viewpoint of ‘Domination Secret Method • Immortal Daoist’, the Immortal Daoist was still struggling against ‘Wielder of the Will White’.

Yet, ‘Wielder of the Will White’ had already reached the Heavenly Dao Dimension World.

[Could it be that the one contending with the Immortal Daoist is not the ‘Wielder of the Will White’, but the New Netherworld Ruler that the white-robed figure has become?]

Newly born Netherworld Rulers have a chance to enter the main world once + exercise Heavenly Dao Authority.

Or perhaps, did the Immortal Daoist become a pitfall?

[No matter what... Now that the white-robed figure has returned, I can no longer stay in the ‘Heavenly Dao Dimension’.] This thought flashed through the mind of the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao.

Whatever Tyrannical Song and the white-robed figure planned to do, it was no longer possible for them to affect it.

The world had already been obliterated.

This time, no one could save the world!

Next, it would transcend... Although it had paid a great price and was nearly leaving as ‘disabled’, it sought transcendence and eternity.

But once successful, from a perspective of ‘transcendence and eternity’, there would always be a way to compensate for its own deficiencies.

Thus, it no longer held any reason to stay in this world.

[Return, then exit the fully enriched ‘Flawless Heaven Dao Mode’.]

No matter what you want to do, Tyrannical Song, I’m not playing with you anymore!

The next moment, the aura of the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao began to fade.

“Leaving in such a hurry, Mister Fourth Heavenly Dao?” The white-robed figure across from it flashed the world’s most handsome smile: “I’ve just come back, and if you’re leaving, wouldn’t that seem like we’ve been poor hosts?”

So, Mister Fourth Heavenly Dao, won’t you stay a little longer—these were the subtitles on Tyrannical Song’s facial expression.

“There is no need,” said the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao slowly.

“No, I think it’s very necessary.” The smile of the white-robed figure became dangerous... or rather, it became forceful: “I hope you stay here until I allow you to leave.”

[Stay here and let you two gang up on me? Have I gone mad?] the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao scoffed.

It activated all its ‘Heavenly Dao Authority’ abilities, preparing to forcibly transfer itself to the ‘Heavenly Dao Dimension’ space.

However, it quickly discovered that the transfer had failed.

What’s going on?

The Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao finally felt uneasy—this unease wasn’t cowardice, but a genuine sense of crisis, as if some insurmountable calamity was imminent.

Perhaps the crisis had already arrived.

What’s the situation?

Why can’t I leave the ‘Heavenly Dao Dimension’?

Even...

Why can’t I exit the ‘fully enriched’ state?

“Confused?” Song Shuhang’s voice turned warm and dependable: “If you’re confused, just look at me.”

Come on, look at my face!

Let my face reveal the truth to you!

In fact, without needing a reminder from Song Shuhang... As soon as it sensed Tyrannical Song’s ‘straightforward face with built-in subtitles’, the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao immediately turned its gaze onto Tyrannical Song’s face the very moment something went wrong within itself.

This time, indeed, it gained sufficient information.

[Mister Fourth Heavenly Dao, do you still have an ample number of ‘Immortal Sand Grains’ required for your ultimate sublimation?]

[!]

“Why do you know about this?” The Dark Heavenly Dao was shocked internally, but still tried to maintain composure, taking the initiative to inquire.

It had shielded this information and altered it during the moment of fully enriching sublimation, temporarily becoming the ‘Flawless Heavenly Dao’.

“[I understand you even better than you think I do!]” Tyrannical Song’s face flashed a subtitle: “[Are you feeling troubled because you can’t exit the ‘Ultimate Sublimation’ state? I’ll ask once again, is your ‘Immortal Sand’ quantity still sufficient?]”

[Why is Tyrannical Song asking if my quantity is sufficient?] The Dark Heavenly Dao pondered for a moment and suddenly thought of a possibility...

Its Ultimate Sublimation was achieved by sacrificing ‘Immortal Body Sand’ to maintain the ‘Flawless Heavenly Dao’ state.

If its supply of ‘Immortal Sand Body’ was insufficient, down to the last grain, then theoretically, it really wouldn’t be able to exit the ‘Flawless Heavenly Dao’ state.

Because at that point, there would be no more ‘Immortal Sand’ for it to fall back on. It would continue to burn as the final embers until the last grain of ‘Immortal Sand’ was completely used up.

“Impossible, my Immortal Sand Grain Number... should still be plentiful. Moreover, I’ve been keeping an eye on them,” the Dark Heavenly Dao examined its own condition internally.

Even after paying half the price to ‘return to the Heavenly Dao’, its Immortal Sand quantity had remained rather substantial. And during its confrontation with Tyrannical Song, it had depleted at most only a dozen or so grains of Immortal Sand, not even twenty.

How could they possibly be exhausted?

After looking inside,

“The quantity, of course, remains plentiful,” the Dark Heavenly Dao breathed a sigh of relief.

Opposite, Tyrannical Song’s facial barrage continued: “[Are you sure your Immortal Sand is still plentiful?]”

“What do you mean?” The Dark Heavenly Dao spoke while secretly opening a ‘space gate’, not using its Heavenly Dao Authority to force a shift, preparing to use the ‘main world’ as a stepping stone to first avoid Tyrannical Song.

“[You have been keeping an eye on your ‘Immortal Sand’ quantity... So when did you last feel that your ‘Immortal Sand Grain Number’ was still plentiful?]” Tyrannical Song’s facial subtitles became more enigmatic.

But this enigma had an irritating and vexing feel to it.

It felt like nitpicking.

And like... a strategic delay.

“I get it now, from start to finish, you wanted to delay time,” the Dark Heavenly Dao felt like it finally ‘woke up’ to the reality.

Consequently, it no longer wasted time with Song Shuhang.

Boom~

It forced open a ‘space gate’ with a punch.

Then, it turned around.

Ready to step into the ‘space gate’.

This time, neither Tyrannical Song nor the white-robed figure tried to stop it.

In fact, both of their expressions were perfectly in sync.

Showing a look of amusement.

“Pretending to be profound!” The Dark Heavenly Dao didn’t hesitate to turn around and stepped into the space gate.

But just as it stepped in... it suddenly felt lighter.

A strange sensation washed over it.

Stepping into the space gate, it was as if it lost its body.

It was like its soul had entered the gate, but its flesh was left behind?

At the last moment, the Dark Heavenly Dao glanced at Tyrannical Song’s face.

“[Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy says: ‘The sky is originally colorless, it didn’t deceive you, it’s your own eyes and mind that deceived you.’]”

“Illusion? Impossible.”

“[Illusion? No, it’s real. Everything you see is real. It’s just you who is mistaken.]”

Illusions should have no effect on the Flawless Heavenly Dao!

Across from it, the Dark Heavenly Dao failed to understand what Tyrannical Song’s final subtitle meant.

It no longer had the chance to understand.

All of the Immortal Sand had already been sacrificed, cleansed.

The Immortal Sands, which should have been able to burn for a long time and were plentiful in number, were suddenly exhausted in a short time.

“[So, when walking in the martial world, one shouldn’t provoke a powerful woman. Why is it that people just don’t understand this?]”
