Chapter 3132: Chapter 3130: Dance, Senior White!
 

Splash~

With the consciousness of the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao completely burned away, white sand-like substances fell from the sky of the Heavenly Principle Dimension, piling up in front of Song Shuhang and Senior White, forming heaps of sand.

These white sand grains shimmered with the glow of eternity, each grain appearing as if it were cast from white crystals, pleasing to the eye—this was the world’s most expensive, most beautiful treasure.

True•Whitewash.

Song Shuhang looked at the treasure loot dropped after the boss fight, nodding in satisfaction.

The virtuous lamia emerged from behind Song Shuhang, curiously floating over to the pile of white sand.

Then, she coiled her snake tail, her snake waist bending into an exaggerated curve, as she gently scooped up a small amount of white sand with both hands.

The fine white sand was lifted by her, brought up to her eyes, and then fell through the gaps of her fingers.

The moment was picturesque.

Song Shuhang quietly captured this scene.

—The virtuous lamia, nonchalant and elegant, had a truly wonderful aesthetic.

Sadly, this picturesque side of her was rarely revealed.

After all the fine sand had run out, the virtuous lamia carefully picked up a single grain of white sand with her index finger, lifting it to her eyes to inspect closely.

A moment later...

The virtuous lamia blinked her eyes, then opened her mouth—it looked like she wanted to taste the flavor of the white sand grains?

“@#%¥, Fairy, stop, don’t!” Behind her, Tyrannical Song hastily stopped her action, “You can’t eat this!”

Not everything should be tasted, you’re not the divine farmer Shennong.

These fine white sand grains were objects that carry the aura of eternity.

They were what remained after the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao paid all of its dues, its Immortal Body completely whitewashed.

Now, these Immortal Sand Grains held no ‘intent’, completely blank.

Finally, they had become what Song Shuhang had wanted!

—If the Immortals knew of their existence, most of them would probably be willing to give up everything they owned to exchange for a single grain.

The virtuous lamia turned her head and looked at Song Shuhang.

Seeing his serious expression, she seemed somewhat regretful as she put the white sand grain from her fingertip back into the heap.

Looks like it really wasn’t edible.

Song Shuhang sighed in relief.

But just as he had relaxed, Senior White had somehow stealthily moved next to the virtuous lamia.

Then, just like the Fairy before, he touched a grain of the pure white sand, seemingly wanting to sneak a taste.

“Senior White!” Song Shuhang cried out, reaching to stop him.

“I didn’t eat it,” Senior White turned around, seriously said.

“You really can’t eat it, and it’s useful,” Song Shuhang seriously replied.

“I know, I’m studying them,” Senior White replied, holding the white sand grain in his hand, a thoughtful expression crossing his face.

Song Shuhang dared not lower his vigilance, keeping an eye on both Senior White and the virtuous lamia, while contacting the ‘Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy’.

—This time, the reason for being able to whitewash the ‘Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao’ so smoothly and easily was that the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy was one of the strongest supporters.

Her preparation of a myriad of contingencies for the ‘Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao’ really helped a lot.

“Fairy, how is your ‘Fourth Heavenly Dao Sand’ doing?” Song Shuhang communicated with the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy through the Heavenly Dao Authority.

“`

After transforming into reincarnation, the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy could sense the outside world, but communication with her became very troublesome. Even the Reincarnation Blade Fairy had to go through a lot of trouble to make contact with the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy.

However, now that Song Shuhang had proven his position in the Heavenly Dao, with the authority of the Heavenly Dao, he could directly converse with the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy.

[Pure, clean, end.] The Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy sent back a few words.

She suppressed a batch of ‘Dark Sun Avatar’ state Immortal Sand through the ‘Reincarnation Seal’ formed by Song Shuhang and Su Clan’s Sixteen.

Now, these grains of sand had also turned pure white; the awareness of the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao within them was sacrificed—in fact, the ‘Immortal Sand’ that stayed with her was among the earliest to become pure white.

The ‘half of the Immortal Body’ price paid by the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao when ‘returning to the seat of the Heavenly Dao’ mostly consisted of the batch that was suppressed by the Reincarnation Seal.

Because this batch of Immortal Sand was suppressed by the Reincarnation Seal and was temporarily of no use, it was the most suitable for the sacrificial half.

[Received, I’ll trouble the Fairy next.] Song Shuhang replied.

As he spoke, through the authority of the Heavenly Dao, he opened the passageway to the ‘Heavenly Principle Dimension’ for the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy.

Rustle rustle rustle~

Another wave of pure white crystal sand fell from the vacuum, landing in front of Song Shuhang and Senior White.

With this, the ‘Body of Eternity’ of the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao was now entirely here.

Not a single grain was missing!

However, to be on the safe side, after all the ‘Immortal Sand’ had accumulated, Song Shuhang also repeatedly inspected and appraised them using the ‘Heavenly Dao Authority’ to confirm that there was no more consciousness of the ‘Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao’ among the sand.

“Senior White.” After the inspection, Song Shuhang looked towards Senior White, hoping he could help him conduct another check.

A single spark can start a prairie fire.

To ensure the success of his next experiment, he could not even leave behind a spark.

He could not give the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao any chance of ‘resurrection’.

“Understood.” Senior White nodded.

The soul link between him and Song Shuhang allowed him to directly understand Song Shuhang’s consciousness; not much speech was needed.

Senior White placed his hands on the two piles of ‘Immortal Sand’ and began to check them one by one.

If under such a thorough examination, the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao could still conceal a wisp of consciousness, then Song Shuhang would swallow that grain of sand raw!

While Senior White was inspecting the sand, Song Shuhang sent another message to the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy: [Thank you for your hard work, Fairy.]

[Joyful.] The Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy replied with a word that expressed her mood at the time.

...

In that final moment, he used two of the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy’s back-up plans to deal with the ‘Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao’.

One was the back-up plan that could be deployed under the premise of [Hypothesis: The Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao is no longer complete + possession of a part of the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao’s body]: Past View.

The Heavenly Dao’s White had once said: The eyes of the divine look towards the future.

‘Past View’ was the opposite, locking the vision onto a certain time period in the past.

The Heavenly Dao is nearly omnipotent, however, it has not completely transcended ‘time.’ Thus, if one wants to impact the Heavenly Dao, it could be done through ‘time.’

But this is not an easy task—due to the ‘undying’ nature of the Heavenly Dao, time techniques often struggle to affect the immortal.

Luckily, the sacrifice made by the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao when ‘returning to the Heavenly Dao’ made it less perfect—it was much like the fat ball, which had a part of itself swallowed by the Confucian Sage after it rejoined the Heavenly Dao.

Under such conditions + the Immortal Sand in the hands of the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy as the ‘casting medium’, and with Song Shuhang’s cooperation, they finally created an effect.

The observation of the ‘Immortal Sand Grain Number’ by the Black Heaven was affected by ‘Past View’—it was observing always a ‘past’ state.

And the passage of this ‘past’ was far slower than the flow of ‘present’ time.

It kept seeing that it had an ample number of ‘Immortal Sand grains’.

“`

“`

But in truth... what it saw was a ‘past’ from long ago.

Illusion spells cannot influence the Will of the Heavens; what the Heavenly Dao sees is the truth—however, like the ‘Future Vision’ of the white-robed figure, this truth can be either the ‘future’ or the ‘past.’

And the ‘past’ seen by the Dark Heaven was from a full ten days ago!

The operation of its second ‘Heavenly Dao Authority Struggle’ with Song Shuhang had, in fact, already lasted a full ten days.

Ten days of time in the main world, not due to any time-acceleration effects. In the main world, it was already February 15, 2020!

That is to say, it had actually already sacrificed its ‘Immortal Sand Body,’ burning for a full ten days and nights, until it finally burned itself out.

And all this time, the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao had not sensed anything.

What caused this effect was another contingency of the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy—a “Seclusion Reincarnation.”

Coupled with Song Shuhang’s Heavenly Dao Authority, this contingency could create an effect similar to seclusion, where ‘in the blink of an eye, ten thousand years pass.’ One exits seclusion and thousands or tens of thousands of years have gone by. Meanwhile, during seclusion, a cultivator feels almost no passage of time.

Overall, the effect of [Seclusion + Past View].

It’s like closing one’s eyes and feeling as if they had only a very short dream, thinking only two minutes had passed. But when they open their eyes, two hours have already gone by.

...

Ten days were enough for Song Shuhang to do far too many things.

Once the Heavenly Dao gets going, within its authority, it can do too many unimaginably amazing things.

And what’s more, Song Shuhang wasn’t alone; he proved his Dao together with Senior White.

A double act of clever maneuvers.

Thus, during these ten days, Senior White, within the ‘Heavenly Dao space,’ used the shadow of ‘Myriad Realms’ to construct a model of the ‘Myriad Realms.’

This model included systems, stars, planets, and other shells that matched the main world 1:1.

Finally, with the authority of the Heavenly Dao and through joint efforts with Song Shuhang, the ‘Myriad Realms Model’ was overlaid onto the Myriad Realms of the main world.

It was like a brief switch between shadow and substance.

The real Myriad Realms entered the shadow, while the model, which was like a shadow, took the place of the Myriad Realms.

—Such an elaborate effort, all to properly handle the batch of ultimate Stellar Destruction Virus that the Dark Heavenly Dao had concocted.

If not dealt with, this batch of virus could ultimately become a hidden danger.

Incidentally... creating a ‘shell’ for the Myriad Realms was also a fun thing to do.

At the very least, Senior White had a lot of fun and wasn’t bored at all in these ten days.

When everything was ready...

Song Shuhang ‘unresistingly’ got thoroughly suppressed by the Dark Heavenly Dao.

The ‘Stellar Destruction Virus’ that destroys everything entered the ‘Myriad Realms’ and the virus was detonated, destroying the world.

The script of world obliteration was complete.

Everything was arranged clearly and unmistakably.

...

The question is still the same—’What if.’

If the Dark Heavenly Dao had a bit more time to observe the world in detail before destroying the Myriad Realms, it might have discovered a flaw.

But sensing the potential return of the white-robed figure and under the pressure of being outnumbered, the Dark Heavenly Dao had no time to choose.

From beginning to end, Tyrannical Song and White never gave it any chance to choose.

With relentless pressure...

Finally, it was forced into the shape Song Shuhang wanted—a purely white Immortal Sand.

The most important point.

These ‘Immortal Sand Grains’ were left behind by the Fourth Heavenly Dao before it ‘exited Heavenly Dao mode.’

Its intent was completely erased, but it was still in a state of the ‘Flawless Heavenly Dao.’

...

...

“No problem at all,” Senior White said as he withdrew his hands from the two piles of ‘Immortal Sand,’ confirming.

Having said that, he turned his gaze toward Song Shuhang. “Do you have plans for these ‘Immortal Sand Grains’?”

“Specifically, it’s just a thought, but whether it will succeed or not, I cannot be sure yet,” Song Shuhang said.

“Leaving a blank Heavenly Dao... Then, the two of us can transcend one after another, right?” Senior White looked at Song Shuhang, not only reading his face but also expressing his own previous idea.

“Yes,” Song Shuhang nodded. “However, because the ‘Immortal Sand’ did not prove the Dao with us ‘simultaneously.’ Without this step, and due to its blank state with no consciousness, taking over our ‘Heavenly Dao Authority’ is not so simple. Therefore, it is still just a thought.”

The ‘simultaneous proving of Dao’ proposed by the white-robed figure is a very important matter.

Only two individuals who proved their Dao simultaneously have the highest degree of compatibility, can fully take over the ‘Heavenly Dao Bind’ from another individual, binding it onto themselves, allowing the other to achieve transcendence.

There’s this gap between the Immortal Sand and Song Shuhang, Senior White.

But its existence also represents a ‘possible future.’

It’s a hope.

Perhaps in the future, it could become a proxy, an agent Heavenly Dao.

And then allow the Heavenly Dao that remains bound, to transfer all of its Heavenly Dao Authority to the ‘Immortal Sand,’ achieving great liberation.

Time is still very long.

Song Shuhang, who just proved the Heavenly Dao, still has plenty of time.

“But for now, let’s not think about that,” Song Shuhang said as he clenched his fist.

Opposite him, Senior White also clenched his fist and gently touched his.

Both Heavenly Dao figures activated their ‘Heavenly Dao Authority’ simultaneously.

The ‘Myriad Realms Model,’ which was being mercilessly destroyed, was rolled up.

The apocalyptic end would continue in this model.

It would mercilessly destroy all these modeled stars.

But this virus would forever remain in this ‘Myriad Realms Model.’

And the real Myriad Realms was safe and sound.

Its countless creatures did not even know that they had once again lived through a ‘world’s end.’

The calamity of the ‘present’ has ended.

The next step is to resolve the obsession of the ‘past’ and bring hope to the ‘future.’

“Transcend, Senior White,” Song Shuhang said to Senior White.

He, the salted fish, had no expectation for true ‘transcendence’ and had no obsession.

But Senior White had a certain obsession with transcending...

Song Shuhang decided to become the hands that opened Senior White’s cage, to unlock the Heavenly Dao Bind from Senior White and bear it all himself.

Then, to grant Senior White true freedom, to soar through the past, present, and future.

Chapter 3133: Chapter 3131: Seniors of the Will of the Heavens Today
 

“Is this your final decision?” Senior White smiled warmly as he looked at Song Shuhang.

Song Shuhang nodded slightly, just about to respond...

Suddenly, the virtuous lamia beside them covered her face with both hands, “Ah~ Senior White~”

Then her body slowly fell to the ground and rolled, abruptly dying.

Song Shuhang was baffled, “???”

The virtuous lamia died in a very dedicated manner this time; she slowly closed her eyes, not blinking them.

—She felt that her ‘death’ this time was very considerate. To avoid interrupting the conversation between Senior White and Song Shuhang, it was appropriate for her wise ‘body of virtue’ to die.

If it weren’t for the fact that she couldn’t move after ‘dying,’ she would have planned to keep rolling, rolling away to a distant place.

After all, she had now become the body of virtue of the Heavenly Dao, and she needed to be more dedicated than ever.

“Ahem.” Song Shuhang coughed lightly and replied, “Senior White, as you know, I’m not obsessed with ‘detachment’. So... it’s better if you, Senior White, achieve detachment.”

“Do you have no regrets?” Senior White still wore a smile—clearly, he was in a good mood.

“There’s nothing to regret,” Song Shuhang said earnestly. “And besides, if we step back a million steps, haven’t we taken down the ‘Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao’? Its immortal body is still in a ‘semi-in-office’ state. Just give me some time... If needed in the future, I might be able to devise a plan for detachment.”

“When is the future?” Senior White leaned back slightly.

Cooperating, Song Shuhang stretched out a hand, and a dark lotus the size of a chair emerged from the void, supporting Senior White.

This was the black lotus from the Lotus Blossoming Walk.

Senior White leaned back against the black lotus and sat down comfortably.

“As for the future, maybe after detachment, you, Senior White, might be able to see it? Anyway, I’ve just proved the position of the Immortal Heavenly Dao, and there should be plenty of time,” Song Shuhang pondered and replied.

“Indeed, we still have quite a bit of time, at least in the short term, we don’t have to worry about the influence of the laws of the Heavenly Dao,” Senior White nodded slightly, his seemingly longer hair fluttering with the movement.

—Once someone holds the position of the Heavenly Dao for a long period, they will be influenced by the laws of the Heavenly Dao, in terms of their insights and thought processes becoming regularized.

The laws of the Heavenly Dao are necessary to maintain the operation of the myriad practitioners in the universe.

The ones who hold the laws of the Heavenly Dao, under subtle influences, will gradually be affected.

If it is a perfect Heavenly Dao, it can restrain these influences to some extent. But for a Heavenly Dao like the fat ball, by its end, it would quickly become an emotionless tool, adhering strictly to the programmed responsibilities of the Heavenly Dao.

“So, do you have any idea about how to apply the ‘Fourth Heavenly Dao Shell’?” Senior White asked.

“At the moment, I don’t really have any specific ideas. Anyway, the few tricks I know could be tried on the ‘Fourth Heavenly Dao Shell’. Perhaps the most important thing is to first cultivate a tacit understanding with these ‘Immortal Sand Grains’?” Song Shuhang said, his right hand instinctively sliding in the void.

The false ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ requires one to invest delicate polishing insights into the saber, communicate with the saber for an hour, and then spend a few minutes using the ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’. Afterwards, one still needs to mesh emotions with the saber.

The true ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ involves crazily sliding one’s hand over the saber—a billion, ten billion, or even a hundred billion repetitions of ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ per second, achieving one’s goals with Cheap Love—and not just with sabers, but applicable to everything.

After proving his Dao and becoming immortal, Tyrannical Song had clearly mastered the essence of ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’.

“There seems to be some feasibility to it,” Senior White also thought about the effects of Song Shuhang’s demonic technique.

This was, after all, a technique all Whites would consider a ‘demonic technique’.

To tell the truth, throughout the ages, all Heavenly Daos have basically been anomalies, and geniuses and anomalies are sometimes equivalent.

And in the history of Heavenly Daos, Song Shuhang is an anomaly among anomalies.

Besides the ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’, Song Shuhang also possessed several other peculiar abilities, such as the secret appraisal technique and the dreamland skill.

These abilities might prove to be tremendously effective when dealing with ‘Immortal Sand Grains’.

“So, Senior White, you can rest assured about me,” Song Shuhang said with a handsome tone. “After all, I’m no longer the cultivation rookie I was a year ago.”

“Yes, you are now a Heavenly Dao,” Senior White chuckled.

A year ago, those fellow friends who had beaten you or won over you in some aspects and were still alive could brag about it for a lifetime.

“So, Senior White, you can detach yourself with peace of mind and not worry about me. If necessary in the future, I can also catch up quickly,” Song Shuhang said.

He was trying to dispel Senior White’s concerns, allowing Senior White to fully detach with peace of mind.

Just as Song Shuhang finished speaking...

Suddenly, heaven and earth resonated.

The rules of the Heavenly Dao operated.

In the main world, at Earth’s location.

Senior Yellow Mountain, who was contemplating and deducing cultivation techniques for Doudou, suddenly shone brightly.

Between heaven and earth, a mighty power blessed him.

Senior Yellow Mountain was utterly bewildered: “???”

What happened?

What have I done?

This mighty power seemed like a blessing mark, and also... like a recognition title granted by the laws of the heavenly earth?

Venerable Yellow Mountain could feel that with this recognition title, the heavenly tribulation would show him sufficient respect when he faced his future tribulations.

“What is this?” Senior Yellow Mountain softly touched his own body.

Moments later, a realization surged in his heart.

The blessing he had received was named “Heavenly Path of Tyrannical Song Respects Senior.”

This blessing was automatically granted by the regulation of the Heavenly Dao after Song Shuhang, who had just proved his Dao, openly acknowledged and genuinely addressed them as ‘seniors.’

The Heavenly Dao acknowledged them as ‘seniors.’ Would any existence in the myriad practitioners in the universe dare not show them respect?

Not only heavenly tribulations, but even ‘spiritual power’ during cultivation would also be particularly proactive and automatically converge towards their bodies.

Besides Venerable Yellow Mountain, other members in the group also received this blessing mark one by one.

Fairy Lychee, Seventh Cultivator of True Virtue, True Monarch Rain Moon from Da Luo Sect, Cloud Gauze Three View Moon, Northern River’s Loose Cultivator, Thrice Reckless Mad Saber, True Monarch Tyrant Flood Dragon, Su Clan’s Seven, Immortal Fortune Teller Copper Trigram, Fairy Dongfang Six, Medicine Master, Seven Lives Talisman... even Young Master Phoenix Slayer and Doudou had similar marks emerge.

After all, Young Master Phoenix Slayer and Doudou were once Tyrannical Song’s seniors, and this would not change.

Besides them, Su Clan’s Sixteen and Soft Feather, who had always been considered peers with Song Shuhang, also slightly shimmered, but their marks were not ‘senior.’

“Is this Song Shuhang distributing benefits after handling his responsibilities as Heavenly Dao?” Senior Yellow Mountain couldn’t help but smile wryly.

However...

A newbie who had just joined the group last year was now the Heavenly Dao.

Thinking of this, Venerable Yellow Mountain silently took out two pills and with a tilt of his head, swallowed them stylishly.

Inside the Heavenly Principle Dimension.

Senior White curiously examined the changes in the myriad practitioners in the universe caused by a single sentence from Song Shuhang.

“This is the regulation of the Heavenly Dao,” said Senior White, his eyes twinkling.

Then.

“One month, Shuhang,” Senior White raised his index finger, deciding, “Take ‘detachment’ as another ascend story. At your usual pace of advancement, reach the critical point of ‘detachment’ next month.”

Song Shuhang: “!!!”

Senior White, this is really asking too much, detachment isn’t as simple as eating or drinking, how could it possibly be completed in a month!

Chapter 3134: Chapter 3132: One year later, when I come out, I will discuss immortality with Tyrannical Song!
 

For myriad practitioners in the universe, the world had recently seen drastic upheavals.

From the time when Tyrannical Song repeatedly showed his divinity in front of the masses, starting with the Profound Sage Speech, the state of myriad practitioners in the universe began to run wild.

The Eighth Wielder of the Will, who felt like he could hold on for a few hundred or a thousand years more, suddenly collapsed.

Soon after, in a short period of time, Tyrannical Song, as a mortal, condensed the ruler of the Netherworld.

Then, seemingly out of nowhere, Daozi of the Ninth Heavenly Dao proved his pseudo-immortality, catching all the top Immortals off guard, their faces dumbfounded as they watched him succeed.

However, after proving his Dao, Daozi didn’t even last a month before he abruptly resigned, taking the achievement of the ‘shortest reign in the Heavenly Dao’ and began the transition of the Heavenly Dao Authority.

—The practitioners wagered that no one could break the achievement of the ‘shortest reign in the Heavenly Dao’!

Next up, logically considered the Tenth Heavenly Dao, Tyrannical Song and White both proved their Dao at the same time, a truly unprecedented feat.

[From the moment Tyrannical Song became active, a torrent of ‘unprecedented’ events began to emerge... even their final proving of Dao had to be out of the ordinary. Tyrannical Song, a man who exists to break the rules.] This was the impression that Tyrannical Song left in the hearts of Immortals.

And this impression was formed without them knowing that ‘Tyrannical Song’ had just started cultivation last year.

Otherwise, had Mama Yellow Mountain, who so coolly swallowed her pills, be the future of all Immortals in myriad practitioners in the universe.

...

...

At this moment, within the ‘Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation.’

Divine Whale ‘Senior Melon Eater’ was still desperately trying to overcome the Thousand Days Tribulation of the Ninth Stage.

Since Tyrannical Song and Senior White successively left the ‘Thousand Days Tribulation’ space, the Ninth Stage Heavenly Tribulation had stabilized and ceased to mutate or cause trouble.

A stable ‘Ninth Stage Heavenly Tribulation’ was not difficult for Senior Melon Eater to resist.

At this rate, in just over a year, it should be able to come out of the ‘Thousand Days Tribulation’ early—thanks to the mischief caused by Tyrannical Song and Senior White before, its tribulation time had been significantly reduced.

“Puff~” A column of water burst forth from Senior Melon Eater’s head, facing the Ninth Stage Heavenly Tribulation and dispersing it.

It leisurely swam around, contemplating in its heart: [Unknowingly, some time has passed since Tyrannical Song and Senior White left.]

[I was on tenterhooks every day when Tyrannical Song and Fellow Daoist White were around, fearing that they would trigger even greater Heavenly Tribulation Mutations. With my limited strength, I couldn’t protect them properly.]

[I had even hoped that they wouldn’t get involved in my tribulation and that they could exit safely ahead of time.]

[Now that they really have left, I find myself missing the days when they were around.]

[This whale is just sentimental after all.]

It was an old-hand at ‘principles of virtue’, representing law-abiding kindness.

A few months ago, when the still relatively weak Song Shuhang was swept into its tribulation, it risked injury to itself by working hard to set up a virtuous network to protect Song Shuhang.

However, as the Thousand Days Tribulation went on, Tyrannical Song and White successively departed.

[I wonder how Tyrannical Song and White are doing now. Ending the ‘Ninth Stage Heavenly Tribulation’ early, could it possibly affect the Tribulation Transcender Realm?] Senior Melon Eater thought as it slapped its tail, once again shattering the Heavenly Tribulation.

Speaking of which, I’ll be able to go out in a year.

By then, I should meet Tyrannical Song and Fellow Daoist White.

Perhaps at that time, I could discuss with them insights into the ‘path to immortality.’

Senior Melon Eater had within the ‘virtuous network,’ suspected to be left by the Will of the Heavens, a segment of the ‘Virtuous Immortal Path,’ and during this tribulation time, it had also been contemplating that path to immortality with slight gains.

And it also believed that given the innate skill and luck of Song Shuhang and Senior White, in a year’s time, they would already have ventured into the path of immortality.

For other cultivators, the mention of a year venturing into the ‘immortal path’ was beyond imagination.

But Senior Melon Eater had much faith in Tyrannical Song and Senior White.

Geniuses are always extraordinary.

Tyrannical Song and Senior White, especially Senior White, was the most special existence it had ever encountered.

Just as Senior Melon Eater was deep in thought...

Suddenly, a ‘blessing’ marking dance descended from the vacuum, directly passing through the Heavenly Tribulation Realm and landing on its body.

Senior Melon Eater shuddered, leaping out of the water with a splash.

“A Heavenly Tribulation Mutation?”

It was primarily because of the frequent ‘Heavenly Tribulation Mutations’ caused by Tyrannical Song and Senior White that Senior Melon Eater had become quite jumpy.

Any strange changes in the Heavenly Tribulation Realm would startle it.

The mark of blessing descended leisurely.

In the end, it split into two.

At the same time, the ‘content’ within the mark slowly began to emerge.

Vaguely, there seemed to be traces of ‘White’ and ‘Tyrannical Song’.

Sage Monarch Melon Eater looked utterly baffled, “???”

Could it be that Tyrannical Song and Fellow Daoist White are up to something again?

As it was distracted, the rhythm of its tribulation was affected.

More dangerously, at that moment, the heavenly tribulation had stored up a wave of spiritual energy, and a thick Ten Directions Extinction Tribulation fiercely slashed down towards it!

The Ten Directions Extinction Tribulation is a characteristic of the Thousand Days Tribulation, every ten days, as the level of the tribulation rises, it gathers strength for a Ten Directions Extinction Tribulation.

If this tribulation hit solidly, without proper defense, the consequences would be dire.

“Hold firm for me!” Sage Monarch Melon Eater instantly put up its defenses, steeling itself for the blow — at this time, it didn’t even have time to pay close attention to those two ‘blessing seals’.

Boom!

The magnificent Ten Directions Extinction Tribulation was about to hit Sage Monarch Melon Eater...

But just at that moment, it hesitated slightly.

Then.

The Ten Directions Extinction Tribulation began to divide itself.

It cruelly split itself into ten parts, weakened to ‘One Direction Extinction Tribulation’.

Then, these ten tiny heavenly tribulations lined up neatly and slowly headed towards Sage Monarch Melon Eater.

Boom!

The heavenly tribulation, weakened to one-tenth its strength, couldn’t even crack Sage Monarch Melon Eater’s shell.

A tremendous grievance!

At this moment, Sage Monarch Melon Eater actually felt a profound sense of grievance from the fearsome ‘Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation’.

Sage Monarch Melon Eater was stunned for quite a long time.

[Did the heavenly tribulation take the wrong medicine?]

[No, the heavenly tribulation definitely wouldn’t make that mistake, so the problem must lie with me... the two marks on my body.]

Only then did Sage Monarch Melon Eater have the time to closely examine the blessing marks on its body.

[Tyrannical Song, recognized by the Heavenly Dao as a friend.]

[The white-robed figure also recognizes you – very tasty.]

Sage Monarch Melon Eater was dumbfounded for quite some time.

In his mind emerged a giant question mark the size of Huaxia.

?

Tyrannical Song, Heavenly Path?

White, Heavenly Path?

Blessings from the Heavenly Dao?

Two at the same time?

Am I still half-asleep?

“Inner Demon Tribulation? Have I developed an Inner Demon?”

“That’s not right, I am currently a body of virtue, where would an Inner Demon come from?”

“Besides, the heavenly tribulation just now was giving me face.”

“To be precise, it was giving face to the blessing seal on me.”

“The only ones who could make the heavenly tribulation pay respects are from the Heavenly Dao, right?”

To summarize...

Have Tyrannical Song and Fellow Daoist White become the Heavenly Dao?

Chapter 3135: Chapter 3133: This is the Will of the Heavens’ Daddy!
 

Sage Monarch Melon Eater calmly thought for a moment.

Then, it condensed a claw of virtue and fiercely punched itself.

It hurt, it hurt immensely.

This was not an illusion.

“The information is too overwhelming, I think I need some time to download, buffer, organize, and accept,” Sage Monarch Melon Eater looked up at the sky, feeling like an ignorant melon-eating bystander.

Just a few months ago, Tyrannical Song was under its protection, barely enduring the ‘Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation’.

In the blink of an eye, he became the Heavenly Dao?

“When I was young, I fantasized about becoming the Heavenly Dao, but even my fantasies followed the basic law—cultivate for a thousand years, live for ten thousand years, then spend a few hundred to a thousand years competing for eternity with the immortals of myriad practitioners in the universe, step by step reaching the peak of the pyramid, and eventually proving the position of the Heavenly Dao.”

Reality indeed was more unbelievable than fantasy.

While it was speaking, the ‘heavenly tribulation’ in the sky seemed to be affected, starting to accelerate its pace and compress its process.

Mainly because Sage Monarch Melon Eater was a very special existence.

It not only had good relations with two Heavenly Daos, but more importantly, it had been eaten by two Heavenly Daos. There was a part of the cause and effect from Melon Eater in the ‘virtue’ of both Heavenly Daos—this was crucial, resulting in a huge resonance with the heavenly tribulation.

Under this deep entanglement of karma and mutual sympathizing, the heavenly tribulation gave Melon Eater discount upon discount.

After crazy discounts, the Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation thundered explosively. It appeared immensely powerful, yet the actual damage was pitifully small.

After the explosion process finished, following the discounts, Melon Eater passed the Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation within a few minutes.

The last wisp of heavenly tribulation stubbornly blew itself up into smithereens, leaving no residue behind, denying anyone the chance to collect ingredients.

Immediately after, Sage Monarch Melon Eater was kicked out of the ‘Ninth Stage Heavenly Tribulation Realm’. In a dazed state, it became the ‘Tribulation Transcender’ it had longed to become.

And in doing so, it casually also achieved the title of ‘First Tribulation Transcender of the New Heavenly Dao Era’.

Sage Monarch Melon Eater continued to look up at the sky, still in a semi-crashed state of mind.

Looking up at the sky, it vaguely saw Tyrannical Song and Senior White seemingly communicating and smiling at it.

After thinking for a long time, Sage Monarch Melon Eater took out a notebook and wrote down a title: “The Autobiography of Melon Eater—My Fellow Friend Suddenly Became the Heavenly Dao, Taking Good Care of Me, and I’m Still Panicked.”

After putting away the notebook, Sage Monarch Melon Eater continued to look up at the sky.

While looking up, it made another new discovery: “I just went through a Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation, and I experienced three cycles of Heavenly Dao reincarnations?”

Heavenly Dao resigned, Daozi ascended; Daozi stepped down, Tyrannical Song and White ascended; was there also a fleeting Heavenly Dao afterward?

So, it seems there might have been not just three cycles, perhaps even four?

This world is too insane.

The Chinese people really do themselves proud!

...

...

In the Heavenly Principle Dimension.

“There are some things you are powerless to do before proving your Dao. After proving it, you can finally resolve them,” Song Shuhang said with a smile, looking at the situation in the main world.

Senior White had set a time for him to attempt ‘transcendence and eternity’ in a month.

Although Song Shuhang was not very confident, since Senior White had spoken, he had to prepare for ‘post-future transcendence’.

After ‘transcendence and eternity’, theoretically, he could gain great freedom... but it was uncertain whether he could still freely use the ‘Heavenly Dao Authority’.

Therefore, before transcending, there were some matters in the main world he needed to lay the groundwork for, to take good advantage of the ‘Heavenly Dao Authority’ without leaving any regrets.

“Who’s next?” Senior White was very interested in the newly acquired ‘Heavenly Dao Authority’.

“Indeed, the seniors from the Nine Provinces Number One Group bestow blessings, but shortly, each of the seniors should undergo reinforcement. At the least, let’s bring them all up to the Nine Dragons Pattern level,” Song Shuhang suggested.

Initially, Senior White had reinforced him up to the Nine Dragons Pattern, laying the strongest foundation for his future cultivation.

Now that he had achieved the Heavenly Dao, it was natural he would not miss out on such an opportunity to reinforce the dragon patterns.

“There are also your disciples,” Senior White reminded.

“Of course, I won’t forget them... As their mentor, I can’t teach them much, but I can at least strive to lay a solid foundation for them,” Song Shuhang said.

As he spoke, he swiped his finger, bringing the image of the modern world – Earth, right before him and Senior White.

At this time, his disciples were still in Wenzhou City, keeping company with Tyrannical Song’s parents.

The monster bird Little Cai was cherishing the time, cultivating her saber techniques, with her saber intent being unfathomably profound.

Chuchu had already integrated her path with that of an ‘immortal chef,’ making rapid progress in her cultivation.

Joseph was also there, holding a ‘holy light blade’ of the Eighth Stage in a sealed state, currently sitting in meditation—the meditation technique was a ‘Holy Light Meditation Method’ given casually by Senior White Crane when it was in a good mood a few days ago.

“Actually, this little guy has quite remarkable innate talent for the holy light element... one could even say it’s stunning. It’s a pity he missed the prime age for cultivation by far, being almost fifty already,” an immortal secretly behind the scenes watching over ‘Tyrannical Song’ spoke out.

Tyrannical Song achieved an undying status, which meant that his ‘residence’ in the modern world would soon transform into a new ‘Holy Mountain.’

Thus, some immortal intentions across spaces were watching, waiting to see when this ‘Holy Mountain’ would form.

Observing the formation of a Holy Mountain also greatly benefits top-tier immortals.

“Being fifty years old yet still able to cultivate ‘holy light’ in such a short period, it’s really too bad that such a seedling wasn’t discovered earlier... Are there any fellow friends from the holy light element paying attention to his child? With his talents, his child’s innate abilities shouldn’t be far behind,” someone said.

“People have already been contacting his daughter secretly; by the time you thought of it now, you were already too late.”

“By the way, what are you regretting... Don’t forget, this little guy is a disciple of Tyrannical Song. What does missing the best cultivation age matter? Now his master is the Heavenly Dao, a trivial matter like the missed opportunity for cultivation is nothing to the Heavenly Dao. We should be envious,” finally, someone couldn’t hold back and reminded.

“My master is Tyrannical Song,” this statement, when spoken now, could break ten thousand laws with a single phrase.

As the immortals exchanged words.

In the vacuum, a will descended, and a mighty voice arose: “Little Cai, Chuchu... Joseph.”

“Disciple here,” Chuchu, setting down her kitchen knife, exclaimed with joy.

“Disciple here,” Little Cai and Joseph echoed, following Chuchu’s lead reverentially.

“I and Senior White have proven our Dao to be immortal, and as my disciples, you three also receive blessings from myriad practitioners in the universe. Now, I will set up nine layers of trials for you... After you breach through the nine trials, I will be waiting for you at the end.”

Song Shuhang chose not to brutally alter his disciples’ data directly, but instead, he opted for trials to maximize their potential gains.

Only through such trials could their will complement their innate talent.

The importance of will in cultivation was something Song Shuhang knew more than well—after all, he was the man who had endured the pain of myriad practitioners in the universe.

“Yes, Master,” Chuchu solemnly replied.

Being a disciple of the Heavenly Dao, this status was so immense it was suffocating.

And they could not disgrace this title.

Shortly after, a seven-colored radiance descended from the sky, showering upon the three of them.

This was the blessing given by Senior White.

Under the radiance, Chuchu’s body transformed back quickly, shifting to an alluring figure.

Little Cai’s monster bird body enlarged slightly.

Joseph was the most apparent; he reverted directly back to his youthful appearance. Although he didn’t exactly revert to ‘the prime age for cultivation,’ it was sufficient for him to participate in the trials set by Song Shuhang.

Some of the surrounding cultivators couldn’t help but shed envious tears.

This is the power of the Heavenly Dao Tyrannical Song!

Chapter 3136: Chapter 3134: I want the whole world to know that the Nine Provinces Number One Chat Group has been contracted by us!
 

“`

For practitioners in the myriad realms, this was the first time they saw up close just how immensely beneficial it could be to have the Will of the Heavens as their backing.

Previous Wielders of the Will might have had close associates too, but for some, the eras are so remote that verification is impossible.

The several generations of the ‘Heavenly Dao’ that are closer in time are somewhat special; after proving their Dao and achieving immortality, there have hardly been any tales of them becoming someone’s backing and bringing them benefits.

Daozi Heavenly Dao is an exception, having a shorter term in office, so let’s set that aside for now.

The previous ‘fat ball Heavenly Dao’ appeared out of thin air. Practitioners across the realms couldn’t even determine its origins, a real loner with naturally no one benefiting.

——If it had been a ‘Confucian Sage’ who had achieved immortality at that time, perhaps a large group of Confucians would have benefited.

As for ‘Heavenly Dao White’ before that, he seems to have cared for very few people in his lifetime, and was quite busy after proving his Dao.

Maybe White-robed Heavenly Dao did have people he ‘cared’ about.

But White-robed Heavenly Dao experienced a long era, across two sessions of Heavenly Dao contention.

If the people he cared about did not step onto the ‘immortal path’, by the time of his second proof of the Dao, those ‘cared for’ would have vanished in the ruthless passage of time.

Mortals who are not Immortals have finite lifespans—after all, Immortals aren’t as common as cabbages, and a majority of worlds ‘across the myriad realms’ have yet to see an Immortal emerge to this very day!

Going back one more generation to ‘Daoist Priest Virtue’, there is even less need to mention.

By the time he became immortal due to a fortunate opportunity, he had already lived for an unknown number of years, and probably had very few people he cared about. Even if they did receive his care, they would not have caused a stir across all realms.

If we go back further from Daoist Priest Virtue... it’s almost impossible to verify due to the exceedingly distant era.

Therefore, the extent of the connection ‘I have the Heavenly Dao as my backing’ can go to, is something cultivators across realms could only speculate about in the past, rarely witnessed by anyone.

However, this generation’s ‘Heavenly Dao Tyrannical Song’ is very special.

He rose to prominence and came into view a few months ago.

After emerging, he made many good friends, took on disciples, fathered a daughter, and even seems to have maintained a relationship akin to ‘parents’.

Honestly, had we not seen Tyrannical Song beat up adversaries from all over and ultimately prove his Dao and achieve immortality... if you look at his network of relationships, it’s exactly like that of a cultivator who had just embarked on the path not long ago!

Everyone present, when young, had parents, dao companions, friends, disciples, children, and other close individuals like Tyrannical Song.

However, as time in cultivation prolonged, many friends and even descendants fell in the relentless river of time and disappeared without a trace.

Gradually, the network of relationships for Immortals became simpler and simpler.

...

[If only Tyrannical Song really were a special individual undergoing ‘Reincarnation Cultivation’, or had just stepped into the path of cultivation, we could establish a good relationship with him in advance, and then benefit from having ‘Heavenly Dao Tyrannical Song’ as our backing once he proved his Dao.] A young Tribulation Transcender lamented.

[By the way, have you studied Tyrannical Song? Before he became famous worldwide with his ‘Profound Sage Speech’, where was he cultivating? Which era’s expert was he?]

[Isn’t he the reincarnation of the Confucian Sage? I have some connections to Confucianism, and they have confirmed this news to be accurate.]

A group of top-notch cultivators exchanged information in secret.

Then, finally, one voice couldn’t help but say, [Actually, have you ever considered that Tyrannical Song might really just be a rookie cultivator who entered the world of cultivation last year, and then advanced one level almost every month, finally managing to achieve immortality by February?]

[???]

[Fellow friend, your fantasy is just too excessive.]

[Dreams should be had at night—dreaming during the day is just daydreaming.]

[How could there possibly be someone who advances one class a month in this world? The journey of cultivation is like rowing a boat against the current, one must proceed step by step. The higher the realm, the more difficult it is to advance. There might be unparalleled geniuses who manage to ascend a realm each month or in a few months during the early stages, but it’s absolutely impossible later on.]

No one was willing to believe what that voice said.

“`

After all, this claim is too absurd; even if you think about it with your toes, it still seems impossible.

A promotion to the next stage every month is something one might only fantasize about when young.

Only a few astute top cultivators paid close attention to the voice that had just spoken.

‘Is it the Almighty Merchant?’ the meditating cultivators thought with a start.

The ‘Almighty Seller’ Senior is a famous existence throughout the myriad practitioners in the universe, and almost no one would be his enemy, after all, there’s hardly anything he can’t procure, and his network of relationships is widespread.

With the relationship network and intelligence of the Almighty Seller Senior... his words are worth pondering.

[If... if Tyrannical Song really did advance one stage per month as the senior said...]

[Then it seems, many mysteries can truly be answered. For instance, why he still has ‘parents’ in the flesh, why he has made so many friends, and why his network of interpersonal relationships is so intricate.]

[But, advancing one stage every month is too ridiculous... perhaps there is some other karmic reason?]

While these meticulous cultivators were secretly communicating, a ‘blessing’ suddenly fell from the vacuum.

In the end, it landed on the head of the ‘Almighty Seller’ Senior.

Everyone was already quite familiar with this process.

It was recognition from Heavenly Dao Tyrannical Song.

[Although you have blocked me, you are forever a great senior in my heart—Heavenly Dao Tyrannical Song.]

This blessing title was especially long.

But it represented that Heavenly Dao Tyrannical Song acknowledged the intimate relationship with the ‘Almighty Seller’ Senior.

Doesn’t that indirectly suggest that what the Almighty Seller Senior said could very well be true?

[Should we go investigate it?]

[Tyrannical Song of the Heavenly Dao doesn’t seem to mind others probing into his past, nor has he stopped the Almighty Seller Senior from divulging his history. So, investigating Tyrannical Song’s past might be within the realm of what the Heavenly Dao permits?]

[As long as we don’t recklessly dig into Tyrannical Song’s private and dark history, but just plainly investigate his cultivation speed, it should be no problem, we can try it. If the Heavenly Dao shows any reaction, we’ll immediately stop.]

A group of curious cultivators stirred with eagerness, quietly communicating amongst themselves.

The Almighty Merchant looked up at the sky, his gaze landing on the ‘Heavenly Dao Certification Mark’ that evoked complex feelings within him.

“Hey, once you really investigate Tyrannical Song’s past and confirm what I’ve said... your hearts will be just as complicated as mine, and you might even need to take some pills.”

This is the only thing I can do for you now~

It’s better to share the joy with others rather than enjoying it alone.

If I have to take medicine, others should join me, that’s only fair.

Having said his piece, the Almighty Merchant took out a bottle of pills—produced by the Yellow Mountain Family—and poured the whole bottle into his mouth in one breath.

Song Shuhang also acted on a whim, sensing the ‘Almighty Merchant’ and the secret exchanges of the top cultivators in the universe, he subsequently sent a blessing to ‘Almighty Seller Senior’ as well.

Regarding his past of ‘advancing one stage per month,’ he didn’t intend to hide it deliberately.

After all, he was now the Heavenly Dao.

“Who else is there to deal with next?” Senior White asked while drawing ‘Dragon Pattern Stickers.’

These Dragon Pattern Stickers are first drawn with ‘dragon patterns,’ and later, every member of the Nine Provinces Number One Group would have one or two applied to them, striving to bring everyone’s dragon patterns up to the First Class level with nine dragon patterns.

“Compared to drawing one by one on the spot, this is a bit simpler and more efficient.”

The monster tree Miruru was currently in the Dream Realm, brought there by Senior White to participate in the ‘God Creation Plan.’ Now, she has a symbiotic relationship with the ‘World Tree of the Dream Realm.’

Given enough time to grow, she could become the spokesperson of the Dream Realm, the daughter of the World Tree.

Dream Realm.

At the base of the World Tree, a tiny sapling struggled to reach immortality.

The little sapling only possessed a faint ‘consciousness’ and was still years away from evolving into complete wisdom.

Under the World Tree of the Dream Realm’s protection, no creature in the Dream Realm dared to harm her.

Today’s Dream Realm was as harmonious as ever.

Suddenly, a finger materialized out of the void, slowly touching the little sapling.

When the creatures of the Dream Realm, the dream demons, and the Inner Demons sensed this finger, they all prostrated on the ground, not daring to stir.

“In the name of Heavenly Dao Tyrannical Song, I bless you. From this day forward, your name shall be Miruru, and you will inherit my once-held dao name ‘Daoist Priest Wood,’ becoming a disciple under me,” the finger gently touched the little sapling.

This was the Heavenly Dao personally awakening a tree monster.

From this day forward, even if Tyrannical Song abdicated his position as Heavenly Dao, the effect of this awakening blessing would not disappear—unless the next Wielder of the Will found Tyrannical Song disagreeable and chose to erase this blessing.

However, if the next Heavenly Dao bore grudges against Song Shuhang, he certainly would have arranged Miruru’s affairs properly before stepping down, not giving the succeeding Heavenly Dao any opportunity to exploit.

With this touch from Tyrannical Song, a cute illusory sprite appeared on the little sapling, resembling a miniaturized version of Miruru from bygone days.

“Disciple Miruru greets Master,” the tiny illusory sprite gently hugged the Heavenly Dao finger.

She had a vague memory of her past life.

But she still remembered that she liked Profound Sage Tyrannical Song the most, had once asked Tyrannical Song for a ‘Sage Seal Signature,’ and eventually died under a heavenly tribulation.

Perhaps her greatest stroke of luck was meeting Tyrannical Song.

Otherwise, a monster willow like her, if dead under heavenly tribulation, would have no hope of living again.

And now, Tyrannical Song was proving his Dao and personally awakening her.

“Grow well, I will always be watching over you,” Song Shuhang said softly, and at the same time, he drew his hand across, and a small ‘liquid metal’ droplet fell next to the monster tree Miruru.

It was the ‘fat ball’ that had its consciousness erased and was reinforced by the authority of the Heavenly Dao. Although it was a small droplet, it could still transform into a cloak.

While it might not be as clever as the ‘Song Fat Ball Windbreaker,’ it was still a powerful Companion Magic Device.

After doing all this,

Song Shuhang’s will descended upon the ‘Black Dragon World.’

Inside the Black Dragon World,

Scarlet Pupil, after practicing hard, was lying on the bed, resting and meditating.

“Master?” he sat up and called out.

“Your brother, Black Pupil... yes, after your trial is finished, I will take you to see him,” Song Shuhang assured.

Black Pupil had been dead for quite a while, and being a creature of the Black Dragon World, even using Heavenly Dao authority to resurrect him would probably not be easy.

But... if one becomes detached, it’s possible to lock onto Black Pupil’s soul and let him be reborn with his memories through the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy’s ‘Reincarnation Channel.’

But now, his master had given him a firm promise, which meant his brother was alright.

The last one, ‘Scholar Kindheartedness,’ would depend on the fortune and karma of that little girl from the Beast Realm.

Sima Jiang, the Fengshou Express Delivery man.

He and Song Shuhang were also connected by ‘fate.’

The two boxes of medicinal materials sent by Soft Feather had been personally delivered by Sima Jiang.

Sima Jiang was positioned between the world of ordinary people and the world of cultivators, being a mortal himself but due to various reasons, had made contact with cultivators.

However, he had never crossed the threshold, failing to truly access the core of the cultivator’s world.

Being the Heavenly Dao, arranging an opportunity for a mortal to ‘make contact with the world of cultivators’ was not difficult.

Whether it’s a fortuitous encounter or an expert suddenly passing by and impulsively taking a disciple, anything could be arranged.

After today, the entire ‘Nine Provinces Number One Group’ will become famous across the martial world.

Chapter 3137: Chapter 3135: Do I, the Will of the Heavens Tyrannical Song, Have No Need for Face?
 

Cultivators’ Fifth Stage Golden Core Realm is a very critical turning point—since ancient times, there has been the saying, “A single Golden Core determines the Great Way.”

And what determines the quality of the Golden Core is the number of draconic patterns on it.

Theoretically, the more dragon patterns a cultivator’s Golden Core has, the better. More dragon patterns signify greater potential for the future, meaning one can go further on the path of cultivation.

It’s precisely because the Demon Emperor Hezhi reached the Immortal Realm with “eight dragon patterns” that he’s an inspirational figure in the demonic sects!

However, in the myriad practitioners in the universe, there is one ‘Golden Core’ that’s an exception... such as the extremely rare ‘patternless golden core,’ Song Shuhang presently only knows that the past “Seventh Heavenly Dao White” and Spirit Butterfly Island’s Soft Feather have patternless golden cores.

“In the Nine Provinces Number One Group, the seniors have at least the status of seven dragon patterns, and there are quite a few with eight dragon patterns. They are all top-notch in the world... This means that actually, every senior needs at most to stick on two more dragon patterns,” Song Shuhang said as he reached out and took a small stack of dragon pattern stickers from Senior White’s hands.

At first glance, there seems to be no difference between the dragon pattern stickers for the Golden Core; the first one looked just like a ‘dragon pattern.’

But if you examine them closely with ‘consciousness and mental energy,’ you will discover that each Golden Core dragon pattern actually contains its own universe, made up of different patterns.

Chapter 3139: Chapter 3137: Young Master Phoenix Slayer, hurry up and come down, if you’re late I might forget the lines!
 

“Not a fairy, so how can she be called ‘Mama Yellow Mountain’?”

Some cultivators of myriad practitioners in the universe, who are outsiders watching and enjoying the spectacle, feel touched by the title ‘Eternal Group Leader’, while also quietly expressing their thoughts in their hearts.

However, he dared not do so.

Mama Yellow Mountain held a very high position in his heart and was a senior worthy of respect. It was okay to occasionally cause Senior Yellow Mountain some liver pain, but absolutely not to cross the line—this was the unspoken agreement among him, Thrice Reckless Mad Saber, Senior Copper Trigram, Doudou, Young Master Phoenix Slayer, and several other members of the group.

It was this understanding that allowed them to be reckless without dying, living on until now.

At that moment, when Senior Northern River received the title, ‘Eternal Group Leader,’ he darkened in expression.

Now, Song Shuhang giving him the ‘Eternal Group Leader’ title, wasn’t this intending to make him sit in this liver-paining position forever?

How could this be acceptable?

The order of the Star Road was also the order of the members of the Nine Provinces Number One Group, whom Song Shuhang had encountered upon entering the world of cultivation.

Soft Feather was the first group member he had encountered in this world, the initial figure in the Star Road, and also one of the ‘guides’ of Song Shuhang’s cultivation journey.

Song Shuhang thought and guessed the reason for Soft Feather’s sudden tears.

It was probably the influence left by the Future Child.

—But it no longer mattered because he and Senior White had already proven their Dao together! The next step was transcendence!

Song Shuhang showed a reassuring smile and said, “Soft Feather, like Senior White, you have a patternless golden core. The Dragon Pattern Sticker is not needed for you. So, I have prepared a compensating spell for you.”

Saying that, Song Shuhang reached out and touched Soft Feather’s forehead, leaving a flower diadem on her brow.

This was the cultivation technique of the Overlord God Pillar, which he and Senior White had calculated and improved using the authority of the Heavenly Dao.

Cultivating to the eighth level and above, one could, through Song Shuhang as a mediator, summon the ‘Tribulation Transcender Pillar, Pillar of Longevity’.

Cultivating to the ninth level and above, one could even summon the ‘Heavenly Dao Pillar’!

This fun secret technique would surely be liked by Soft Feather.

—The best way to prevent Soft Feather from being influenced by emotions like ‘sadness’ was to let her find amusing things or activities.

Sure enough, upon receiving this secret technique, Soft Feather’s face broke into a brilliant smile.

This interesting secret technique piqued her interest.

She gently touched her forehead and giggled, “Thank you, Senior Song, I truly love this gift.”

Pear blossoms bathed in tears, she smiled radiantly.

“You are the guide on my cultivation path, and I could enter the ‘Nine Provinces Number One Group’ because of you. From the beginning to now, I am the one who should be thankful,” Song Shuhang said as he handed her a ‘Liquid Fat Ball.’

Each person got one; it was standard equipment, naturally not excluding Soft Feather.

They were tears of joy.

Each teardrop sparkled with delight.

Although Soft Feather didn’t fully understand, she still gently slapped his palm.

After the slap, her tears stopped instantly.

Even her initially reddened eyes returned to their naturally fair state.

Song Shuhang maintained his dependable smile and withdrew his hand.

—He had already received the wish of Future Child!

Rest assured and leave the future to Senior White and me!

No matter what kind of future it is, we will turn it around for you to see!

After the slap, Soft Feather’s figure gradually disappeared.

In the real world.

Saint Monarch Spirit Butterfly, who had been sharpening his sword and was ready to ascend to the Heavenly City with his mortal body to challenge the Heavenly Dao, silently put away his fifty-meter greatsword after seeing his daughter’s eye sockets return to normal.

In the scene where divinity is shown in front of the masses.

The ‘Dragon Pattern Sticker,’ which neither Venerable Yellow Mountain nor Soft Feather needed, actually had its first use for them.

Senior Medicine Master and Riverly Purple Mist had worked hard day and night and had finally borne fruit.

The man without despair is truly enviable.

Did I just make a silly suggestion?

“Do these dragon patterns differ?” Riverly Purple Mist asked curiously while choosing.

However, when scanned with spiritual consciousness, you will find that each dragon pattern conceals a universe within, each harboring a different design. Riverly Purple Mist gazed intently and indeed found different designs within these dragon patterns.

There were fruit designs, specifically one resembling lychees—perhaps prepared by Senior White for Fairy Lychee?

There were also designs of the Calabash Brothers, which is purely because Senior White used to paint Calabash Brothers for Song Shuhang so often that it became second nature.

There were designs of disposable flying swords—this was a specialty of Senior White.

There were also designs of divine and mythical beasts—however, since Senior White’s style leaned towards stream of consciousness, if his mood was right, he could depict them brilliantly, lifelike. But if his mood was off, the creatures he painted according to his fleeting thoughts would require closer inspection to barely make out the original form of the divine beasts.

Among the designs of divine and mythical beasts, recognizable at first glance were those of dogs, cats, creatures looking both like wolves and huskies, and designs of snakes or flood dragons.

These were likely prepared for the group’s Ah Cat, Ah Dog, Ah Wolf, and Ah Jiaojiao.

Medicine Master: “???”

Mountains, mountain peaks?

Clearly, these designs were the brainchildren of Senior White’s stream of consciousness when his thoughts were distorted.

“Let the BGM start!” Beside them, Song Shuhang snapped his fingers.

A blast of music ensued, both exciting and suitable for lovers, sounds of the Great Way mixed together...

In previous times, their appearance was limited to transforming into sounds of bells, flowing water, or Buddhist and immortal melodies.

But now, under the guidance of Heavenly Dao Tyrannical Song, various forms of ‘Sounds of the Great Way’ intertwined, forcibly orchestrating a lovers’ BGM.

However, they were rather fortunate, at least they weren’t treated as Heavenly Tribulation’s meal like Big Brother.

When the sounds of the Great Way resonated, cultivators across myriad realms could benefit and attain enlightenment.

This also constituted a small benefit Song Shuhang sent out to the myriad practitioners in the universe—it wouldn’t be fair to have everyone just looking upward at the ‘Nine Provinces Number One Group’ members receiving rewards and only being able to watch enviously.

If there weren’t some benefits, the audience’s time, which is also precious, might lead many to stop watching.

There had to be something enticing.

Amidst the BGM music, Senior White extended his hand toward the dantians of Medicine Master and Riverly Purple Mist, virtually pressing.

Two Golden Cores emerged.

The process was the same as when Senior White had painted golden dragon patterns for Song Shuhang.

Now, he used stickers.

In the Nine Provinces Number One Group,

Chapter 3140: Chapter 3138: So, Don’t Die!
 

“`

However, no matter how much Thrice Reckless Mad Saber urged, Young Master Phoenix Slayer had already stopped seeing.

He was no longer paying attention to the messages in the ‘Nine Provinces Number One Chat Group’.

After entering the ‘Divinity Platform’, Young Master Phoenix Slayer’s body instinctively sprang into action—he posed like a model under the camera’s lens, subconsciously adopting striking poses that showed off his most handsome angles to the camera!

Young Master Phoenix Slayer was considered quite the handsome man even among the ‘Nine Provinces Number One Group’, and had a small degree of fame within Earth’s cultivation world.

Centered around Earth, he even had a group of young admirer fairies.

How to display his ‘handsomeness’ without any blind spots had become his instinct, second nature to him.

“Senior Phoenix Slayer,” Song Shuhang called out to him, “Feeling nervous?”

“Do I look like someone who would get scared by such a small display?” Young Master Phoenix Slayer lifted his head with a dashing tilt, reminiscent of a shampoo commercial, his hair flying about elegantly and stylishly.

“But your palms are sweating,” Song Shuhang said bluntly, “As everyone knows, a cat’s sweat glands aren’t well-developed, and the only place they can sweat from is the pads on their feet.”

Young Master Phoenix Slayer’s stylish movements froze slightly—he almost wanted to lick his palm to check if he was sweating from nervousness.

Fortunately, at the critical moment, he restrained the impulse to lick his palms.

This was in front of myriad practitioners in the universe, he couldn’t let Song Shuhang lead him into a pit and damage his image.

“Aren’t you less nervous now?” Song Shuhang laughed heartily from across him, “Actually, once you get used to showing your divinity, you’ll get accustomed to it. Like me, after showing it seven or eight times, I can calmly face any stage setting.”

Young Master Phoenix Slayer: “...”

Do you think everyone can show their divinity seven or eight times like you?

“Should I choose dragon patterns, Senior White?” Young Master Phoenix Slayer didn’t want to be led by Song Shuhang anymore, and turned to ask.

“No need, no need, yours, Doudou’s, True Monarch Tyrant Flood Dragon’s, Cave Lord Snow Wolf’s, I’ve already prepared them for all of you,” Senior White said, squinting as he took out the dragon patterns prepared for the group’s cats and dogs.

“What kind of BGM do you want for your presentation, Senior Phoenix Slayer?” Song Shuhang asked faintly, feeling somewhat left out by Young Master Phoenix Slayer’s cold shoulder.

“I refuse!” Young Master Phoenix Slayer waved his hands continuously.

The BGM idea that Medicine Master had brought up earlier was too foolish. Each fellow friend getting their dragon branding could even trigger different BGMs; one or two was fine...but after many, it felt a bit awkward.

Song Shuhang withdrew his hand regretfully.

A few breaths later.

Senior White personally branded Young Master Phoenix Slayer with the dragon pattern, gently pressed his hand on his head, and said, “Cultivate well, Phoenix Slayer. I’ve experienced many farewells between life and death. In the past, every time I emerged from secluded meditation, I would always worry about hearing that a fellow friend had met a cruel death—but there was nothing I could do. Now, you all have the Nine Dragon Pattern... so, at the very least, aim for the Immortal Realm!”

Young Master Phoenix Slayer replied solemnly with his head lowered, “I will, Senior White.”

Senior White revealed a satisfied smile.

Beside him, Song Shuhang recalled the scenes soon after he met Senior White.

At that time, Senior White had a premonition and seemed to want to enter an extended period of secluded meditation, which was estimated to be several hundred years. At that time, Senior White had also said something similar to him—hoping that the next time he emerged from secluded meditation, he would still see him alive.

Senior White had experienced farewell of life and death many times, yet he had never got accustomed to it.

“So, don’t die, Senior Phoenix Slayer; you have to live longer than me!” Song Shuhang passed a ‘Liquid Fat Ball’ to Young Master Phoenix Slayer.

“Don’t jinx me, you are now the Heavenly Dao,” Young Master Phoenix Slayer responded coolly as he took the ‘Liquid Fat Ball’.

Whoosh—

The Liquid Fat Ball transformed into a white windbreaker, draping over Young Master Phoenix Slayer.

He turned around and stylishly waved at Song Shuhang, “Although you’ve surpassed me, as a former senior, We will not easily stop our forward march.”

In the past, some members of the ‘Nine Provinces Number One Group’ might have lacked a bit of ‘potential’.

But now, after the Dao Foundation Dragon Pattern was supplemented to nine dragon patterns, their potential had been filled to the brim.

The Immortal Realm...

Will become the goal for every member of the ‘Nine Provinces Number One Group.’

And this, this was also the fundamental reason why Senior White and Song Shuhang boosted the members of the ‘Nine Provinces Number One Group’ with additional dragon patterns.

Nine Dragon Patterns, Nine Stage prospects, pointing straight at the Immortal Realm!

“`

When Young Master Phoenix Slayer stylishly donned the fat ball’s windbreaker and waved his hand nonchalantly, a BGM played.

This was a BGM with a touch of sentiment amid its vicissitudes of life.

Under the moving sound of the Great Way BGM, Young Master Phoenix Slayer’s figure gradually faded.

After Young Master Phoenix Slayer disappeared, the next silhouette did not show up right away.

Under the watchful eyes of all, the Heavenly Dao Tyrannical Song seemed to be making some arrangements, ready to welcome the next member.

[Could the next fellow friend to enter be someone special? Or perhaps a very important person?] The audience from myriad practitioners in the universe wondered.

“Who’s next?” Senior White asked.

Senior White stroked his chin and nodded in approval, “If it’s Thrice Reckless, indeed, we should be on guard.”

The private communication between Will of the Heavens White and Heavenly Dao Tyrannical Song did not transmit outward.

However, in the main world, Thrice Reckless could no longer wait.

Within the Nine Provinces Number One Group.

“It’s my turn, right? Shuhang?” Thrice Reckless Mad Saber asked.

Why haven’t you pulled me up yet?

“After Thrice Reckless, it’s me.”

Some things, it depends on who says them—when the exact same words are said by different individuals, the effect can widely differ.

An ordinary person saying, “Come here, eat whatever you want,” and a doctor saying, “Eat whatever you want,” have entirely different meanings.

The same goes for Tyrannical Song.

The word “pregnant,” when uttered from Song Shuhang’s mouth, carried a particular authoritative and daunting effect.

The practitioners across the universe stared with wide eyes at the scrolling ‘show my divinity in front of the masses’ subtitles, speechless.

Big Shot Tyrannical Song truly was an existence that trampled the rules of ‘showing divinity in front of the masses’ underfoot.

Even after proving his Dao and achieving pseudo-immortality, he still wouldn’t spare this entertaining segment.

But—would you actually play an advertisement?

Don’t just talk the talk.

Will of the Heavens White seemed to have sensed the cultivators’ intentions from across the universe, and his heart moved slightly.

Then, he added a few small words beneath the subtitles written by Song Shuhang—[Golden advertisement spots for rent].

After some thought, he also included Venerable Yellow Mountain’s phone number.

In the main world.

Mama Yellow Mountain: “...”

He just couldn’t take any more.

Elsewhere.

Thrice Reckless Mad Saber’s fingers gently circled at his temple, and then, like a robot without any enlightenment, he began to recite the ‘words’ in his mind.

As soon as he spoke, what came out was the language of some unknown era.

To Song Shuhang, it was all gibberish.

This was a family of languages even Senior White hadn’t heard of – quite normal considering there were so many languages in the myriad practitioners in the universe.

He and Song Shuhang were now embodying the Heavenly Dao, and no matter what language it was, even if they had never heard it before, they would automatically comprehend the meaning after Thrice Reckless Mad Saber finished speaking.

The Heavenly Dao is the ’cause’ and ‘source’ of everything in the world.

Language is naturally included in this ‘source and cause.’

He was genuinely envious of Senior Thrice Reckless Mad Saber’s tongue, able to articulate such complex language sounds.

Back in the day when he was learning the ancient language, he had wished he could have surgery on his own tongue!

Obedient to the point of being distressing.

The speech delivered by Thrice Reckless Mad Saber began to be translated with the aid of the power of the Heavenly Dao Authority.

Meaningless syllables sounded out from the vacuum.

Chaotic and disjointed.

As if random words from a dictionary had been pulled out, scrambled, and combined.

“Interesting,” thought Song Shuhang.

His ‘Cultivation Chat Immortal Path’ activated.

All the words translated by Senior White were thrown into Song Shuhang’s ‘Cultivation Chat Immortal Path.’

His ‘Cultivation Chat Immortal Path’ was coded in the background by Lady Kunna of the Dragon Network.

As he had guessed.

Song Shuhang said, “The black-haired Fairy Skylark is being very cautious; it seems she’s deliberately avoiding something?”
