Every sentence relayed was encoded several layers deep.

The image in the projection showed a bustling world.

But not the ‘myriad practitioners in the universe’ as it is now.

“It’s the world corresponding to the era of the ‘Black Dragon World,'” Song Shuhang explained.

He had ‘seen’ this world during his time in the Black Dragon World.

Different in form, but the feeling of the aura was similar.

Song Shuhang had once seen an entire world collapse and a giant black dragon, carrying the last life seed, streak across the sky.

“The Ninth Wielder of the Will detached, and its era ended.”

There was no sound in the image, but it conveyed information to both Song Shuhang and Senior White.

Then, the bustling world in the image suddenly began to collapse.

Without any signs of collapse.

However, after the Ninth Wielder of the Will detached, they did not engage in a new divine battle to elect a new ‘Wielder of the Will’ as was usual.

The world simply couldn’t withstand it and was completely finished.

And this scene is precisely the message the ‘black-haired Skylark’ wanted to deliver to Song Shuhang and Senior White.

Today’s ‘myriad practitioners in the universe’ and the former ‘Black Dragon World’ are not the same.

But there are huge similarities in some respects.

The Ninth Heavenly Dao must not detach lightly.

Once detached, it could lead to the collapse of the world.

“If that’s true, then the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao really has... been working in vain,” Song Shuhang said aloud.

In other words, the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao doesn’t actually have to work behind the scenes on anything.

Just waiting silently would suffice.

Once the ‘Ninth Heavenly Dao’ takes office and then detaches as usual, that would trigger the collapse of the world.

At that time, the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao could re-emerge and implement its ‘Transcendence Method’ and reap the benefits?

Too hasty.

After all, haste doesn’t bring success, does it?

“But we are different,” Song Shuhang said to Thrice Reckless Mad Saber: “Senior White and I are two distinct entities proving our Dao.”

Even if one entity ‘steps down.’

There’s no need to worry that the myriad practitioners in the universe will collapse.

Another Heavenly Dao would continue to hold sway!

It’s just... the plan for both to transcend at the same time would have to be put on hold.

Before they could be certain that detachment of the ‘Ninth Heavenly Dao’ would definitely lead to the collapse of the myriad practitioners in the universe, he had to stay and keep a steady hold on this world!

Chapter 3141: Chapter 3139: Eternal Eighth God Plan and Immortal Replacement Plan
 

“Thrice Reckless Mad Saber, please inform Senior Skylark... We have received the message she intended for me and Senior White,” Song Shuhang spoke out, “Moreover, we are not the same as the Ninth God of the Black Dragon World initially. It merely freed itself from the seat of heavenly authority, whereas Senior White and I aim to go even further, to transcend eternity!”

The message that black-haired Skylark meant to convey to him and Senior White was likely advising them to act cautiously in their forthcoming endeavors, to avoid inadvertently causing the collapse of the myriad realms of the universe.

“Yes, don’t worry,” Senior White assured from beside him.

At that moment, Senior White had made the utmost decision in his heart.

—If the dissociation of the Ninth Heavenly Dao from its divine seat caused the world to collapse, then transcending even further might also likely induce cataclysmic changes to the heaven and earth.

So, he decided it would be best for him to stay.

Senior White was aware of his unique qualities in certain aspects.

If he were to transcend the Immortal Heavenly Dao first, leaving Song Shuhang behind, there was no guarantee that he could prevent a collapse of the ‘myriad realms.’

But, if Song Shuhang transcended first, he could ensure the subsequent safety of all realms.

Because, as long as he was here, it would serve as the strongest testament to ‘peace’!

This was something Senior White was very clear about in his heart.

He was humorously known as the human mascot of the Nine Provinces Number One Chat Group, a title he never took pride in.

So... it would be him to oversee the myriad realms.

And then, he would study a plan to let the cleaned-up ‘Fourth Heavenly Dao Shell’ replace him.

“With Senior White’s guarantee, I suddenly feel much relieved,” Thrice Reckless Mad Saber obediently nodded his head.

His words carried an implied message—that the previous guarantees from Tyrannical Song hadn’t been entirely reassuring.

After all, Song Shuhang’s standing in the group was roughly at the same level as him, Copper Trigram, and Doudou.

Perhaps due to being fellow sufferers, Song Shuhang immediately picked up on the undertones in Thrice Reckless’s words, “...”

“So, I’ll go back and relay this to Skylark,” Thrice Reckless Mad Saber stood up.

“Don’t rush, let me first apply the dragon pattern stickers of tsunami and waves to you,” Senior White stopped Thrice Reckless Mad Saber.

“There’s no need, Senior White, I’m quite alright as is,” Thrice Reckless Mad Saber repeatedly waved his hands.

But who could resist the Heavenly Dao White?

Soon, two dragon patterns were added to his golden core.

And Heavenly Dao Tyrannical Song also bestowed a ‘Liquid Fat Ball’ on the side.

The whole process was like presenting a certificate plus a trophy.

After completing the procedure, Song Shuhang gently tapped and sent Thrice Reckless Mad Saber back to the main world—without giving Thrice Reckless any opportunity to showcase himself.

Some viruses are best left to spread within the Nine Provinces Number One Chat Group and not infect the myriad realms.

After seeing off Thrice Reckless Mad Saber.

“Who’s next?” Senior White asked.

“Um... Who was it again?” Song Shuhang also paused.

He entered an inner sight state, examining the star road map on his fat whale golden core.

At that moment, the message from black-haired Skylark, transmitted through the ‘Cultivator Chat System,’ had some additional content.

This portion was clearly intended to ‘avoid Thrice Reckless.’

It was content that black-haired Skylark did not want Thrice Reckless Mad Saber to see.

“Shuhang,” Senior White called.

“I see it,” Song Shuhang tacitly replied.

More content began to gradually emerge from the information left by black-haired Skylark:

[The departure of the Ninth ‘God’ will cause the world to collapse, the heavens and earth to lose order, leading to a complete reboot.]

[The Second God, possessing the divine authority to ‘divine the future,’ foresaw this possibility.]

[Subsequently, the plan to forge a pure ‘Immortal Replacement’ began.]

[Simultaneously, the eternal ‘Eighth God’ plan was laid out.]

[Eons passed.]

[The Immortal Replacement Plan continued until the world collapsed, yet it was still not perfected. The Immortal Replacement was not sufficient to bear the pressure of the Heavenly Dao role.]

[The eternal ‘Eighth God’ plan also failed to prevent the ascent of the Ninth God. The originally supposed perfect Eighth God held significant flaws, thus becoming the shortest reigning among past gods.]

As Song Shuhang connected this information with the intelligence he had, assorted thoughts raced through his mind.

The Eternal Eighth God? If he recalled correctly... The Eighth God of the Black Dragon World, also appeared to be a sphere?

Was the spherical god of the Black Dragon World pushed into proving its Dao by behind-the-scenes forces?

According to this theory, originally, the Second God might have aimed to build an eternally online, devoid of emotions, Eighth God to firmly occupy the seat of the Eighth Heavenly Dao, blocking the path for the Ninth God.

—As long as I live long enough, not to mention my son, even my grandson wouldn’t have the chance to inherit my throne!

Unexpectedly, the Eighth Heavenly Dao itself had defects; the ‘Eternal Eighth God’ plan did not succeed.

This scenario was somewhat similar to the experiences of the current Heavenly Dao in the main world.

Today’s fat ball and its corresponding heavenly authority also failed to perfectly prove its Dao due to its defects, and it didn’t stay in the heavenly seat for long.

“So, could the current ‘Sphere Heavenly Dao’ of the myriad realms also have been created to prevent our ascent as the Ninth Heavenly Dao?” Song Shuhang speculated.

“Hmm, possibly,” Senior White added, “But regardless, that’s all in the past now. We have already proved the Ninth Heavenly Dao, which is an unchangeable fact. Hence, we only need to look forward!”

“So, the other ‘Immortal Replacement’ plan... It must be Senior Skylark herself then,” Song Shuhang stated.

This answer was already quite clear.

Senior Skylark’s purpose of creation was to replace the Ninth God once it vacated the heavenly seat, becoming a ‘Substitute Heavenly Dao’, ensuring the continued stability of the myriad realms.

Yet, even with the successful creation of the ‘bone of eternity’, Senior Skylark alone wouldn’t suffice to act as Heavenly Dao.

—At the very least, she would need to achieve the state Song Shuhang had before proving his Dao, the ‘Full Body Semi-Immortal plus Perfect Immortal Whale Golden Core,’ to tentatively hold the position of Heavenly Dao and withstand the pressure of eternal power.

“Therefore, black-haired Senior Skylark conveyed this content to us... Is it because, with no choice left, she wants us to use her?” Song Shuhang guessed, deducing that these revelations came after Thrice Reckless had left.

“Skylark doesn’t know we possess a complete, pure ‘Fourth Heavenly Dao Shell’, so she must be considering this,” Senior White stated, “However... the original ‘Immortal Replacement’ plan is precisely what we need.”

He and Song Shuhang had originally planned to conquer this topic within a month!

Unexpectedly, a perfected plan had quickly come knocking on their door.

Chapter 3142: Chapter 3140: Live the Way You Like It
 

“It seems that I really have to meet Senior Skylark,” Song Shuhang said with a smile.

That feeling of ‘whatever you wish for will come to you’ can be addictive. Indeed, teaming up with Senior White was the right thing to do!

Especially under the premise that one has already become ‘eternal and Fearless of any disaster’.

Even if Senior White’s ‘seeking wealth amidst danger’ attribute was triggered, and getting what he wanted came with risks, it couldn’t possibly harm an everlasting being!

“However, what we need to meet... is the black-haired Fairy Skylark,” Senior White said, stroking his chin.

According to Thrice Reckless Mad Saber’s previous description, Fairy Skylark had already returned to her blue-haired mode.

For the black-haired Fairy Skylark to appear again, the current blue-haired Skylark would need to accidentally cross the ‘courting death’ limit and suffer a cruel death, entering resurrection mode.

Moreover, this ‘courting death’ limit had to be a ‘major death event’.

Ordinary ‘minor deaths,’ like dying from poisoning, getting shot in the head, or dying from sheer shock, would not bring out the black-haired Fairy Skylark.

—In the tumultuous life of Fairy Skylark, these ways of dying were relatively peaceful.

The black-haired Fairy Skylark generally appeared when the blue-haired Skylark was crushed to bits, dying down to the cellular level or even smaller units, and only then, through the ‘bone of eternity,’ entered the resurrection phase.

“That means, we need to let Senior Skylark die once?” Song Shuhang said, voicing a very cruel notion.

Senior White shook his head.

He couldn’t bring himself to act against a member of the Nine Provinces Number One Group.

Even if he knew that the other party had an eternal body, it was the same.

“I can’t do it either,” Song Shuhang said with a slight smile.

He could be harsh to himself, after all, a man has to be tough on himself. But he couldn’t bring himself to be cruel to a good friend who was also a senior.

“The reason I shook my head is... we are the Heavenly Dao,” Senior White said calmly.

This useful authority of Heavenly Dao should not always be overlooked.

As long as the Heavenly Dao is willing, there’s no need to let Fairy Skylark die even once, yet the black-haired Fairy Skylark could still appear.

Song Shuhang clapped his hands, “I almost forgot, I am the Heavenly Dao.”

He had just taken office; he was still not used to the reality that he had shifted from a ‘cultivator’ to ‘Heavenly Dao.’

“Then that’s settled, we’ll meet with Senior Skylark later.”

“Keep the live broadcast screen on the advertising interface for now.”

Senior White and Song Shuhang silently agreed.

Within the Nine Provinces Number One Group.

I noticed that after I returned from showing my divinity, there were 98 unread messages, but from the beginning to the end as I read, I only saw 94 chat messages.”

Among them, four must have been neglected.

Those neglected four must have been the scholar’s messages.

Northern River’s Loose Cultivator: “...”

Behind the scenes of the divinity-revealing.

Song Shuhang brought Fairy Skylark before him.

With blue-haired Skylark’s consent, Senior White exercised the authority of the Heavenly Dao to show black-haired Skylark.

The thick blue hair and eyelashes of Skylark quickly turned pitch-black.

“It looks like, my message, Fellow Daoist White and Song Shuhang, you already received,” black-haired Skylark said softly.

“Yes, Senior Skylark,” Song Shuhang said, “Senior White and I need the detailed original plan and operating steps of the ‘Immortal Replacement’ scheme.”

So, when it comes to that point, I hope you, Fellow Daoist White, and Song Shuhang will consider everything carefully before making a decision.”

“Don’t worry, Senior Skylark. We have better items to replace the heavenly authority in our hands,” Song Shuhang slightly smiled.

“Skylark, you don’t need to carry unnecessary pressure. You can live in the way you like, according to your own intent, and not as a part of the ‘Immortal Replacement Plan’,” Senior White said, and slightly showed the ‘Fourth Heavenly Dao Shell’ to Skylark.

Chapter 3143: Chapter 3141: Techniques that can Influence the Will of the Heavens!
 

“This is the spoils of war that Senior White and I, along with the Fourth Heavenly Dao, obtained after an unprecedented fierce battle. The Fourth Heavenly Dao is truly an incredibly powerful opponent, even capable of briefly reclaiming the Heavenly Dao Authority to confront us,” Song Shuhang transformed into the ‘black blower’ at this moment, extolling the strength of the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao.

When the black-haired Skylark saw the complete, pure, and unconscious Heavenly Dao shell presented by Senior White, she stopped thinking for a moment, her mind went blank, and she couldn’t say anything.

How did the white-robed figure and Shuhang come up with something ‘almost impossible to exist in the world’?

Normally, once the Heavenly Dao leave their ‘Heavenly Dao seat,’ their ‘existence’ becomes restricted, and they can no longer enter the main world—until now, people still have no idea where those ‘retired’ Heavenly Dao have gone, or where they might be hiding, whether they continue to pay attention to the main world.

In other words, encountering a ‘complete Heavenly Dao shell’ in the main world is almost an impossibility.

Moreover, the Heavenly Dao are eternal and indestructible.

Even the Heavenly Dao who have retired from their ‘Heavenly Dao seat,’ as long as their immortal shells remain, their consciousness is protected by the power of ‘eternity.’

Even the Heavenly Dao currently in office cannot erase the consciousness inside the retired Heavenly Dao shell!

Unless, the retired Heavenly Dao volunteered?

But how could there be such a ditsy, retired Heavenly Dao who would voluntarily erase their own will?

But the fact lay before her eyes.

What Senior White showed her was such a pure, unconscious Heavenly Dao shell. It was indeed a perfect ‘Immortal Replacement.’

There would be no better Heavenly Dao substitute in the world—because it was the Heavenly Dao itself.

“It’s fantastic, simply the most miraculous masterpiece,” the black-haired Skylark remarked with emotion after coming back to her senses.

At the same time, in that instant, she felt the ‘burden’ on her shoulder suddenly lifted.

It was as if she had become incredibly relaxed.

“I and Senior White are ready to tackle the challenge of ‘using the Heavenly Dao shell’ in lieu of the Heavenly Dao. Therefore, we need the detailed contents of the ‘Heavenly Dao Replacement Plan’ that Senior Skylark has,” said Song Shuhang.

“No problem, I’ll send all the steps of the plan to you via the ‘Cultivator Chat System.’ If you have any questions during the process, you can consult me at any time,” nodded the black-haired Skylark.

She bundled all the detailed content of the plan and sent it to Shuhang and White.

Having done all this, Skylark’s black hair started to gradually return to blue from the tips up.

After today, even the last mission that could give her a sense of ‘burden’ in this myriad practitioners in the universe was perfectly resolved.

She could live even more freely according to her heart’s desires.

—That said, she might be letting the giant turtle of disaster down; in the future, their workload would probably increase significantly.

After receiving the original draft of the ‘Heavenly Dao Replacement Plan,’ Song Shuhang and Senior White began to deduce it together.

“The one who conceived this plan, the Second God of the Black Dragon World, must have done more than just ‘deduce the future,” Senior White murmured.

“Could it be like the once white-robed figure who reached near-transcendence and directly spied into the distant future, even being able to affect it?” Song Shuhang speculated.

“It’s indeed possible,” Senior White nodded, “Overall, this plan has a very high feasibility rate. However, because the rules of the Black Dragon World and our myriad practitioners in the universe have some small differences... We need to rededuce and modify some minor details in the plan.”

“I will send this plan to the ‘Sage’s Eye Research Group’ so that the seniors can also assist in tackling it,” said Song Shuhang.

This time it should be the last time to ask the seniors to tackle a problem.

Once this topic is overcome, Song Shuhang should be able to graduate from ‘Heavenly Dao seat.’

Once successful, there would be no more topics for Tyrannical Song to delve deeply into in the myriad realms.

After all, other previous Heavenly Dao in this discipline could only be considered as dropouts.

Even Senior White could only be seen as ‘failing and repeating’ the course.

“Senior White and Shuhang, I wish you success,” the black-haired Skylark, slowly returning to blue hair, blessed Song Shuhang and White.

“Thank you for your kind words, Senior Skylark... We will definitely succeed,” Song Shuhang said resolutely.

Black-haired Skylark: “Since you’re all so confident, I can rest easy now.”

“Fairy Skylark... at the very end, I’d like to ask. When the ‘Black Dragon World’ collapsed during the Ninth God’s departure, did anything unusual happen?” Senior White suddenly brought up this question.

Previously, one could only see the Ninth God’s departure and the sudden collapse of the world... There were no signs of where the collapse originated.

“As for the source of the world’s collapse, I really can’t be sure. But if I had to offer a clue, the last time I died in that era, I vaguely saw an entity lifting the Black Dragon, making it the final land of hope. However, I have a feeling that this entity is also related to the world’s collapse,” the black-haired Skylark couldn’t be sure if what she saw last was real, and this was merely her speculation.

“Who does Fairy Skylark think that entity could be?” Song Shuhang thoughtfully asked.

An entity that both supported the Black Dragon and was the root of the world’s collapse was a very contradictory existence.

The black-haired Skylark shook her head: “Sorry.”

She couldn’t even confirm if her last vision was real or an illusion, let alone speculate the identity of that entity.

“No, Senior Skylark, the information you’ve provided is already plentiful. We should be thanking you,” Song Shuhang assured. “We’ll take it from here.”

The black-haired Skylark waved at Song Shuhang and Senior White, her form gradually disappearing.

“Got any leads?” Senior White inquired.

“Mm, if that ‘entity’ is not just an illusion of Senior Skylark, then its identity is quite deducible,” Song Shuhang analyzed. “Senior Skylark is a masterpiece of the Second God. That is, she has experienced all ‘Gods’ from the Second to the Ninth. Yet, that ‘entity’ is someone that Senior Skylark doesn’t recognize.”

“So, it’s the First God,” Senior White nodded, his conjecture aligning with Song Shuhang’s.

Song Shuhang continued, “If we were to compare it to our ‘myriad practitioners in the universe’... it would be the First Heavenly Dao!”

Compared to the Black Dragon World, their First Heavenly Dao was clearly more troublesome.

Because there were no records, data, or traces of the First Heavenly Dao.

Everything had been erased, completely wiped clean.

It was even uncertain whether the ‘First Heavenly Dao’ had graduated from the seat of the Heavenly Dao.

“Knowing this possibility, we just need to be a little more cautious. As long as we don’t give the other party a chance to show up, we’ll ensure the ‘Ninth Heavenly Dao’ continues to exist,” Senior White summarized. “Besides, we have a two against one advantage.”

The proposal put forth by white-robed figure—’two Heavenly Dao proving their Dao at the same time’—could almost perfectly face many challenges.

“It’s not just two against one; it could be three against one, or even four against one,” Song Shuhang chuckled.

The ‘Imperial Dragon Robe’ cleansed by the white-robed figure.

The ‘Immortal Shell’ in the main world.

If used well, each of them could play a role in a conflict at the ‘Heavenly Axiom-level’.

...

In the Nine Provinces Number One Group.

“Thrice Reckless, is Skylark back?” Northern River’s Loose Cultivator asked.

They had just tagged Xuan Nu Sect’s Skylark, but there was no response.

“She’s back, just got back,” Thrice Reckless Mad Saber replied, as he wistfully looked at his Golden Core being upgraded to ‘nine dragon patterns’.

Nine dragon patterns were just too flashy.

Spirit Butterfly Island’s Soft Feather: “Sword Sage, are you there? Did you make it up?”

“I reply, can you all see it?”

Spirit Butterfly Island’s Soft Feather: “I think Sword Sage Senior must have ascended since he hasn’t responded.”

“The advertisement of ‘show my divinity in front of the masses’ has finally been removed... it looks like the gentleman is finally going to show his divinity. Shuhang, this time, has finally done humanly possible,” Northern River’s Loose Cultivator remarked with emotion.

“Scholar Daoist friend must be very moved, I’m gradually losing my impression of him, I hope this showing of divinity will let me remember him anew,” Young Master Phoenix Slayer nodded.

“How did you manage to each read a different wrong name, yet still carry on the conversation together?”

“Huh? The number of messages is off again; three messages have appeared out of thin air. Could it be that Daoist Sword Soldier hasn’t ascended yet?” Immortal Fortune Teller Copper Trigram had been paying close attention to this detail.

Spirit Butterfly Island’s Soft Feather: “@Tyrannical Song, Senior Song, Senior Song, don’t forget about Senior Soldier! (ง•̀_•́)ง”

“Don’t panic, I’m here!” Song Shuhang replied, “I was just deducing something with Senior White; we’ll pull up the scholar immediately.”

The moment Song Shuhang gave a firm reply, the scholar’s eyes moistened.

A short while later.

Cultivators from myriad practitioners in the universe, once again witnessed the scene of “showing their divinity in front of the masses.”

This time, the one ascending the stage was a very handsome and charismatic mister.

This mister possessed an elegant aura, like that of a noble orchid in a secluded valley.

He’s the type that leaves a lasting impression on people.

“Does anyone else feel this mister looks familiar, as if we get the chance to see him every month?”

“Is he a Confucian mister? Such a refined temperament, he must be a good choice for a dao companion, right?”

“For cultivators, outer beauty isn’t the true measure of beauty. What truly matters is the aura, and this mister has the elegance of a hermit in the deep mountains, truly worthy of being a friend of Tyrannical Song.”

Then, they blinked.

During the blink, it seemed as though they forgot something.

And they started repeating the lines above.

But deep inside, that strange feeling of familiarity grew even stronger.

In the void.

The scholar took a deep breath.

At this moment, the gaze of everyone in thriving in the myriad realms was focused on him.

[Look at me, everyone is looking at me!]

How wonderful!

There are some things that you don’t cherish when you have them. But when you lose them, you realize their value.

Like sunlight...

Like presence...

The scholar, in his youth, didn’t care much about ‘presence.’ Compared to the Cultivation Realm, what was presence worth?

Trading presence for powerful cultivation seemed like a worthwhile exchange to him.

But only after he truly began to lose presence bit by bit, did he experience the wonder of ‘everyone looking at me.’

Just being watched made him feel content.

Sometimes, the happiness of cultivators is that simple~

“Thank you, Shuhang.” The scholar sincerely said.

Having a friend who’s a Heavenly Dao is really great.

It would be great if I could ‘show my divinity’ every few days like this.

“You don’t need to be polite, Senior Drunken Moon; you’ve taken care of me before too,” Song Shuhang said with a slight smile—the scholar was a big spender who once frightened him, a newbie, with a huge phone bill that shook him to the core with its string of zeros.

The scholar stiffened slightly upon hearing Tyrannical Song’s thanks.

This stiffening of the muscles felt very much like ‘network lag, character stuck in a game,’ very apparent.

“Drunken Star.” The scholar turned his head and said bitterly to Song Shuhang, “I am Drunken Star, Shuhang.”

Could it be that even the Heavenly Dao can’t remember his dao name?

Does my stupid cultivation technique even affect the Heavenly Dao?

What about my future?

What do I do when I cultivate to the Eighth Stage Profound Sage or even Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender Realm?

“Senior Drunken Moon, wake up,” Song Shuhang reminded him, “Others may have forgotten your dao name, but how can you forget your own dao name?”

The scholar: “???”

“In fact, not long ago, you corrected someone else, saying your name is Drunken Sun, you said it yourself, I saw it in the group,” Senior White’s voice slowly rose.

The scholar: “???”

“Sun, Moon, Star? Is it a cycle?” Song Shuhang wondered.

Senior White said, “I think the scholar has simply forgotten what his dao name is... I even suspect that Drunken Moon might not be the scholar’s original dao name at all.”

The scholar looked up to the sky.

“Why don’t we ‘account reset and retrain’? With me and Senior White here, perfect cleansing of your cultivation to the initial state shouldn’t be a problem. Then, Senior, you can choose a new technique to cultivate. With everyone’s help and a foundation of the nine-dragon-patterned golden core, your Cultivation Realm will definitely skyrocket,” Song Shuhang suggested.

“Account reset and retrain, is it possible?” The scholar looked up, his eyes full of hope.

“Yes,” Senior White replied affirmatively.

For the Heavenly Dao, a mere nine-dragon-patterned doodle was not a problem; what’s more an account reset and retraining?

The scholar’s heartbeat began to speed up.

Account reset and retraining.

Moreover, the support of the Heavenly Dao was behind him.

A safety net in the form of the Golden Core with nine dragon patterns.

Plus, he retained all his ‘insights’ for breakthroughs, so there would practically be no bottlenecks in cultivation. With this, he could cultivate extremely rapidly; reaching the Seventh Stage Venerable Realm might only take a few decades...

The scholar couldn’t help but be moved.

He opened his mouth and was about to say “yes.”

But for some reason, the word just wouldn’t come out of his throat.

Because, at the last moment, he hesitated again.

After another long silence.

“Never mind.” The scholar sighed deeply, “This is my path, my own choice.”

As he made up his mind.

The next moment, his realm broke through the bottleneck of the Seventh Stage Venerable Realm and advanced to the Eighth Stage Profound Saint.

The heavenly tribulation descended.

With the permissions of Song Shuhang and White, the tribulation pulled the scholar into the space.

Senior White and Song Shuhang silently watched the Heavenly Tribulation Realm.

——Just now, Song Shuhang had an illusion. If he hadn’t brought the scholar to the position to show divinity, the heavenly tribulation might have ignored the scholar!

At the Eighth Stage, the scholar’s technique had an even greater effect.

As he was contemplating, suddenly, Song Shuhang was startled: “Drunken... what, Scholar?”

After the scholar advanced to the Eighth Stage... this time, even the Heavenly Dao was affected!

“No, there’s something very wrong with the series of techniques practiced by the scholar,” Song Shuhang said seriously.

Chapter 3144: Chapter 3142: I Know the True Dao Name of the Scholar
 

Before, he had not ascended to the position of the Heavenly Dao, which is why it was understandable for him to be influenced by the techniques of Scholar Drunken Something, even if only slightly.

But now, he was the incumbent Heavenly Dao, the ultimate authority dog of the myriad practitioners in the universe, the “source and cause” of the myriad realms!

There was no reason he should still be affected by the effects of Scholar Drunken Something’s techniques.

Yet reality was paradoxically bizarre.

Scholar Drunken Something, who was merely transitioning from the Seventh to the Eighth Stage, had affected him—the Heavenly Dao—to the extent that he couldn’t remember the Scholar’s dao name.

What level of defiance against the natural order would that technique reach if the Scholar were to ascend one more level and reach the Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender Realm?

Could even the “Heavenly Dao” forget this individual’s existence?

Perhaps even the entire “myriad realms” and “Heavenly Dao Origin” would forget this figure!

By then, the Scholar would truly become an “audience.”

An entity detached from the world, observing it in spectator mode?

A role that cannot be “observed” by others?

“If we follow this line of reasoning, Scholar Drunken Something’s technique seems to hold a very high status,” Song Shuhang murmured.

“It’s Drunk Star,” Senior White corrected as he neatly arranged a stack of “Dragon Pattern Stickers”: “Of course, it could also be other dao names.”

“Senior White, aren’t you affected?” Song Shuhang asked, puzzled.

“From the beginning, I was not affected by the Scholar’s techniques. I have always remembered his dao name... though he, himself, has changed it three times along the way,” Senior White said as he found a place to sit.

[Indeed, Senior White is still that one exceptional existence.]

[While Scholar Drunken Moone’s technique may be unique, it still can’t override the exceptionalities of Senior White.]

Now, the few most special individuals in the world all stood within his own camp, which was the most reassuring thing.

“Senior White, you mentioned Scholar Drunken Something earlier; what are the dao names he switched to?” Song Shuhang asked.

“Drunk Moon, then Drunk Sun, and now Drunk Star,” Senior White patiently explained to Song Shuhang.

“Drunk Sun, Drunk Moon, Drunk Star?” Song Shuhang’s eyes suddenly lit up: “Senior White, I get it, the true dao name of Scholar Drunken Something—Drunk Star!”

“Hmm... if you’re happy, then it’s fine.” Senior White settled into his seat and took out his tea set, readying the secret tea blend provided by Cheng Goudan’s Father and began brewing tea.

“Speaking of which, I have also cultivated Scholar Drunk Star’s techniques,” Song Shuhang said as he sat down beside Senior White: “But even if I pushed these techniques to the ‘Ninth Stage Tribulation Immortal’ level, I haven’t achieved the effects of the Scholar’s Eighth Stage.”

His Three Corpses•Self Corpse had cultivated Scholar Drunk Star’s techniques and had pushed them to their limits.

Currently, the Three Corpses roamed the myriad realms, becoming a part of Song Shuhang’s ‘Cultivator Chat System’, enhancing the effects of the ‘Chat and Path to Immortality’.

Song Shuhang had not retracted the Three Corpses. The Three Corpses were different from the light of virtue—once retracted after becoming the eternal Heavenly Dao, they would be utterly merged back by the ‘eternal’ power into the main body, unable to manifest again.

Thus, the current state of the Three Corpses was quite favorable.

“It may be a matter of constitution,” Senior White said as he handed a cup of immortal to Song Shuhang: “Some techniques require a specific constitution to be cultivated to the true extreme. If the constitution doesn’t match, even if one cultivates it, the effects will be greatly reduced.”

Even if Song Shuhang elevated the techniques to the ‘Tribulation Immortal Level’, the effects couldn’t compare to those of Scholar Drunk Moon’s Eighth Stage. This showed how perfectly the Scholar’s constitution matched his techniques.

“I’ll divert a strand of mental energy to monitor Drunk Star’s tribulation to prevent any accidents... and to observe the Scholar’s state. Maybe I can gain some insights from him,” Song Shuhang voiced his plan.

As he spoke, he willed it, and two strands of the Heavenly Dao’s intent descended on the ‘Eighth Stage Profound Sage Heavenly Tribulation’ world, quietly observing Scholar Drunk Star’s act of overcoming tribulation.

Song Shuhang had an intuition... that the Scholar’s technique might prove useful in the future.

For example, if he could evolve the Scholar’s techniques to their ultimate form and apply them to himself while using Cloud Gauze Three View Moon’s ‘Immortal Replacement Plan’.

Then, it might be even more beneficial for his ‘Heavenly Dao Graduation Plan’!

This was his intuition as the ‘Heavenly Dao’, not to be underestimated.

The intuition of the Heavenly Dao often foreshadows the future.

...

In the Eighth Stage Profound Sage Tribulation World,

Drunk Star Hermit was casually strolling through the heavenly tribulation.

He might be the most laid-back transcendee Song Shuhang had ever seen—well, aside from himself who had proven his Dao for immortality and Senior White.

The Eighth Stage heavenly tribulation was fiercely striking down.

Moreover, there were modern heavenly tribulation guided missiles performing a ground-sweeping bombardment on the space below.

However, the small space where Drunk Star Hermit was located always seemed to be ‘forgotten’ by the heavenly tribulation.

Sometimes, Drunk Star Hermit would deliberately crash into the location of the heavenly tribulation.

But the heavenly tribulation seemed to have ‘forgotten’ about that area, as if it were ‘an Eighth Stage Profound Sage Tribulation Space,’ stubbornly forgetting to drop tribulation bombs there.

The mere Eighth Stage level heavenly tribulation was completely influenced and distorted by the effects of Drunk Star Hermit’s technique.

If this continued, Drunk Star Hermit’s transcendence of the tribulation would be utterly effortless.

One of Song Shuhang’s Heavenly Dao intents nodded slightly, then began to deliberately record the energy fluctuations around Drunk Star Hermit.

So far, the effect of the Hermit’s technique could only influence Song Shuhang’s impression of the Hermit’s dao name; Song Shuhang could still ‘observe’ the Hermit as an individual.

Then, another of his Heavenly Dao intents quietly dragged away one or two helpless lightning of tribulation from the Eighth Stage Profound Sage Tribulation, twisted them into a giant dough twist, and forcibly pulled them out of the ‘Heavenly Tribulation Realm.’

Although drinking tea is not like drinking alcohol, it could still be paired with some seeds or peanuts... This heavenly tribulation dough twist, cut up, could also be make do with.

...

It seems Drunk Star Hermit’s heavenly tribulation would continue for a while longer—after he transcends it, he will truly ‘show his divinity in front of the masses.’

It’s just that, even the ‘Heavenly Dao’ would be affected and forget his dao name.

Song Shuhang could already envision the heart-wrenching scene of the Hermit ‘showing his divinity in front of the masses.’

Taking advantage of the Hermit still being in the tribulation phase, Song Shuhang started to re-summon the remaining members of the Nine Provinces Number One Group.

On the star road, behind Drunk Star Hermit’s figure was Fairy Lychee.

Fairy Cheng Lin had a twin sister due to an ‘accidental’ operation—Song Shuhang always held doubts regarding Fairy Cheng Lin’s ‘accidents.’

Fairy Lychee’s figure appeared on the showing divinity interface.

“Is it finally my turn?” Fairy Lychee looked towards Song Shuhang.

“I’ve made Fairy Lychee wait too long,” Song Shuhang said, learning from previous experiences, he asked ahead, “Fairy Lychee, how many dragon patterns do you have?”

Since she was ‘Cheng Lin’s little sister,’ Song Shuhang suspected that the Fairy’s qualifications should be at the level of ‘nine dragon patterns.’

But Fairy Lychee’s response was somewhat unexpected for Song Shuhang, “Eight dragon patterns.”

Eight dragon patterns?

Not nine dragon patterns?

“What’s with that strange expression, Shuhang? Eight dragon patterns are already pretty high, okay?” Fairy Lychee reached out to lightly pat Song Shuhang’s head a total of four times—she had originally subconsciously wanted to spin Song Shuhang with a ‘big windmill rotation.’

But midway through her motion, she suddenly remembered that Shuhang was now the ‘Heavenly Dao.’

To give ‘Heavenly Dao Shuhang’ some face, Fairy Lychee’s ‘big windmill’ was temporarily switched to four pats on the head.

Every cultivator in the myriad realms who was watching the live stream saw this scene.

—In the eyes of cultivators across the myriad realms, ‘Heavenly Dao Tyrannical Song’ was just a vague figure, and the ‘white-robed figure of the Heavenly Dao’ was the same.

This was a thoughtful consideration from Song Shuhang to avoid the impact of ‘Heaven’s Will’ on the cultivators.

“`

However, people could see that the vague figure was none other than “Heavenly Dao Tyrannical Song.”

This Fairy Lychee, she actually dared to directly touch the tiger head of Heavenly Dao Tyrannical Song!

“Indeed, having eight dragon patterns is already very powerful,” Song Shuhang said with a gentle smile.

Beside him, Senior White handed a cup of immortal tea to Fairy Lychee.

“Thank you, Senior White,” Fairy Lychee said, sitting down beside Senior White and holding the teacup with both hands.

As she savored the tea, Senior White used his Heavenly Dao Authority to restore her “Fifth Stage Golden Core Realm,” then took out the already-prepared “Lychee Dragon Pattern” to complete her set of nine dragon patterns.

After all was done, Senior White put the golden core back in place and restored Fairy Lychee’s realm to the Sixth Stage Realm.

During this process, Song Shuhang watched over Fairy Lychee’s aura change with great care.

The entire procedure seemed similar to the experience of Northern River’s Loose Cultivator and several other seniors who had their dragon patterns replenished.

However, if one were to follow the “strings of karma,” they would discover that another end of Fairy Lychee’s karmic strings was stirred as she completed her nine dragon patterns.

The other end of Fairy Lychee’s karmic strings branched out, connecting to two karmas.

One end connected to Cheng Lin, who had become fragmented and was still in the hands of Father Goudan.

The other end was connected to Senior Sister Ye Si, who, despite having pushed the “Scholar” techniques to their limits, could not hide her own information after Song Shuhang became the Heavenly Dao.

Sixteen and Senior Sister Ye Si were especially left for the last by Song Shuhang.

At this moment, as the strings of karma were stimulated, Senior Sister Ye Si opened her eyes slightly, looking somewhat baffled.

The response on Cheng Lin’s end of the karma, however, was more significant.

In the midst of violent tremors, the “fragments of Cheng Lin” held by Father Goudan began to merge piece by piece.

In the blink of an eye, they were restored to their original state.

“What a headache,” Cheng Lin muttered, massaging her brow after being restored.

Because she and Song Shuhang had not entirely separated.

Originally, according to the plan, she and Song Shuhang were to completely differentiate themselves by utilizing the karma of becoming “shattered to pieces.” Then, they would restore themselves as two individuals through “rebirth.”

That way, Cheng Lin would be Cheng Lin, and her karma could be distinguished from Song Shuhang’s.

But now, their plan had failed due to the triggering of the karma as “Fairy Lychee” was replenished with the nine dragon patterns.

Sensing that Cheng Lin’s state had been restored, Father Goudan tapped and cracked open the shell he held.

The freshly restored Fairy Cheng Lin had to face the person she dreaded most—Heavenly Emperor Da Da Zi.

At the moment, the Heavenly Emperor’s child looked at Cheng Lin with a smile that wasn’t quite a smile, making her scalp tingle.

Moreover, behind Heavenly Emperor Da Da Zi, there was karma belonging to “Song Shuhang” queuing up.

“Fairy Cheng Lin,” Fairy Cheng Lin looked up and addressed Father Goudan.

“Cheng Goudan!” Father Goudan responded to her enthusiastically.

“I don’t want to be human anymore,” Cheng Lin said earnestly.

Father Goudan: “???”

“Come on, Heavenly Emperor’s child. It’s about time,” said the newly-restored Fairy Cheng Lin, standing up without waiting to fully recover, forgoing treatment.

The Heavenly Emperor’s child did not immediately respond to Cheng Lin.

Instead, she sent a message to Song Shuhang, “Senior Song... I’m going to settle some personal grievances with Cheng Lin— I’ll be back soon.”

“Don’t go too far; you are both Father Goudan’s eggs,” Song Shuhang cheerfully replied.

Heavenly Emperor’s child: “...”

She stood up and gave Cheng Lin a slight nod.

—She, along with Cheng Lin and Song Shuhang, could be said to be the largest “fragments of Ghost God Cheng Lin” in the myriad practitioners in the universe.

Among them, the fragment that was Cheng Lin herself was the largest.

Furthermore, Cheng Lin possessed some information about the “Wielder of the Will Striped Dragon” that neither Song Shuhang nor the Heavenly Emperor’s child knew.

The Heavenly Emperor’s child stood up, and Cheng Lin opened a space passage ahead.

Both figures disappeared into the space passage one after another.

Behind them, Father Goudan gently poked his chin with dragon mustaches.

“Father Goudan, just letting them go like this, is that really okay?” the three-eyed young senior chuckled— your two eggs are about to explode.

“No worries, they’re not kids; they know the limit,” Father Goudan said softly.

With Cheng Lin and the Heavenly Emperor’s child left, Father Goudan vaguely sensed something.

“Myopic Love, your Heavenly Dao is the creator of the ruler of the Netherworld... You created the ruler of the Netherworld to serve as a ‘Dao Mark,’ right?” Father Goudan asked.

“Yes,” the three-eyed young senior replied, not very eager to discuss this topic.

“It might not be long before this function will come in handy,” Father Goudan mused.

Hearing this, the projection of Senior White two turned his head slightly to look at the white horse, which was grazing like an ordinary horse.

Feeling the gaze of Senior White two, the white horse lifted its head and grinned.

“Reincarnation is set for the Ninth Heavenly Dao, so... could the previous Heavenly Dao return?” Senior White two queried.

Other Heavenly Dao could return.

But Senior White two had a faint feeling that Big White Heavenly Dao might no longer have the chance to ‘return.’

...

...

In the live broadcast of showing their divinity before the masses.

Fairy Lychee, looking pleased, bid farewell to Song Shuhang and Senior White and disappeared from view.

Song Shuhang had a somewhat troubled look on his face.

Because... Song Shuhang had recovered ahead of time.

Headache.

Evidently, Fairy Lychee’s “eight dragon patterns” served as a trigger, likely intentionally left by Fairy Cheng Lin.

“Fortunately, I have now become the Heavenly Dao,” Song Shuhang mused to himself.

I’ve become the Immortal Heavenly Dao; am I still afraid of karma?

“Who’s next?” Senior White inquired.

“It’s Dharma King Creation’s turn,” Song Shuhang answered.

“If we’re going to bring Dharma King Creation onto the live broadcast... it would be best to bring Fairy Creation along too,” Senior White carefully suggested.

If they only brought Dharma King Creation onto the live broadcast, an accident might occur.

But with Fairy Creation there to assist, the rate of accidents could be minimized.

“Mhm,” Song Shuhang nodded.

Fairy Creation and the virtuous lamia were different; she could not be brought into the ‘Heavenly Principle Dimension.’

Now that he had proven his Dao, it was time to lend Fairy Creation a hand... to see what her wish was!

Chapter 3145: Chapter 3143: I Entrust Everything to You
 

Song Shuhang had originally thought that as soon as Senior Creation arrived, he would start a concert—because he saw the small trumpet in Senior Creation’s hand.

Even Senior White thought so.

Therefore, the two new Wielders of the Will had even built a stage for Dharma King Creation and were planning to bring out Fairy Creation—the true Sound of Nature—in order to neutralize the impact of Dharma King Creation’s Deathly Music on the myriad practitioners in the universe.

However, could members from the Nine Provinces Number One Group ever behave predictably?

The small trumpet of Dharma King Creation was not for singing, but for playing music.

And it was a very delightful song performed by a woman’s voice.

A true self-contained BGM effect upon entrance.

With this series of pleasant singing, Dharma King Creation, dressed as an elegant cultivator, gracefully arrived.

Song Shuhang was somewhat baffled as to what exactly Dharma King Creation was planning to do.

—Originally, he had been wondering if Senior Creation was going to hold a ‘concert’ on the spot, then he could assess the ‘damage’ it would inflict on sentient beings.

Then consider adding ‘Dharma King Creation’s Brain-penetrating Demon Sound’ to the Heavenly Tribulation Grand Banquet!

It wasn’t that Song Shuhang was heartless after becoming the Heavenly Dao; he was seeking to create benefits for practitioners in the universe.

He, Song Shuhang, had transcended so many heavenly tribulations, but the ‘sound tribulations’ within it were quite weak and far less stimulating than Dharma King Creation’s music. Moreover, transcending the ‘sound tribulation’ didn’t provide any benefits for cultivators themselves.

However, Dharma King Creation’s music, combined with ‘Fairy Creation’s Sound of Nature’, could strengthen the will of practitioners and reduce their Inner Demons!

It offered greater training than a mere ‘sound tribulation.’

It appeared more intense, but the overall danger was significantly reduced.

This was a hidden gift package that he, the ‘Heavenly Dao’ who was often tormented by heavenly tribulations, was secretly providing to practitioners in the myriad realms.

However, Senior Creation didn’t seem to plan on singing.

As the BGM came to an end, Dharma King Creation smoothly made his entrance and happened to arrive right before Song Shuhang and Senior White.

Fairy Creation also emerged alongside him.

After appearing, Fairy Creation stretched gracefully and skillfully floated behind Song Shuhang, entering pendant mode.

“Senior Creation, would you like to introduce yourself?” Song Shuhang spoke up.

—He was creating an opportunity for Dharma King Creation.

“That sounds good,” Creation replied with a slight smile, like a Confucian cultivator, refined and elegant.

Then he faced the practitioners in the universe.

“Fellow friends of the myriad realms, greetings. I am known as Dao Hua in the path of cultivation, and I’m pleased to meet all of you here.” Dharma King Creation greeted with a stylish bow, then continued, “I have a hobby in my life.”

[Here it comes.] Song Shuhang’s heart stirred.

“And that hobby is calligraphy!” Dharma King Creation continued.

Song Shuhang: “???”

In Tyrannical Song’s puzzled face, Dharma King Creation took out the paper and brush he had prepared in advance and began to perform his not-too-shabby calligraphy.

Members of the Nine Provinces Number One Group felt tingles in their scalps.

“What’s Dharma King Creation up to?” Young Master Phoenix Slayer removed the earplugs from his four ears.

Northern River’s Loose Cultivator wasn’t sure either: “A change of hobby?”

“Impossible, Senior Creation was still looking for me a while ago, hoping that I would collaborate with him for a concert,” Fairy Dongfang Six spoke up.

“Then what’s he doing showing calligraphy on the Divinity Platform?” Medicine Master voiced his confusion.

Fairy Lychee pondered and suggested: “Why don’t we @ a few ‘sick friends’ at this time, such as @Thrice Reckless Mad Saber, @Immortal Fortune Teller Copper Trigram, @Spirit Butterfly Island’s Soft Feather, @Doudou, @Young Master Phoenix Slayer.”

“Please don’t @ me, Fairy Lychee. By @ing me like this, you make me seem like a Thrice Reckless patient,” Immortal Fortune Teller Copper Trigram seriously voiced: “However, I think that Dharma King Creation probably just wants to ‘set up a persona.'”

Doudou followed up: “Set up a ‘skilled in calligraphy’ persona, concealing his true hobby. In the minds of fellow friends across the myriad realms who are unaware, leave a deep ‘first impression’... and then, get ready for next time.”

“It might not just be for the next time, but also laying the groundwork for the time after next,” Thrice Reckless Mad Saber spoke: “Knowing the Dharma King’s character, he might only reveal his true self after the Eighth Stage Profound Sage Speech is over and after collecting the power of virtue.”

True Monarch Yellow Mountain: “...”

Isn’t it good enough to just sing if you want to?

Why make it so complicated?

It’s precisely this kind of behavior that erodes trust between people, you know?

Inside the Divinity Show Space.

While Dharma King Creation was performing ‘calligraphy’, Song Shuhang looked up again at Fairy Creation.

Another ‘past obsession’ needing to be addressed was added to the list.

Pavilion Master Chu’s Crystal-clear Water Pavilion, the last of the thirteen Tribulation Transcenders’ lustrous scholar of Fairy Creation, the older brother of Scarlet Pupil from the Black Dragon World, Black Pupil.

Dharma King Creation didn’t open his mouth to sing until the last moment.

He came with elegance and left with style.

Fairy Creation did not leave; she chose to enter the ‘Sage Eye Golden Core.’

The immortal ‘Scholarly Sage’s Eye’ did not isolate Fairy Creation—just like the relationship between the virtuous lamia and Song Shuhang’s main body.

The original Fairy Creation had a part to do with guarding the ‘Sage’s Eye.’

One of the most reliable members of the Nine Provinces Number One Group, hand-in-hand with Fairy Sixth Cultivator of True Virtue... Seventh Cultivator of True Virtue!

The young little Guoguo, Shi, and Zhu.

Senior White had used a special method to store the ‘dragon patterns’ inside their bodies in a reserved manner.

He looked at Song Shuhang with hopeful eyes.

[But what kind of blessing would this little guy want?]

“I understand.” Song Shuhang laughed heartily and reached out to pat the young monk’s head, blessing him as he did so, “By the authority of my name, Heavenly Dao Tyrannical Song, I bless you, little Guoguo. From now on, in your cultivation journey, you shall no longer be troubled by hemorrhoids.”

“Thank you, Senior Brother Song, you’re the best,” little Guoguo’s face brightened with joy.

Many of the cultivators from myriad practitioners in the universe subconsciously touched the area around their behinds.

In fact, among cultivators, before reaching a certain level of strength, a significant number were troubled by hemorrhoids.

The event wherein Senior White and Song Shuhang announced to the myriad practitioners in the universe “The Nine Provinces Number One Group is under our contract” came to an end.

Following this.

The figure of Sixteen was transferred to the ‘main world,’ then appeared by Song Shuhang’s side through the ‘main world.’

The White Dragon wrapped herself around Sixteen’s neck, “I thought you were going to forget about Sixteen, Shuhang.”

“Sixteen is part of my nine dragon patterns,” Song Shuhang smiled.

He reached out to hold Sixteen’s slender hand, and at the same time, the other hand was held up flat, with the projection of a ‘golden lotus’ phantom emerging in it.

“Shuhang, are you and Senior White preparing to transcend?” Sixteen turned her head to ask.

“`

Senior White sipped some immortal tea at his side, revealing a tranquil smile and nodded slightly.

“What will the state after transcendence be like?” Sixteen voiced the curiosity and confusion in the hearts of the White Dragon sister as well as the pendants on Song Shuhang’s body.

“No one has truly transcended before, but according to the descriptions from Big White, graduates of the Heavenly Path should possess great freedom, not confined by any time or space. They should be able to appear at any time node, anywhere, soaring above the river of time,” Song Shuhang replied.

As he spoke, he reached out and handed the ‘projection of the golden lotus’ towards Sixteen’s chest–there, Tyrannical Song’s lustrous heart was beating powerfully.

Due to Song Shuhang proving his Dao and becoming pseudo-immortal, this ‘Tyrannical Song’s heart’ was subtly reinforced by the rules of the Heavenly Dao.

However, since it had left Tyrannical Song’s body before proving his Dao, it wasn’t considered part of ‘Tyrannical Song’s individual’ by the rules of the Heavenly Dao.

Therefore, this lustrous heart had not become immortal.

But it already possessed the potential for ‘infinite evolution.’

It was the prototype of the ‘bone of eternity’ or ‘undying fat whale golden core.’

As long as it’s nurtured, allowing it to evolve and perfect endlessly... In the future, Sixteen might also own an ‘Immortal Heart.’

Song Shuhang inserted the ‘projection of the golden lotus’ into the lustrous heart.

“This is the key to the ‘main world,’ with it you and Senior Sister Ye Si can open the main world anytime, coming and going freely. You can also use the method of the ‘Branded Wooden Saber’ to leave coordinates, appearing wherever you wish throughout the myriad practitioners in the universe,” Song Shuhang explained.

Sixteen paused slightly and softly pressed a hand to her chest.

The lustrous heart’s beating quickened slightly.

Inside the lustrous heart, it seemed as if another world had emerged–the main world, closely connected to Song Shuhang.

If one day all the myriad worlds were to be obliterated,

then the main world would most likely be one of the last refuges.

“The main world is all I have, everything I own, treasures, assets, it’s all in there,” Song Shuhang whispered to Sixteen, “Now, its key is in your hands.”

The White Dragon sister: “!!!”

The Tyrannical Song, after proving his Dao as pseudo-immortal, had truly opened up wonderfully.

Even she felt her heartbeat quicken at this flirtatious move.

“With the main world, your safety will have the greatest protection,” Song Shuhang whispered.

In the past, the main world could sometimes yield in the face of great enemies–not because it was weak, but because being affected by Song Shuhang’s rank, powerful beings could block and seal the space, preventing the main world from opening.

In truth, the main world was not weak; we must remember that at the Eighth Stage, it could forcefully open even under the seal of a Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender!

At Ninth Stage, it could even forcefully open under the sealing space of an enemy at the Immortal Realm!

In other words, it has always been forcefully opening spatial passages a level higher.

Weakness was simply an illusion!

It has actually been very strong!

And now, the main world’s master, Tyrannical Song, has proved his Dao to be pseudo-immortal, becoming one of the men with the most authority in all the worlds.

No one in this world could make the main world yield!

Even facing an immortal existence at the ‘Heavenly Dao’ level,

the main world could still activate protective functions, guard people like Sixteen, and safely transfer them into the main world to protect them.

Even if the myriad worlds collapse and all things fall, the main world could also be protected by Song Shuhang’s ‘immortal’ properties, ensuring complete safety!

Chapter 3146: Chapter 3144: Worldly Ties
 

The next day, February 16th.

After the grand actions of the Heavenly Path of Tyrannical Song yesterday, cultivators from all heavens and worlds had come to know of a special group called “Nine Provinces Number One Group” and had become acquainted with all its members.

Now, in the myriad practitioners in the universe, even those cultivators who might be face blind to “humans” forced themselves to memorize all the members of the “Nine Provinces Number One Group.”

—These were the targets protected by the Will of the Heavens.

They were not to be trifled with!

Should the opportunity to meet them arise, one must not make enemies, but instead try to make connections, to see if one could perchance rub off some relationships or the like.

And if one dared to dream a little bigger, one might even try to see if there was a chance to join the “Nine Provinces Number One Group” through the relationship with the immortal known as “Mama Yellow Mountain,” and enjoy the benefits of being shielded by the Heavenly Path of Tyrannical Song?

All the members of the “Nine Provinces Number One Group” had become desired individuals in the myriad practitioners in the universe overnight.

And after the grand actions of Tyrannical Song had ended... the myriad practitioners in the universe had also entered a period of stable development.

The “Battle for the Heavenly Dao” had officially ended.

The laws of the Heavenly Dao began to operate in an orderly manner.

Due to the absence of the chaos when the “Fat Ball” was on the verge of collapse, coupled with the incoming tide of spiritual energy, this era could be considered a golden era for cultivation in the myriad practitioners in the universe.

Immortals and Tribulation Transcenders no longer remained in hiding and would occasionally make an appearance, leave behind inheritances, or take away talented disciples they fancied.

Song Shuhang, Senior White, and the members of the “External Assistance Research Group” began tackling the final subject—perfecting the “Immortal Replacement” plan.

They hoped to fully unleash the effects of the pure physical body of the Fourth Heavenly Dao and use it to replace the “Tenth Heavenly Dao,” thereby creating the ultimate tool-type Heavenly Dao.

The entire research process was in full swing.

Members of the External Assistance Group threw themselves into the project with unprecedented passion and effort.

As for Tyrannical Song, who was now one of the Heavenly Dao, he was slightly distracted—he was still working hard to digest the principles and knowledge of the laws of the “Cause of the Fruits, and the Source of All Things,” and didn’t have many opportunities to contribute to this final research topic.

He had indeed been working very hard!

It was just that he had far too little time to study.

Moreover, even though he was slightly distracted... his distraction was not simply a blank mind, but rather he was dispersing wisps of his “Heavenly Dao consciousness,” wandering in every corner of the mortal world.

Firstly, to completely exterminate the “Stellar Destruction Virus” laid out in the myriad practitioners in the universe by the “Dark Big Shot,” ensuring that the virus had no chance of resurgence.

Secondly, it was to meet some people and see some old friends.

...

All Heavens and Myriads of Worlds • Shadow Realm.

Here resided an unparalleled Immortal big shot, the Sector Lord Ruler of Shadows.

According to Song Shuhang’s previous estimates, the Ruler of Shadows, with the added “sector lord authority,” might also have reached the level of a Confucian Sage or the Heavenly Emperor, just like Mister Tian Zhi of the Mo family.

A wisp of Song Shuhang’s consciousness quietly descended here.

Senior Shadow, the Ruler of Shadows, became aware of his arrival instantly and awakened from his slumber.

“It’s been a long time, Senior Shadow,” the consciousness of Heavenly Dao Song Shuhang spoke.

“A long time? Wasn’t it just a few months ago?” the Ruler of Shadows replied with a smile. “For us, it’s just a blink of an eye.”

As he spoke, a humanoid form condensed out of the Ruler of Shadows’ enormous figure, facing Song Shuhang.

“But for me, it was a grand and tempestuous half of my cultivating life,” said Song Shuhang, extending his palm to reveal a somewhat cracked magical treasure bracelet.

The special Secret Artifact “Shadow Sanctum.”

“I’ve come this time to repay the artifact owed to Senior,” Song Shuhang said, as his right palm began to glow slightly—the effects of the Heavenly Axiom-level “Saber-Nurturing Technique” spread out.

Under the formidable power of the “Saber-Nurturing Technique,” all cracks in the Shadow Sanctum were healed. Moreover, the quality of the magical treasure was elevated to another level; deep within the bracelet, a wisp of “aura of eternity” emerged in the form of Dao Trace.

“Unfortunately, even after ascending to the Heavenly Dao, I couldn’t gather all the spirit stones I owed to Senior. Now, I can only rely on some techniques and authorities to repair this magical treasure, as compensation to Senior,” Song Shuhang handed over the artifact.

“Compared to spirit stones, I prefer this upgraded ‘Shadow Sanctum’ bracelet,” said the Ruler of Shadows as he reached out to receive the “Shadow Sanctum.”

—

— But despite his seemingly steady exterior, his inner turmoil was so complex it defied description.

Waves overturning rivers, volcanic eruptions, tsunamis, doomsday meteorites... Essentially, any word related to disaster could describe the current state of the seemingly calm Ruler of Shadows’ inner world.

After all, to the Ruler of Shadows, the man before him had truly become the Will of the Heavens in the blink of an eye!

“If Senior likes it, that would be great. After all, even if I wanted to compensate you with a pile of spirit stones right now, I wouldn’t be able to produce them in a short time,” the will of Song Shuhang joked.

In truth, as the Will of the Heavens, he could certainly scan all the heavens and worlds at any time, find a ‘Spirit Stone Source’, and then mine it.

He could even use the authority of the Heavenly Will to command the spiritual power of the world and condense it into a Spirit Stone Source beneath the guidance of the Wil of the Heavens.

But that no longer mattered.

...

At the same time, on Earth • Jiangnan College Town location.

Another wisp of Song Shuhang’s consciousness was strolling near the Jiangnan College Town.

As he walked, the spiritual power in his vicinity became more concentrated, the grass on the lawns revived, branches sprouted new growth, and flowers blossomed during the chill of winter.

“Unknowingly, it’s been almost a year,” Song Shuhang’s gaze swept the surroundings.

Even though he was living here just last year, when he looks back now, this area feels both familiar and foreign.

After a short walk, he saw from a distance the monster willow Light Dance, rooted within the college town.

Light Dance was a pet collected by Senior White.

Logically, her share of ‘When one person attains Dao, their chickens and dogs ascend to heaven’ should have been given by Senior White.

But compared to Senior White’s ability to rear pets, his talent in pet care was seriously lacking. In Senior White’s heart, the presence of the monster willow Light Dance might be relegated to a ‘corner’.

If it weren’t for Light Dance’s ability to fend for herself, White might have accidentally cared for her to death.

Thinking up to this point, Song Shuhang smiled slightly, and this wisp of consciousness floated over to Light Dance.

At this moment, Light Dance seemed to be happily browsing an online shopping mall, adding one item after another to her cart, eager to clear the cart as soon as the delivery companies resumed operations next year.

She was so engrossed in her shopping that she didn’t even notice Song Shuhang’s consciousness approach.

After Song Shuhang approached, he discovered that Light Dance would occasionally open a ‘Dormitory Friends Group’.

Inside were Gao Moumou, Yang De, and Tubo... but there was no Song Shuhang.

In the group, Light Dance occasionally answered some of their questions, resolving their doubts about martial practice.

After the ‘Evil Spirit Event’ ended, Song Shuhang devoted himself to cultivation, leaving the matters of the current world for Light Dance to resolve.

Light Dance must have disclosed her identity to her roommates, but she still hadn’t given up on her goal of nurturing Song Shuhang’s three roommates into ‘homebody cultivators’.

“Thank you for your hard work, Light Dance,” Song Shuhang said softly.

The monster willow Light Dance, who was focused on shopping and nurturing her roommates, was startled and trembled: “A sick man in his death-bed shakily rises, as a hidden wind brings rain through the cold window!”

Song Shuhang: “???”

“It’s the venerable Tyrannical Song,” Light Dance said, relieved, and modestly added, “All of this is what a small monster should do.”

“For my three roommates, I hope you will continue to take care of them in the future,” said Song Shuhang. He took out four ‘Dragon Pattern Stickers’ and applied them to the monster willow Light Dance, boosting her to the level of a Nine Dragon Patterns Demon Pill.

He then left a blessing mark on behalf of Senior White for Light Dance.

Finally, he passed on the perfected ‘Thirty-Three Divine Beasts’ Technique’ cultivation method to Light Dance, for her to guide his roommates onto the path of cultivation in the future.

His three roommates had long passed the prime age for cultivation and were no longer child Daoists; achieving anything on the path of cultivation had been difficult.

— But that was in the past.

Now, Song Shuhang had proven his immortality.

His three roommates, who got along well with him and shared a compatible temperament, now followed the ‘My roommate is the Heavenly Dao’ protagonist template.

Age and the state of being a child Daoist were no longer obstacles.

If the Heavenly Dao couldn’t even change these small issues, what would it be called?

—

Song Shuhang secretly bestowed his roommates with the talent for cultivation, tuning their bodies to the “most suitable age to cultivate,” and left them with a small blessing.

Furthermore, with the monster willow Light Dance quietly offering guidance, they wouldn’t lack early-stage elixirs...

He had already pushed open the gates of cultivation for his friends.

He had even mostly paved the way for their future in cultivation.

As for their future achievements, that would depend on their own efforts.

After all, Song Shuhang couldn’t play the mother hen, unable to care for everyone every minute of the day.

...

In the Confucian world of the golden lotus.

After celebrating the New Year, Papa Song and Mama Song returned to this Human World Fairyland aboard an immortal boat.

In the Confucian lineage, the couple received the highest standard of treatment.

Currently, the Confucian disciples believe that Tyrannical Song is the “reincarnation of a Sage,” and the parents of that Sage are the parents of all Confucians.

Moreover, since Tyrannical Song had proved his Dao and become “Heavenly Axiom,” as his parents, they would receive the highest treatment wherever they went.

At this moment, by the lake in the world of the golden lotus.

Mama Song was leaning against a tree by the lakeside, resting with her eyes closed.

She placed one hand on her belly—though she had just recently become pregnant, her abdomen had already begun to swell significantly.

This notable change occurred the moment Song Shuhang proved himself as “Eternally Unchanging.”

From that moment when Song Shuhang formally proved his Dao, his parents who were closely related to him and the ‘sister’ in his mother’s womb were affected.

This little life, yet to be born, had already received blessings from all the practitioners in the universe.

She was Tyrannical Song’s sister.

Even before birth, she was one of the most revered and beloved beings in all the myriad worlds!

Far away, Papa Song, carrying the immortal fruits gifted by the Confucian lineage, approached with a smile, each step he took was elegant—”Virtuous Man’s Ten Thousand Mile Walk.”

As the biological parents of the “current Heavenly Axiom,” their physical constitution was no longer limited by age or vitality from the moment Song Shuhang proved his Dao.

The couple had begun to dabble in the pure Foundation Establishment cultivation techniques of Confucianism.

The Confucian Foundation Establishment cultivation method is one of the most suitable methods throughout all the myriad realms, especially the “Virtuous Man’s Ten Thousand Mile Walk” quick movement technique, which cultivates with every step taken.

As Papa Song was drawing near, Mama Song suddenly opened her eyes a crack.

“Awake?” Papa Song asked with a smile.

“Mhm,” Mama Song said softly, patting her belly: “Just now, it seemed like I saw Shuhang appear by my side, quietly listening to his sister’s heartbeat.”

“Maybe Shuhang really did come,” Papa Song said with a smile: “According to what the several ‘heads’ of Confucianism say, Shuhang has now proved ‘Eternity,’ and with all the myriad realms under his gaze, he can be omnipresent.”

Although he was still not entirely clear about the classifications of realms like ‘Heavenly Axiom, Eternity,’ Papa Song had somehow accepted the fact that his eldest son had ‘become a god.’

Just a few months prior, watching their son bring home one beautiful fairy after another, hearing about his pregnancy, and learning about his ‘cultivation,’ the couple was shocked.

Now, however, he could calmly accept his son’s deification.

The ancestral great heart technique was indispensable!

“The heads of Confucianism have all said that the child in your belly is invaluable,” Papa Song said, sitting beside his wife and handing over an immortal fruit.

“It’s a pity that Shuhang himself hasn’t left us with a child. I’ve heard that after reaching the Eighth Stage Profound Sage, one is almost sterile. Shuhang has now become an even higher ‘Heavenly Axiom’... The chances of us having a grandchild are even slimmer,” Mama Song lamented.

“No matter, we are still young. After birthing a daughter, we’ll have another son for Shuhang,” bragged Papa Song: “Whether I’m a grandpa or an external grandfather, I want the title!”

“Furthermore, there might be a turning point, right? Before Shuhang cultivated to the ‘Eighth Stage,’ didn’t he bring several fairies home? With so many fairies, we might have the chance to become grandparents in advance,” added Papa Song.

Not far away, a wisp of Song Shuhang’s consciousness showed an embarrassed smile.

Feeling unable to jump into the conversation where his parents were showering affection on each other, there was a subtle feeling of being excluded.

After watching his parents from a distance for a while, the wisp of Song Shuhang’s will quietly left, heading deep into the Confucian golden lotus world.

In that place, an extremely important ceremony was being conducted.

The resurrection ceremony of “Daozi,” the senior of the 8.5 Heavenly Dao.

Daozi’s resurrection this time involved cutting away all ties with “everything related to the Heavenly Dao” and resurrecting as the immortal “Daozi,” instead of leaving his position like the previous Heavenly Daos.

Song Shuhang’s will descended to ensure the safe and smooth process of Daozi’s resurrection.

With him supporting from the sidelines, it wouldn’t be long before an energetic Daozi would return.

...

Besides this,

wisps of Song Shuhang’s will drifted through several places within the myriad worlds.

In the Earth of the main world, in a hospital in Wenzhou City, Zhao Yaya had become a qualified doctor. Song Shuhang, watching from afar, this cousin who once cared deeply for him, extended his hand to bless her, altering her aptitude, and having his three corpses—Tyrant Kindness—to secretly guide her onto the path of cultivation in the future.

Aside from Zhao Yaya, there were several relatives and friends closely related to Song Shuhang whom his will passed by one by one, presenting them with a ‘chance’ for their future. Whether they could grasp the opportunity was up to their own choices. Even if they couldn’t, under the blessings of the Heavenly Dao, they would still lead a peaceful life.

Then there was a small tribe in the Beast Realm, where the will of Song Shuhang looked upon the kind young girl of the beast cultivators from afar. After a moment of thought, he decided to leave her with some ‘possibilities,’ seeing if he could guide her to become his last disciple.

In the main world, within a place full of resentment, a bald Western monk with hands clasped, was chanting scriptures, soul-ferrying resentful spirits. As he soul-ferried through kindness, a gentle palm from the vacuum blessed him and left him with a precious elixir—a pill capable of healing his master’s injury and resolving the ‘root cause’ of their ailment.

In a building in Jiangnan Town, two professors from Jiangnan College met for a meal. It was Professor Renshui and a seemingly stern Lecturer Smith who, unexpectedly, had become good friends. As Song Shuhang’s will passed by them, he lightly pointed and granted them a little blessing, ensuring they would live the rest of their lives free of disasters and diseases and slightly extending their lifespans.

Song Shuhang’s will wandered through the heavens, passing by one person after another.

Offering blessings, granting opportunities, or meeting face-to-face.

There were also those he merely glanced from afar before leaving—such as Demon Emperor Hezhi.

After a long while,

The wills of Tyrannical Song in the myriad worlds returned one after another.

The human affairs were over.

Song Shuhang opened his eyes, his gaze gentle.

“Is it over?” Senior White asked softly.

“Yes, Senior White, you know already,” Song Shuhang said somewhat embarrassedly as if caught daydreaming while everyone was working diligently.

“I’m also the Heavenly Dao,” Senior White said. The gaze of the Heavenly Dao spanned the myriad worlds, after all.

“How is the progress on the final topic?” Song Shuhang scratched his head and asked.

“The deduction is almost complete. Next, we need to run a few small experiments according to the data obtained and make the final revisions,” Senior White replied.

They had him, the last shred of consciousness of Daozi that was about to dissipate, and Lady Kunna of the Dragon Network, three ‘Immortal Level’ entities leading the endeavor.

Supplemented by big shots like Big White two, Little White two, Dark Song, Father Goudan, the three-eyed young senior, and fat ball as rulers of the Netherworld.

And the aid of tools like Reincarnation Blade Fairy, who could occasionally communicate with the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy.

With the brilliant help of Immortal personages like the children of the Heavenly Emperor, Pavilion Master Chu, The White Dragon, Immortal Fairy White Bones, Great Northern Emperor, and so on.

Plus, a Heavenly Dao Song Shuhang to fill in the gaps!

This ‘External Assistance Research Group’ was unprecedentedly powerful and extravagant, unlike any other in history.

With this ultra-luxury research team working together, there was hardly such a thing as an ‘unsolvable problem’ left in the myriad worlds.

What Senior White initially gave Song Shuhang a month to research was now seeing significant breakthroughs in just one day!

“It’s progressing this fast?” The idling Heavenly Path of Tyrannical Song was somewhat ashamed.

Therefore, he decided, “I’ll be the subject for the final experiment. I will cooperate with the Fourth Heavenly Dao’s shell to carry out the ‘Immortal Replacement’ plan.”

Song Shuhang volunteered himself. Although he couldn’t become a ‘researcher,’ at least he could be an ‘experiment subject’ or ‘research subject,’ contributing to the final studies!

That way, in the future, he could proudly claim to be one of the members who perfected this ‘grand scheme.’

After this plan’s experiment was complete.

The next step... it would be time to graduate from the Heavenly Dao seat!

Chapter 3147: Chapter 3145: Tyrannical Song and White, we are very enthusiastic about hospitality!
 

Tyrannical Song’s time always seemed so urgent.

Moreover, he was always eager to break various records set by the “myriad practitioners in the universe” and to create new ones.

Currently, the rather special records he held included: the Xuan Nu Sect’s Saint with the most divine appearances throughout history, the Immortal who had achieved immortality in the shortest time, the existence that had changed the path to immortality the most number of times, the first big shot to possess the ruler of the Netherworld before becoming pseudo-immortal, the first instance of two Heavenly Daos proving their Dao simultaneously... among others.

Most of these records were unprecedented, and it would be very difficult for any successors to follow.

Now, Tyrannical Song and Senior White were probably going to challenge the “8.5th Heavenly Dao” Daozi’s record for “the shortest-serving Heavenly Dao in history.”

Such a meaningful record was worthy of their serious attention.

“When can we start the experiment?” Song Shuhang asked aloud.

Lady Kunna from the Dragon Network replied, “If you’re willing, we can start now.”

“Is there something we need to prepare?” Song Shuhang asked, glancing at what was placed in the “Heavenly Principle Dimension,” the most beautiful work of art in history—the Fourth Heavenly Dao Shell after being washed pure by the sand of transparent crystal.

“There are a few things we should pay attention to,” Father Goudan warned. “For example, your Inner World, which is tightly bound to you. During the experiment, you’ll need to keep it tightly closed and not activate it, to prevent any data interference.”

“Received~ I will notify Sixteen, Senior Sister Ye Si, and Fairy @#%# to be careful,” Song Shuhang nodded and replied.
