“Also, before you prove your Dao, you received the ‘Overlord World’ sector lord authority. Just in case, you could choose a successor and temporarily transfer the authority of the ‘Overlord World’ to them during the experiment,” the three-eyed young senior also advised.

Song Shuhang’s “Overlord World” was special; it wasn’t one of the ‘wild’ myriad of realms, but a new artificial world created by Song Shuhang himself. Hence, even after proving ‘eternity,’ the authority of the Overlord World remained tied to him.

To avoid any possible interference, it was best to choose a successor to the Overlord World before the experiment.

“I understand. Just give me a moment,” Song Shuhang replied.

...

After a moment.

A thread of Song Shuhang’s will entered the ‘Inner World,’ gently brought out his daughter ‘little Lingxiao’ and Li Yinzhu, and took them into the ‘Overlord World.’

When Song Shuhang’s ‘Heavenly Dao will’ descended into the ‘Overlord World,’ every inch of the Overlord World began to cheer, as if welcoming the arrival of Song Shuhang’s will.

Members of the ‘original Limitless Demon Sect,’ who were developing the Overlord World, were moved and stopped what they were doing to welcome the arrival of Boss Song.

The disciples of the Limitless Demon Sect had mixed feelings at that time.

“My boss is the Heavenly Dao, yet we’ve been working for him for free, originally just for a ten-year term, but should we consider working for him indefinitely?”

Who would’ve thought that big shot Tyrannical Song would become the Heavenly Dao so soon!

The idea of working for the Heavenly Dao was something to be proud of.

Moreover, they became ‘under the Heavenly Dao’s protection’ members in some way.

Perhaps establishing an ‘Overlord Sect’ in the ‘Overlord World’ would also be delightful?

After his will arrived, Song Shuhang’s will blew into the ‘Overlord World’—suddenly, the spiritual qi surged, transforming into a holy land of cultivators, a human world fairyland.

A few members who were serious about their work received some rewards, entering into a state of ‘enlightenment’ granted by Tyrannical Song, breaking through their bottlenecks!

After doing all of this, Song Shuhang’s will gently set his two daughters down.

“Ah Song~” little Li Yinzhu rubbed her eyes and sat in Song Shuhang’s arms.

Xiao Lingxiao, whose lower half was still a mechanical egg, lay on top of Song Shuhang’s head.

The young Tyrannical Song, at this moment, enjoyed the happiness of ‘family happiness.’

“Which of you two wants to inherit my ‘Overlord World’ and become the second-generation lord of the Overlord World?” Song Shuhang asked.

After some time, when his disciples returned from their ‘trials,’ he planned to establish his own sect on the ‘Overlord World’ and lay down his lineage.

In this way, it would be more reliable to leave the authority of the Overlord World in the hands of his daughter or disciples.

Little Lingxiao shook her head; she was the ‘original Heavenly Dao successor,’ and her future progression would be very rapid, so the authority of the Overlord World was of little use to her.

Li Yinzhu looked at Song Shuhang and asked, “Does Ah Song need us to succeed the Overlord World?”

“Yes, exactly,” Song Shuhang replied indulgently.

“Don’t you want to save it for Ah Song’s sisters or children?” Li Yinzhu blinked.

“They aren’t fully formed yet,” Song Shuhang said. “Besides, I will make other arrangements.”

“Alright, if that’s the case, then I’ll take over the position of ‘lord of the Overlord World’ on behalf of Ah Song,” Li Yinzhu stood up, hands behind her back, putting on an expression of a little adult.

Little Lingxiao clapped her hands vigorously, emitting a metallic clang in support of her sister.

Song Shuhang laughed heartily, stretched out his hand, and lightly brought out his ‘Seal of the Sector Lord of the Overlord World.’

Under the control of Song Shuhang’s will, the seal split in two, forming two smaller seals.

One of the smaller seals merged into Li Yinzhu’s body.

After accepting the Seal of the Sector Lord, Li Yinzhu closed her eyes and went into a meditative state.

With the identity of the sector lord’s successor, the support of the power of an entire realm behind her, along with the identity of ‘Heavenly Dao’s foster daughter,’ Li Yinzhu’s future was like a thoroughfare of ten lanes, clear and unobstructed.

Song Shuhang set aside a forbidden area in the core of the ‘Overlord World,’ then took Li Yinzhu into it and left it under the protection of Three Corpses • Tyrant.

After all this, Song Shuhang’s will looked toward a certain area of the ‘Overlord World.’

There was the site of a prison.

It was built in imitation of the ‘Lock Immortal Prison’ from the Inner World—since ‘outsiders’ would not be allowed in the Inner World in the coming plans, those imprisoned in the Lock Immortal Prison were relocated by Song Shuhang.

Among them was Young Master Hai, who held the title ‘Tyrannical Song’s Life Enemy.’

But in the moment that Tyrannical Song proved his Dao, Young Master Hai had already given up on thinking.

...

...

Having determined the successor, Song Shuhang took little Lingxiao back to the ‘Heavenly Principle Dimension.’

“Seniors, the Inner World has been sealed, and the succession of the Overlord World has been determined. Is there anything else that needs to be prepared?” Song Shuhang asked.

“Wait a moment; I’ll also close the channel between your Inner World and the ‘Sinful Black Lotus World,'” Senior White Two said.

Everything was ready.

“The formation is set up properly. For the next step, Shuhang, you stand in that other formation. I’ll place the Fourth Heavenly Dao Shell in the formation opposite,” Senior White instructed.

“When was the formation set up?” Song Shuhang was startled.

Senior White chuckled, “While you were away, transferring the Overlord World’s authority to little Li Yinzhu.”

“That quickly?” The experimental body, Heavenly Dao Tyrannical Song, felt that all he had to do was lie down.

Indeed, proving his Dao with Senior White was the right thing to do.

There was hardly any difficult task that required his attention; he simply needed to lie down.

“[Next step preparation.]” Reincarnation Blade Fairy said, “[I’m in charge of recording the experiment’s status and data, and will make fine adjustments to the plan according to the experimental data later. Shuhang, you and little Sixteen start coordinating to resonate and enter the primordial treasure mode.]”

This task was one she had actively fought to take on—she wanted to watch with her own eyes as the ‘Fourth Heavenly Dao Shell’ was experimented on time and again, turning it into an unwitting tool of the Heavenly Dao.

At the same time, it was also her fighting for ‘benefits’ for her Su Clan’s fairy maidens.

As long as Sixteen became a ‘primordial treasure’ and entered the observer mode to witness the experiments of the Heavenly Dao firsthand, the benefits would be indescribable!

“Received.” Song Shuhang responded.

He happily communicated with Sixteen, and a strand of his intent first resonated with Sixteen for the ‘Divine Weapon Transformation’, then further resonated to enter ‘Reincarnation Blade Mode’, bringing Sixteen into the Heavenly Dao dimension.

——The ability of the Heavenly Dao to appear instantly anywhere in the myriad realms is just terrific.

Having authority really allows one to do as they please.

“[Shuhang, remember this during the experiment: this time you are just conducting an experiment, not actually transferring ‘Heavenly Dao Authority’, so when you get to the last step, don’t truly pass on the ‘Heavenly Dao Authority’ to the Fourth Heavenly Dao Shell.]” Father Goudan reminded him again.

“Got it, rest assured Father Goudan.” Song Shuhang replied.

Synchronization and detachment were his and Senior White’s goals—if that wasn’t possible, he was prepared to reserve the first slot of detachment for Senior White.

“[Everyone get ready, Reincarnation Blade Fairy will do a live broadcast and report the data to the group.]” Lady Kunna said.

“[Has Fairy Skylark entered?]” Senior White Two asked.

“[I am here.]” Cloud Gauze Three View Moon replied.

“[Are you in the black-haired Skylark state?]” Senior White Two asked again.

“[Yes, Lord White, rest assured, I won’t have any problems here, I’ll closely observe the progress of the plan.]” Cloud Gauze Three View Moon replied.

Senior White Two: “...”

When I get back, I’m gonna have to take out Dark Song Shuhang—this title of Big White Two is really bothering him.

“[The first experiment officially begins.]” Heavenly Emperor’s child tapped in the command.

The Immortal Replacement Experiment was activated.

The experimental subject, Tyrannical Song of the Heavenly Dao, and the Fourth Heavenly Dao’s Immortal Shell enter the formation.

Immortal fat whale golden core was ‘spat out’ by Song Shuhang first—Song Shuhang’s undying fat whale golden core has the same function as a ‘demon cultivator’s inner core’, which can leave the body in critical moments.

The ‘Immortal Replacement Plan’ from Cloud Gauze Three View Moon was based around the ‘bone of eternity’, unfolding around it.

Thus, on Song Shuhang’s end, the plan was also started with the ‘undying fat whale golden core’ at the center.

The White Heavenly Dao was in charge of overseeing the whole situation.

The laws of the Heavenly Dao, the data of the Cause of Myriad Fruits, enveloped Song Shuhang and the Fourth Heavenly Dao’s Immortal Shell.

Several breaths later...

The Fourth Heavenly Dao’s shell turned into an eternal Great Sun, radiating white brilliance.

On the opposite side, at Song Shuhang’s location, a massive vortex black hole formed, as if to swallow everything.

“[The first phase of the experiment is progressing smoothly; Tyrannical Song’s black hole frequency data and the Fourth Heavenly Dao Shell’s Great Sun light data are stable.]” The Reincarnation Blade Fairy was responsible for recording the data and broadcasting the live screen through Sixteen’s body directly to the ‘External Assistance Research Group.’

“[Does anyone see anything that needs to be changed in the first phase?]” Father Goudan asked.

“[No problems with the details; we can directly enter the second phase.]” Fairy Skylark responded.

“[I agree with Fairy Skylark’s opinion.]” After repeated checks, Lady Kunna also expressed her opinion.

“[White Heavenly Dao, how stable is the formation?]” Father Goudan asked again.

Senior White confirmed, “[It’s going very well, and... I feel it’s progressing smoothly.]”

“[Then proceed to the second stage, and try to transfer a portion of the ‘Heavenly Dao Authority’ to the body of the Fourth Heavenly Dao.]” Senior White Two stated with certainty.

In the experiment, Song Shuhang, following the hints from his seniors, began transferring a small amount of ‘Heavenly Dao Authority’—such as the ‘Divinity Sage Authority’ and ‘Heavenly Tribulation Authority’ operations he was familiar with.

The process of transferring the authorities went exceptionally smoothly—mainly because, at the last moment of the Fourth Heavenly Dao’s self-sacrifice, it was still in the state of ‘burning oneself and returning to the Heavenly Dao seat.’

That meant it maintained a connection with the Heavenly Dao Authority interface until its consciousness completely dissipated.

“[There are no abnormalities in the second phase.]” Reincarnation Blade Fairy communicated the data.

The entire experimental process brought her pleasure.

“[The third phase is theoretically about transporting the ‘Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao’ into a black hole, and through this ritual, swapping its position with Tyrannical Song’s, achieving an ‘Immortal Replacement’ effect. We’ll only simulate this process, don’t do it for real. Shuhang, pay attention to this yourself.]” Senior White Two reminded him again.

“[Additionally, Shuhang, you mentioned before... you can try to use that technique from the fish belly sword sage to reduce your presence. During the third phase, give it a try and see if it can make the ‘Heavenly Dao Replacement Plan’ even more perfect.]” The three-eyed young senior advised.

“[O an’ K, I’ll activate Drunk Star Hermit’s technique.]” Song Shuhang replied.

The third stage simulation began...

As the simulated experiment started, Song Shuhang vaguely felt as if he was about to leave the ‘Heavenly Dao seat.’

It wasn’t graduation but more like dropping out, similar to previous Heavenly Daos.

This was not the outcome he desired.

“[The third stage requires minor adjustments.]” Senior White, who was continuously observing the changes in the formation, advised, “[The desired experimental outcome we need is maintaining a ‘both Heavenly Daos in office’ mode. We cannot let Shuhang truly leave his position, but rather, continue to retain the state of the Heavenly Dao.]”

Lady Kunna of the Dragon Network ran through the procedure and answered, “[For that to happen, there is a prerequisite—that is, before this experiment begins, White Heavenly Dao, you must graduate first. Place the ‘Binds’ of both Heavenly Daos on Shuhang. That way, Shuhang can transfer a ‘Bind’ to the body of the Fourth Heavenly Dao. Finally, follow the ‘graduation’ channel of White Heavenly Dao and graduate again.]”

“[Hmm, with that, there shouldn’t be too much of a theoretical issue. We just need to adjust the third phase a bit.]” Senior White Two nodded.

“[Well then... let’s conclude the first trial.]” Heavenly Emperor announced.

Senior White nodded and began to adjust the formation and Shuhang’s state.

Song Shuhang and the body of the Fourth Heavenly Dao gradually disengaged from the experimental state.

A few moments later.

While still gradually withdrawing from the experimental state, Song Shuhang, along with Senior White maintaining the experimental formation, simultaneously turned their heads.

The gazes of the two Heavenly Daos, through the dimension of Heavenly Principle, pierced deep into the myriad practitioners in the universe.

Deep within the myriad practitioners in the universe, a ‘figure’ seemed to faintly appear.

This scene evoked in both Senior White and Song Shuhang the memory of the black-haired Skylark’s description of when the Black Dragon World was destroyed, where a mysterious figure had seemingly appeared.

The First Heavenly Dao?

“Did our experiment just now trigger the prerequisite conditions for the ‘Ninth Heavenly Dao’ to drop out?” Song Shuhang was stunned.

“It shouldn’t have... you are still in office.” Senior White responded.

While they talked, the vaguely appearing figure seemed to start fading again.

“[We can’t let him slip away!]” The thought simultaneously arose in the hearts of Song Shuhang and Senior White.

Come and now trying to leave?

Wouldn’t that make people think that I, Tyrannical Song, and White, are not hospitable enough?

Chapter 3148: Chapter 3146: Return of the Will of the Heavens
 

“We can’t let this ‘figure’ retreat!”

This intuition was not only a “Heavenly Intuition” but also originated from the “first response” of Senior White’s body. This response was then fed back to Song Shuhang’s brain through the direct connection between Senior White and him.

If they allowed this ‘vaguely flashing’ figure to retreat, it might affect their own and Senior White’s “Heavenly Way graduation” plan!

This was a dual warning of Heavenly Intuition and Senior White’s luck instinct.

Therefore, no matter who this guy was, whether or not he was the ‘First Heavenly Dao’, Song Shuhang and Senior White, without any hesitation, took action at the same time.

With just a thought, the space around that figure began to distort—under the gaze of the Heavens, the myriad worlds are exposed, and distance is no limitation for the ‘Heavenly Dao.’ With a mere thought, any corner of the myriad worlds could become the target of the ‘Heavenly Dao’s’ wrath!

In an instant, within the means of Senior White, the vacuum of that world was silently replaced by a desert, made up of vast expanses of yellow sand.

Beside Song Shuhang, he reached out with a flick of his finger, and pillars infused and strengthened by the Heavenly Dao Authority — the ‘Heavenly Dao Pillars’ — thunderously crashed down, nailing around the ‘figure’, sealing it within.

The ‘Dao’ and ‘will’ of the past Heavenly Daos turned into Heavenly Dao Pillars + the methods of Song Shuhang and Senior White could be said to embody the might of all the Heavenly Daos from the 2nd to the 9th editions!

“What’s happening?” Reincarnation Blade Fairy, taking advantage of Sixteen, broadcasted every move of Song Shuhang and White Heavenly Dao back to the ‘External Assistance Research Group.’

Therefore, this sudden action by Song Shuhang and White Heavenly Dao was also witnessed by all the group members.

The angle of Reincarnation Blade Fairy’s broadcast shifted, sweeping through the depth of the myriad worlds along the trajectory of Song Shuhang’s action.

—The next moment, a figure vaguely locked by the desert world and the Heavenly Dao Pillars appeared in the frame.

When Fairy Skylark saw this footage, she was spiritually shaken and posted a series of exclamation marks in the group: “!!!”

Just yesterday, she had mentioned the ‘potential appearance of a figure’ to White Heavenly Dao and Shuhang, and today, Song Shuhang and White Heavenly Dao actually encountered this figure!

“Who is this?” Daoist Senior, the last grain of Heavenly Dao consciousness, wondered.

Once a Heavenly Dao himself, Daozi sensed a familiar formula from this figure.

Was it the scent of ‘eternity’?

“Strange, if my sight shifts slightly away from him... my brain immediately forgets his existence. Even if I keep staring at him, I always end up inadvertently ignoring him.” The three-eyed young senior frowned, even though he had already activated his third divine eye.

But that strange ‘transparency’ was still affecting him.

If it weren’t for Song Shuhang securing the figure with nine ‘Heavenly Dao Pillars,’ they probably wouldn’t be able to set their gaze on him at all, and the eyes would likely subconsciously overlook this existence.

“Does Fairy Skylark know the ins and outs?” Big White Two asked aloud.

“I’m not sure if this ‘figure’ and the one that appeared in our Black Dragon World are the same. I only have a suspicion... This figure might be related to the ‘First God’ or the ‘First Heavenly Dao.'” The black-haired Fairy Skylark replied: “However, this is just my guess and should not be taken as fact.”

“Even if it’s not the First Heavenly Dao, it’s very likely still related to the First Heavenly Dao,” the three-eyed young senior spoke up: “This feeling as if ‘he doesn’t really exist’ is clearly related to how the First Heavenly Dao completely erased its existence, leaving behind only scant marks.”

“Hey hey, it might also be related to the Second Heavenly Dao,” Father Goudan chuckled: “Mirrored Eye Addiction, don’t forget... your Heavenly Dao did things related to the First Heavenly Dao before it resigned. It also erased the majority of its existence, leaving behind only a few marks.”

After pondering seriously for a moment, the three-eyed young senior replied: “Indeed... it might also be related to the corresponding Heavenly Dao.”

He didn’t refute Father Goudan because he was very aware of the unreliability of his own Heavenly Dao.

“Whether it’s the first or the second Heavenly Dao, what I’m more concerned about is why he appeared, what is his purpose?” Daozi, the last grain of Heavenly Dao consciousness, asked aloud.

“Perhaps, it’s to bring an end to this world. Our experiment just now might have already touched on the conditions for the ‘Ninth Heavenly Dao’s resignation.'” Fairy Skylark responded: “This was an experience of my world.”

“The Ninth Heavenly Dao is a turning point. Is it related to this matter?” Big White Two inquired.

Several past Heavenly Daos or the rulers of the Netherworld who correspond to them had vaguely deduced that the ‘Ninth Heavenly Dao is a turning point.’ But precisely how this ‘turning point’ turns out remains unknown.

What is certain is that during the Ninth Heavenly Dao’s era, there will definitely be some significant changes that differ from those of past Heavenly Daos.

It could be a blessing, or a disaster.

“The Fourth Heavenly Dao has spent this entire lifetime meddling around, pointlessly.” Reincarnation Blade Fairy laughed.

If the Fourth Dark Heavenly Dao did nothing and simply waited for the opportunity, biding its time until the Ninth Heavenly Dao stepped down before making its move, wouldn’t that be a favorable situation?

Yet, such an almost certain win was turned into a losing game through its own needless complications.

Isn’t it good to just lay low? Why stir up trouble?

“If indeed the First Heavenly Dao is provoked and intends to end this world... can Song Shuhang and White Heavenly Dao keep it from happening?” Lady Kunna slowly said.

“With two current Heavenly Daos, 2 against 1, they should be confident. The Fourth Heavenly Dao could just be cleansed like this.” The three-eyed young senior pondered, “Moreover, there’s the main body of Reincarnation Blade Fairy, the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy, who could also lend a hand.”

As they spoke, the scene within the mirror began to change.

The trapped ‘figure’ suddenly prostrated, and from its body as the center, a pitch-black shadow began to emerge.

The shadow seemed to connect to another world.

In that world, a special existence familiar to Song Shuhang and others began to appear.

—Remains of a Wielder of the Will.

And not just a single one.

From the Second Wielder of the Will up to the Eighth, all the remains started to manifest, floating in and out of the shadows.

Each Heavenly Dao had hundreds, if not thousands, of varying sizes of ‘Heavenly Dao remains.’

These remains were supposed to dissolve after a new Wielder of the Will took the position.

But now, it seemed they had not dissipated and were instead collected into another special world.

A vast number of Heavenly Dao remains materialized and merged into the shadow.

The area of the shadow began to expand limitlessly.

Everything within this shadow began to decay and perish.

Even the ‘desert world’ created by Senior White was no exception.

“Unsheathe!” Song Shuhang commanded firmly.

Eight Heavenly Dao Roots emitted a clear ringing sound, and blades known as ‘Heavenly Dao Blades’ unsheathed from the pillars, their blade light bursting forth to cut down all things.

Simultaneously, another pillar representing ‘Lady Kunna’s Stardragon Pillar’ slammed down, also unsheathing and joining the eight below to complete a set of nine pillars!

On each ‘Heavenly Dao Pillar,’ there was both ‘Immortal Data’ and ‘Heavenly Dao Marks,’ shielding them even from the power of ultimate death and decay.

The blade light of the Heavenly Dao Blades could cut through anything.

The initially expanding shadow halted under the suppression of the blade light.

“Who would have thought that the ‘Overlord God Pillar’ we deduced together would have such power,” remarked a member of the External Assistance Research Group.

Indeed, the ‘demon god pillars’ secret technique of the Demon Emperor Hezhi holds infinite potential.

When pushed to the limit and combined with sufficiently powerful ‘raw materials,’ it can conjure up something as absurd as ‘Heavenly Dao Pillars!’

Unfortunately, true ‘eternity’ cannot be transmuted into ‘Overlord God Pillars.’

Otherwise, if real ‘Heavenly Dao Bodies’ could be used to form Overlord God Pillars, that would be the truly invincible pillar.

“The innate skill in saber techniques that Tyrannical Song possesses,” Senior Daozi added with his last bit of consciousness, “is also why he is able to bring the ‘Overlord God Pillar’ secret techniques to such a level.”

“Thank you, Brother Daozi, for the compliment,” Dark Song shyly said.

One had to admit, Song Shuhang’s talent in saber techniques was indeed formidable.

Eight Heavenly Dao Blades combined with the Dragon Network Saber emerged, where saber intent and blade light seemed to fuse into one, firmly suppressing the shadow.

From the looks of it, Tyrannical Song and White Heavenly Dao might even have a chance of capturing the figure suspected to be the First Heavenly Dao alive.

“Fairy of the Reincarnation Blade,” White Heavenly Dao inquired, “shall we cooperate with Shuhang to capture this individual and then figure out a way to study them?”

“White says, wait a moment,” Little White Two spoke up.

Even responding was something Senior White needed Little White Two’s help for... Does that mean Senior White was preoccupied at the moment?

But wasn’t the figure, possibly the First Heavenly Dao, being suppressed by Song Shuhang?

Fairy of the Reincarnation Blade gave it some thought and, using Sixteen as an intermediary, activated a second ‘camera’ and entered a dual-camera filming mode.

The second camera focused on Senior White’s position.

And then she saw Senior White, facing another direction in the ‘myriad practitioners in the universe,’ reaching out his hand!

Following the trace of power left by Senior White, the camera moved along... and Fairy of the Reincarnation Blade saw another ‘ethereal’ figure appearing at another location in the myriad practitioners in the universe.

This figure, too, was shrouded in a ‘domain-like’ shadow, with remains of an Ancient Heavenly Dao floating in and out of visibility within the shadow.

More than one such figure?

Or could it be that all these figures are ‘one’ but can act simultaneously from many locations in the myriad practitioners in the universe?

At that moment, as Senior White’s hand came down, a desert of sand bound the second figure.

But this desert was different from the previous one.

This time, each grain of sand was like a star... This desert was more like a galaxy!

And this galaxy exuded an ‘eternity’ flavor.

This was the true form of Senior White’s desert world.

The huge galaxy world completely trapped the second figure.

This second figure appeared more distressed than the first, with an even smaller range of movement.

However, the members of the External Assistance Research Group, who were watching the live stream, all frowned.

If there were two... there very likely could be three!

No one could guarantee that other locations within the myriad practitioners in the universe wouldn’t reveal a third figure.

While contemplating, a splendid light of virtue materialized behind White Heavenly Dao.

A ‘Heavenly Dao Body’ set foot.

It was the Sixth Heavenly Dao, Daoist Priest Virtue.

At this moment, Daoist Priest Virtue, his body’s ‘karmic flames’ all but extinguished, transformed back into a radiant light of virtue. His features, enveloped in the light of virtue, seemed illusory.

“Bright, too bright, change the camera!” Father Goudan exclaimed.

“Eye drops, eye drops,” the three-eyed young senior fumbled in his embrace.

Luckily, the appearance of Daoist Priest Virtue’s body was fleeting.

Taking a step from behind White Heavenly Dao, he stepped out of the Heavenly Principle Dimension and headed for a certain location within the myriad practitioners in the universe—clearly, a ‘third figure’ was manifesting there.

His Body of Eternity was required for suppression.

“Fairy of the Reincarnation Blade, can you communicate with your main body? If possible, it would be best to have the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy prepare... I have a bad feeling,” Senior White Two voiced out.

In this myriad practitioners in the universe, the third figure had already appeared... could the fourth, fifth, or even sixth figures emerge next?

At present, within the External Assistance Research Group, only the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy and Lady Kunna were capable of contributing in this high-level battle.

However, once Lady Kunna left the ‘Black Dragon World’ to enter the main world, her combat effectiveness would be greatly reduced; it was unknown how much of a role she could play.

“I understand; I’ve forwarded the message to my main body. But... unless absolutely necessary, my main body had best not move. Preferably, we should draw the enemy into the sphere of the ‘Reincarnation Seal,'” Fairy of the Reincarnation Blade replied.

Once the Reincarnation Seal moved, the newly established system of reincarnation would be severely affected.

It was best to lead the enemy into the range of the Reincarnation Seal so the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy could suppress them directly.

“The fourth figure has appeared,” Dark Song solemnly stated.

His words were, in effect, Song Shuhang speaking.

“Can we lure it to the edge of the Reincarnation Seal?” Fairy of the Reincarnation Blade spoke up.

“Wait... Tyrannical Song is trying to see if he can mobilize the Fourth Heavenly Dao’s husk to suppress it,” Dark Song responded.

“At this time, there’s no need to panic,” suddenly, Heavenly Emperor’s son came online.

Father Goudan: “Dada Egg, has your session with Cheng Goudan ended?”

Heavenly Emperor’s son: “...”

At this moment, the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber hanging on Song Shuhang vibrated slightly.

It affectionately rubbed against Song Shuhang’s face, then broke through the Heavenly Principle Dimension and headed towards a location in the myriad practitioners in the universe.

In that place, Fairy Cheng Lin and Heavenly Emperor’s son stood side by side.

The Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber landed between the two immortals.

Cheng Lin and Heavenly Emperor’s son, for the first time setting aside their prejudices, both reached out and grabbed the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber.

The Confucian Virtuous Golden Lotus, the Netherworld’s Sinful Black Lotus, and the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber all resonated.

Under the combined efforts of the two worlds, the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber, Heavenly Emperor’s son, and Cheng Lin, a pathway seemed to open.

Father Goudan: “!!!”

Because it realized that it had become the coordinate for this ‘pathway.’

And the only possibility for an existence that used the ruler of the Netherworld as a ‘Dao Mark’ was emerging.

A gigantic striped dragon, whose body was even more enormous than the stars, appeared from the channel.

With a missing leg, agile dragon mustaches, and a hopping, bouncing way of proceeding.

Another Father Goudan!

The moment the gigantic striped dragon appeared, it shrank in size and used its dragon mustaches to wrap around the ‘Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber,’ striking out with a paw at the fourth figure!

Heavenly Dao Return!

Heavenly Dao Father Goudan was truly the first, the returning Heavenly Dao.

Chapter 3149: Chapter 3147: You are Shuhang, You are a Free Squirrel
 

The moment the Wielder of the Will Striped Dragon returned, Father Goudan became irritable.

At some point in the past, Father Goudan’s temperament was the complete opposite of the Wielder of the Will Striped Dragon. Back then, it was cold, indifferent, taciturn, and lacked empathy, a very qualified ruler of the Netherworld.

Until that year, the Wielder of the Will Striped Dragon told Father Goudan that it was going to retire from the ‘Heavenly Dao seat.’

Father Goudan always thought that once the striped dragon left the Heavenly Dao seat, it, as the ruler of the Netherworld, would disappear, become ‘the past,’ and cease to exist completely.

But when it awoke, it found itself still alive, carefully preserved in a mysterious space in the main world—while the striped dragon had vanished without a trace.

At that moment, the previously cold Father Goudan was gone.

Later, gradually, Father Goudan began to take on the appearance of the striped dragon...

Perhaps deep inside, it always felt that the ‘Wielder of the Will Striped Dragon’ was already dead.

The legendary ‘return of the Heavenly Dao’ seemed to be so far out of reach.

But now.

The scene from its imagination, deemed ‘unattainable,’ suddenly appeared in front of it.

The Wielder of the Will Striped Dragon hopped around, appearing before Father Goudan with a cute bouncing posture.

Without giving anyone time to mentally prepare.

For some reason, Father Goudan suddenly couldn’t control its emotions and erupted in fury.

It wanted to burst out at the striped dragon, to vent all its pent-up emotions onto the other party!

Father Goudan manifested its real body, its dragon-clawed feet scraping against the ground, wishing it could immediately open a space gate and appear beside the striped dragon to kick it!

“Father Goudan, calm down! Control your emotions, don’t panic. Since your Heavenly Dao has already come back, there’s no rush to confront it later! For now, let it complete its mission of suppressing an ‘image.’ Afterward, you can do whatever you want to it. Right now, you have to consider the bigger picture!” the three-eyed young senior approached insincerely and did everything in his power to restrain the irate Father Goudan.

This act of standing on the ‘side of righteousness’ and forcefully restraining Father Goudan, while happily watching it continue to be irate, was incredibly satisfying for the three-eyed young senior.

The more furious Father Goudan became, unable to vent, the happier the three-eyed young senior felt.

Sometimes, the happiness of the ruler of the Netherworld was just so simple and childish.

The overly deliberate behavior of the three-eyed young ruler was so much that even Senior White Two nearby found it difficult to watch.

But the three-eyed young ruler’s actions were correct.

Even though his intentions were twisted, his actions were right.

Doing the work of justice with a heart of darkness.

...

In the vacuum, with one foot, the Wielder of the Will Striped Dragon stepped on the ‘Fourth Shadow,’ while it swung its dragon mustaches, wrapping around the ‘Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber,’ and delivered a powerful cut!

With its foot crushing its mighty enemy, it brazenly swung the saber.

The Wielder of the Will Striped Dragon made an imposing entrance unmatched by any!

And its saber strike was just as majestic.

Contained within that single strike were seemingly nine different kinds of intent, as if the striped dragon was experiencing nine different lives.

These intents layered upon each other seamlessly.

And within the final layer of intent, there was a hint of Song Shuhang’s breath, merged with the power of the striped dragon, transforming into an unparalleled slash.

The ‘Fourth Shadow’ underfoot was continuously sliced apart, losing any strength to counterattack, struggling to resist, firmly suppressed by the striped dragon beneath its mighty foot!

Having suppressed the main ‘Fourth Heavenly Dao Figure,’ the Wielder of the Will Striped Dragon looked towards Fairy Cheng Lin and Heavenly Emperor with a vivid demonstration of ‘evident joy and cheerfulness.’

Then, it raised its head, and toward the vacuum, opened its mouth, as if it was silently saying something.

“What is Heavenly Dao Father Goudan saying?” Daoist Senior uttered, barely sustaining his last bit of consciousness. The world now plunged into a massive crisis, and Daoist Senior, with this shred of consciousness, was not willing to close his eyes. He wanted to witness the world becoming ‘safe and sound’ before he could take his last breath!

“[It is saying that time is limited.]” Father Goudan’s dragon body was silently suppressed on the ground by the three-eyed young senior, unable to move: “[It relies on the power of the ‘Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber,’ using me as a marking, temporarily returning. Before it can solve the restriction after ‘breaking free,’ the time it can stay in the main world is limited, and it needs to continuously pay a price.]”

This resembles the ‘Dark Heaven.’

The Dark Heaven usually stirs trouble in the main world by using a part of its ‘Immortal Shell + its own ruler of the Netherworld’ transformed into the Avatar of the Dark Sun.

The true ‘Dark Fourth Heavenly Dao’s main body, every time it descends to the main world, is limited by time. After a while, it must return, falling into an endless slumber. To exercise the authority of the Heavenly Dao, it must burn the ‘consciousness’ within its immortal shell as a price.

The ‘price’ paid by the Wielder of the Will Striped Dragon is the saber intent armor on the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber.

The Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber, which had finally transformed into ‘Eighth Revolution,’ now has its seal saber intent armor gradually degrading.

“[That is to say, the Heavenly Dao Father Goudan hastens Shuhang... or White Heavenly Dao, hoping they quickly come up with a countermeasure.]” Lady Kunna guessed.

The words of the Wielder of the Will Striped Dragon were certainly meant for Song Shuhang or the white-robed figure.

Reincarnation Blade Fairy frowned, “[Can Shuhang and Fellow Daoist White come up with a plan?]”

One after another, materialized ‘phantoms,’ each one needing an ‘Immortal Level’ existence to suppress.

Shuhang and White Heavenly Dao, who had just proved their Dao immortality, could they come up with a solution?

“[If we really talk about a plan... there is only one.]” Senior White Two spoke softly.

“[What I’m more worried about is that there might be more than four ‘phantoms.]” Daozi, with his last bit of consciousness, said bitterly.

In fact, just as he feared,

In another part of the myriad practitioners in the universe, the fifth ‘phantom’ still manifested.

Even as everyone was unwelcome to its arrival, even as everyone rejected its emergence, it still had the audacity, amid communal loathing, to make its entrance.

Then, Dark Song spoke up, “[Reincarnation Blade Fairy, please relay this to Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy, to get ready for suppression.]”

“[My main body is already prepared,]” replied Reincarnation Blade Fairy.

Dark Song quickly added, “[Lady Kunna, please lend me your power.]”

“[Call me Lady Fat Ball, what do you need me for?]” Lady Kunna responded.

“[Please assist me in controlling the Fourth Heavenly Dao’s body—Cultivation Chat Immortal Path 999%, activate!]” Dark Song stepped out from the Netherworld Realm, taking over Tyrannical Song’s ‘Cultivator Chat System’ power, and in one breath, pushed it to its current limit.

The ruler of the Netherworld, in its lifetime, has one chance to enter the main world, one chance to exercise the authority of the Heavenly Dao.

Without hesitation, Dark Song used these two chances all at once.

In the vacuum, the pure body of the Fourth Heavenly Dao descended from the ‘Heavenly Principle Dimension,’ materializing in front of Dark Song.

Dark Song slapped the pure body of the ‘Fourth Heavenly Dao,’ using the ‘Cultivator Chat System’ to activate a newly completed feature—remote desktop control.

The Fourth Heavenly Dao had once sneakily registered an account in ‘Cultivator Chat System’—although it quickly deleted its account, the ‘root’ of it remained within Song Shuhang’s ‘Cultivator Chat System.’

Now, Dark Song reactivated the Fourth Heavenly Dao’s account and connected it with Lady Kunna, allowing her to remotely control the Fourth Heavenly Dao’s pure shell by using the ‘remote desktop control’ feature!

This function was developed by Song Shuhang while he was figuring out how to control the ‘Fourth Heavenly Dao Shell,’ borrowing the idea from a modern chatting software.

Unexpectedly, it could be put to use at this time.

Lady Kunna, who was equally familiar with the ‘Cultivation Chat System,’ quickly got the hang of it and took control of the ‘Fourth Heavenly Dao’s’ shell.

“[Should I suppress this fifth ‘phantom?’]” Lady Kunna replied.

“No, Lady Fat Ball... first, we join hands to transfer it to where the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy is! You have other targets to deal with.]” Dark Song started to exert Heavenly Dao authority, forcibly performed a space switch.

“[Understood.]” Lady Kunna nodded her head.

The sky full of Heavenly Dao debris picked up, wrapping around the ‘fifth phantom,’ working in tandem with Dark Song’s space switching ability.

Heaven and earth change.

The ‘fifth phantom’ was transferred by Dark Song and Lady Kunna next to the Reincarnation Seal of the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy.

“`

The fifth against the fifth.

The Fairy of the Fifth Heavenly Dao had long been prepared, and as soon as the Figure of the 5th appeared, it was pressed down by the Great Seal, the power of reincarnation wildly sweeping down and pulling it into the infinite cycle of reincarnation.

Lady Kunna took timely control of the ‘Body of the Fourth Heavenly Dao’, detaching it from the ‘Figure of the 5th’.

“Who is my target?” Lady Kunna asked.

“Go!” Dark Song pushed with his hand, and the Body of the Fourth Heavenly Dao shifted.

There, the Figure of the 6th was subtly bubbling up—unlike the previous five figures, the Figure of the 6th was moving stealthily.

But just as its head emerged, the Body of the Fourth Heavenly Dao remotely controlled by Lady Kunna already descended like a sky-covering blanket.

Each grain of sand fell like a star.

Moreover, the more they attacked, the more stars there would be. Slice one star, and it split into two stars.

The Figure of the 6th was suppressed.

At this point, Song Shuhang had exhausted all his methods.

Yet those ‘figures’ seemed as if they hadn’t reached their end.

The 7th figure was also beginning to show signs of taking form...

“Three-Eyed, can you summon your own Heavenly Dao back?” Father Goudan asked.

“How would I know? I don’t get along with it; I’m just a tortured experimental subject. Besides, even if that guy shows up, no one can guarantee which side it will take. It might very well stand against us.” The three-eyed young senior spoke gravely.

“Lord White, what about your Heavenly Dao?” the last consciousness of Daozi asked.

Senior White Two gently shook his head: “He might not be able to return, and perhaps, might not be able to appear again.”

Not every Heavenly Dao can come back.

For instance...

Fat Ball.

The Heavenly Dao of the Fat Ball, the Eighth Heavenly Dao, is impossible to reappear.

Within the Heavenly Principle Dimension.

“Senior White, we can’t keep dragging this out. Heavenly Dao Father Goudan’s return has a time limit... Lady Kunna is remotely controlling the Body of the Fourth Heavenly Dao, which is fine for a short time, but over a longer period, flaws are likely to emerge... The Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy is also in charge of the ‘Reincarnation System’, she can’t keep suppressing the other side indefinitely,” Song Shuhang said.

At this moment, he had made up his mind.

Although he really wanted to wait a bit longer to perfect the ‘Immortal Replacement’ plan and then transcend with Senior White as two separate individuals to avoid leaving any problems behind, it seemed like time waited for no one.

No matter how fast Tyrannical Song ‘advanced,’ time always pressed him to keep moving forward, leaving him no time to stop and rest.

Therefore, Song Shuhang was prepared to let Senior White transcend first and become a graduate of the Heavenly Dao.

Now, it seemed that only by transcending, surpassing the Heavenly Dao, surpassing time, surpassing space, and surpassing the Heavenly Dao Authority, could the current dilemma be resolved.

“Yes, we indeed cannot keep dragging this out,” Senior White said softly.

So...

You are free, Shuhang.

Senior White didn’t say this out loud.

He merely whispered it in his heart.

He might have an obsession with ‘detaching from the Heavenly Dao and graduating from it,’

But he didn’t have that much determination for what he wanted to do after detaching.

Whether it’s the ‘past’ leftover obsessions or the ‘distant future’ hopes, they were all entangled with Song Shuhang.

Isn’t it natural for matters belonging to Song Shuhang to be handled by himself?

Moreover, him staying behind is more important than Song Shuhang staying.

At least he can suppress the luck of the myriad practitioners in the universe.

With Senior White’s will and decision.

The time in the Heavenly Principle Dimension seemed to pause.

Two Heavenly Dao wills were activated, manifesting from Song Shuhang and Senior White.

These were not the wisps of Heavenly Dao will that Song Shuhang had previously differentiated into the main world, but a complete, unbroken, immortal will of the Heavenly Dao’s main body.

The two Heavenly Dao wills were activated, projecting from the Heavenly Principle Dimension all the way to the myriad realms, where their phantoms were vaguely observed by cultivators across all worlds!

This signified that the Heavenly Dao was about to do something big.

An event significant enough to shake the myriad realms would have such a projection.

“Have you finally decided?” Senior White Two whispered.

This was the best choice to resolve the current predicament.

Within the Myriad Realm Void.

The ‘Heavenly Dao’s Will Projection’ belonging to Song Shuhang gradually became more distinct. Vaguely, one could see some principles and rules entwined on his body.

These rules and principles represented not only power but also Bind.

To have power is to have obligations and responsibilities!

“Senior White?” Song Shuhang’s Heavenly Dao will was still somewhat bewildered.

Opposite him, the Heavenly Dao will of Senior White gently bent over, reaching for the ‘rules and principles’ on Song Shuhang’s body, tugging violently.

The constraints of these rules were pulled to the limit in Senior White’s hands, making a sound on the verge of snapping.

But just then...

Two ‘figures’ materialized in the vacuum simultaneously.

The 7th and the 8th figures.

These two figures appeared in the vacuum, launching their attacks across space at that ‘projection.’

Their attacks seemed to penetrate the ‘projection,’ directly targeting the real bodies of Song Shuhang and Senior White.

“Be careful!” the last consciousness of Daoist Senior called out unwillingly.

He wished he could still summon his own ‘Heavenly Dao Body’ to block the two attacks.

But he was the 8.5th Dao, different from a true Heavenly Dao; he didn’t have a ‘Heavenly Dao Return’ feature!

At that moment...

A pair of bewildered eyeballs appeared in front of the 7th and 8th figures.

Boom boom~

The attacks of the two figures directly blasted the body of the bewildered eyeballs.

“Ah~ I’m dead~” the puzzled eyeballs let out a drawn-out cry.

The three-eyed young senior couldn’t help but post a huge question mark in the group chat: “?”

“Is that not your butler?” Father Goudan asked.

The suddenly appearing puzzled eyeballs were indeed the old butler of the three-eyed young senior, the one that always wanted to switch employers!

Chapter 3150: Chapter 3148: The Final Boost, Detached!
 

Butler, butler, why are you here?

The three-eyed young senior pinned down Father Goudan but had an ominous premonition in his heart.

The eyeball butler appeared too abruptly.

The members of the External Assistance Research Group present were either top-tier Immortals or rulers of the Netherworld.

Yet, no one saw how the eyeball butler appeared in front of Song Shuhang and the White Heavenly Dao.

It was as if it had been guarding in front of Song Shuhang and White all along, waiting for the attack to come.

“Is it okay to be blown up?” Father Goudan asked.

—However, thanks to the eyeball butler taking the hit, the ceremony for Song Shuhang and the White Heavenly Dao had entered its final stage.

“It’s fine; it’s just a matter of being blown up,” the three-eyed young senior said softly.

But there was an indescribable complexity in his tone.

Normally, it wasn’t his first or second time blowing up the eyeball butler. The death history of the eyeball butler in the past year might not be less formidable than Song Shuhang’s.

But this time was somewhat different.

In the scene.

After blowing up the eyeball butler, the 7th and 8th figures continued to step forward, intending to strike against Song Shuhang and White again...

“Hey~ Where are you looking?” A magnetic young voice rang in the ears of the 7th and 8th figures.

Behind them, the flesh and blood of the previously blown-up eyeball butler formed an eyeball pattern formation.

In the center of the formation, a black-haired young man with delicate features appeared from the pattern.

Dressed in a blue robe adorned with eyeball patterns, he wore an unflustered smile, stepped out of the formation, reached out with both hands, and deftly hooked his arms around the necks of the 7th and 8th figures, resting on their shoulders.

“While suppressing you both in one breath is slightly strenuous, fortunately, the transformation of the Ninth Heavenly Dao has already ended,” the black-haired young man said, using a chokehold to pull the 7th and 8th figures toward himself and dragged them into the ‘formation.’

The three-eyed young senior’s eyes widened: “!!!”

If there’s a possibility for something to go wrong, no matter how small that possibility is, it will always happen.

The person he least wanted to see had ultimately shown up.

That utterly detestable smile; those brazen, flirtatious actions of wrapping his arm around a stranger’s shoulder—this was his corresponding Heavenly Dao, the main body of the Second Heavenly Dao.

“Father Goudan, knock me out,” the three-eyed young senior said gravely.

If he wasn’t knocked out, he feared he wouldn’t be able to resist stepping forward to furiously rebuke his own main body.

“Leave it to me!” Father Goudan’s face revealed a delighted smile—what goes around comes around, what should come will eventually arrive.

Knocking out a ruler of the Netherworld was exceptionally difficult.

But knocking out the three-eyed young senior was, even if grueling, a task he would perform without charging a single fee.

...

Meanwhile.

As Senior White, the Wielder of the Will, reached out and tugged, all the ‘rules and responsibilities’ bound to Song Shuhang were unravelled.

The ‘Heavenly Dao responsibilities and rules’ that were released did not rebind themselves to Song Shuhang but instead coiled around Senior White’s arms.

At this point, Senior White alone was bearing the constraints of two Heavenly Daos.

“Senior White?” Song Shuhang asked in confusion. “Wasn’t it agreed that you would transcend first?”

Senior White was obsessed with ‘graduating from the Heavenly Dao.’

Thus, he had already clearly conveyed that he wanted Senior White to transcend and graduate first.

“Um...well, there are still many new experiences with the Heavenly Dao Authority that I find interesting. I feel like I could probably play around for another month or so?” Senior White said with a smile.

Indeed, this was also one of the reasons why Senior White wanted to remain in the ‘Heavenly Dao seat,’ but it probably accounted for only about one-tenth of the reason.

“Don’t worry about me. The constraints of the Heavenly Dao Authority cannot bind me. If I want to detach...it can be done very quickly. So for now, go and resolve every issue. The past, present, and future—once everything is settled, come back,” Senior White added.

“But Senior White...I don’t know how to take the final step to detachment,” Song Shuhang said anxiously.

Among the historical Heavenly Daos, only the Seventh Heavenly Dao White had once been ‘near-transcendent.’

Senior White was a unique being, perhaps knowing how to take the final step toward “detachment.”

But Song Shuhang was truly a novice in the ways of the Heavenly Dao.

Even though the “laws of the Heavenly Dao, Bind” that restricted him had been lifted, he still didn’t know what to do next.

“Don’t worry, someone will tell you what to do.” Senior White reached out and gently pushed Song Shuhang.

Song Shuhang’s figure detached from the “Heavenly Principle Dimension” and was pushed into the main world.

There, a handsome white horse, trotting on its hooves, proudly passed in front of him.

Song Shuhang hurriedly called out, “Fellow Daoist Ma.”

The white horse paused slightly, turned its head to look at Song Shuhang, and signaled him to follow.

Song Shuhang’s figure moved, closely following behind the white horse.

Man and horse began running through the vacuum.

Faintly, one could see that with every step the white horse took, it left a mark in the vacuum.

Stepping on these hoofprints, with each step Song Shuhang took, he felt as if his body were about to “float up,” as if to completely detach from this world.

Not knowing how long they had run...

As he ran, Song Shuhang gradually entered a state of near-transcendence, much like the “white-robed figure” had once experienced.

The white horse was not Wielder of the Will White, but a final gift and guide left by the white-robed figure for “White.”

But this final gift was now passed on by Senior White to Song Shuhang.

Bang~

The final step, the black horse landed on all fours on the ground, forcefully leapt in the vacuum, leaving behind four hoofprints.

Song Shuhang closely followed the horse’s tracks, leaping forth with all his might.

But this “last leap” seemed to lack some strength.

He always felt something was missing.

“What’s missing?” said Song Shuhang in a soft voice.

As he pondered, a ninth figure started showing their divinity below him.

A total of nine figures, each vaguely corresponding to the successive reigns of the Heavenly Dao.

But this time, there was no one left to assist Song Shuhang or suppress this ninth figure.

The Seventh Heavenly Dao, white-robed figure, left only the black horse to lead the way.

As for the Eighth Heavenly Dao, the fat ball, there was no possibility of “return.”

Now, the only one who could block this ninth figure was the “Senior White Two” born corresponding to Netherworld Realm’s ruler.

In the instant Song Shuhang’s thought flickered, that ninth figure below slowly stretched out a hand, supporting his feet, and forcefully lifted him upward.

This push gave Song Shuhang the last bit of assistance he needed.

Like a fish leaping through a dragon gate, Song Shuhang soared high, catching up with the white horse’s trail.

?

Song Shuhang looked down at the ninth figure with some confusion.

Why would it offer him the final push?

Below him, the ninth figure showed a kind smile toward Song Shuhang.

He looked somewhat familiar.

But at this moment, Song Shuhang had no time to think any further.

His form broke through the last Bind.

Finally, he entered a state of complete “detachment.”

And unlike the original “Wielder of the Will White,” he was no longer bound by the Heavenly Dao Authority!

The sea is wide for fish to leap across, and the sky is high for birds to soar!

At this moment, Tyrannical Song became the most free squirrel in the world!
